# astro-ph.IM [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Semianalytic Sensitivity Estimates for Out-of-Bank Gravitational-Wave Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14045)
*Aditya Vijaykumar,Reed Essick*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出一种快速半解析近似方法，利用拟合因子（fitting factor）估计引力波搜索对模板库中未显式建模的物理效应的灵敏度，并通过旋转双中子星、轨道偏心率及广义相对论偏离等案例验证其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确估计引力波搜索的灵敏度对天体物理学和基础物理学研究至关重要，但传统方法对模板库中未显式建模的效应（如广义相对论偏离、环境效应等）难以高效评估灵敏度。

Method: 发展了一种快速半解析近似（fast semianalytic approximation），利用拟合因子（fitting factor）——即候选信号与搜索模板库的最大重叠（maximum overlap）——来估计匹配滤波搜索（matched-filter search）的灵敏度。

Result: 通过与旋转双中子星（spinning binary neutron stars）实际搜索性能的对比验证了该方法的准确性，并成功评估了包含轨道偏心率（orbital eccentricity）或广义相对论（general relativity）偏离的致密双星系统的搜索灵敏度。

Conclusion: 该工作为快速评估模板库中未建模效应（如广义相对论偏离、环境效应、引力透镜效应及波形/校准系统学）的搜索灵敏度铺平了道路，适用于多种天体物理学和基础物理学应用场景。

Abstract: Estimating the sensitivity of gravitational-wave searches is important for a wide variety of scientific applications spanning astrophysics and fundamental physics. In this work, we develop a fast semianalytic approximation for estimating matched-filter search sensitivity to physical effects not explicitly modeled in the template bank. This approximation utilizes fitting factors, i.e., the maximum overlap of a candidate signal over the search bank. As illustrations, we compare our estimates to the actual performance of searches against spinning binary neutron stars, and evaluate search sensitivity to compact binaries possessing orbital eccentricity or deviations from general relativity. Our work thus paves the way for fast sensitivity estimates for a variety of applications, including unmodeled effects in template banks such as deviations from general relativity, environmental effects, gravitational lensing, and waveform/calibration systematics.

</details>


<div id='astro-ph.GA'></div>

# astro-ph.GA [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [On the survival of dark matter spikes: Stellar and compact-object perturbations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13761)
*Theophanes K. Karydas,Francesca Scarcella,Bradley J. Kavanagh,Gianfranco Bertone*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文通过银河系中心观测约束的案例研究，分析了暗物质（dark matter）密度尖峰在核星团和恒星质量黑洞引力扰动下的演化，发现暗物质分布在引力波（gravitational wave）产生区域外受恒星散射明显消耗，但在核心区域内仍保持约82%的初始过密度，表明暗物质致密结构在恒星扰动和黑洞并合历史中基本完整。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立超大质量黑洞（supermassive black hole）附近暗物质分布的现实预期，对于评估引力波信号中的环境印记至关重要。

Method: 以银河系中心为观测约束案例，分别研究核星团恒星散射、已知最近恒星扰动体（S2和S38）以及历史上极端质量比旋进（extreme mass ratio inspiral, EMRI）事件对暗物质密度尖峰的引力扰动影响。

Result: 核星团散射在$r \sim 10^{-1}~\mathrm{pc}$处显著消耗暗物质分布；S2和S38在$r \sim 10^{-3}~\mathrm{pc}$处仅引起可忽略的密度变化；历史EMRI事件在$r \lesssim 10^{-5}~\mathrm{pc}$处仅将密度降至初始值的约82%。

Conclusion: 至少在银河系中心，中心黑洞周围的暗物质过密度在恒星扰动和合理的恒星质量黑洞并合历史下预计将基本保持完整。

Abstract: Establishing realistic expectations for the dark matter (DM) distribution near a supermassive black hole (BH) is essential for assessing environmental imprints on gravitational wave (GW) signals. Using the Galactic Center as an observationally constrained case study, we investigate the evolution of DM density spikes under gravitational perturbations from the nuclear stellar and black hole populations surrounding the central BH. We find that scattering of DM particles by the nuclear star cluster depletes the DM distribution at radii $r \sim 10^{-1}~\mathrm{pc}$, far outside the region where the relevant GW signals are produced. At smaller radii, at $r \sim 10^{-3}~\mathrm{pc}$, the closest known stellar perturbers, S2 and S38, induce only negligible changes to the density profile. At still smaller radii, where no stellar perturbers are currently known, we assess the cumulative impact of past EMRIs by modelling successive mergers with stellar-mass BHs of mass $\sim10~\mathrm{M}_\odot$, in numbers consistent with the expected rate over $10~\mathrm{Gyr}$. We find that these events do not erase the central overdensity, reducing the density only to approximately $82 \%$ of its initial value at $r \lesssim 10^{-5}~\mathrm{pc}$. Our results indicate that, at least at the Galactic Center, DM overdensities around the central BH are expected to remain largely intact under stellar perturbations and plausible stellar-BH merger histories.

</details>

# math.NA [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [Mathematical Modeling of Salt Precipitation and Multi-Phase Flow in High Enthalpy Fractured Geothermal Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14328)
*Micheal B. Oguntola,Omar Duran,Eirik Keilegavlen,Inga Berre*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于持久主变量（压力、焓、总盐质量分数）的新型组分流模型，用于模拟高焓裂隙地热储层中非等温、多相、多组分流动与盐类结垢的耦合过程。模型采用离散裂隙-基质方法，结合相关驱动的相行为线性化策略和Kozeny-Carman动态孔隙度-渗透率模型，在开源框架PorePy中实现。通过一维盐溶解基准验证和二维裂隙储层应用，展示了模型在预测石盐沉淀模式、渗透率损伤及能量采收方面的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高焓裂隙地热储层涉及非等温（non-isothermal）、多相（multiphase）、多组分（multicomponent）流动与强非线性热力学（thermodynamics）的复杂耦合过程，而矿物结垢（mineral scaling）如石盐（halite）沉淀会进一步损害储层渗透率和井产能，现有模拟工具难以处理此类耦合问题。因此，亟需一个开源、数值稳定的模拟工具来准确预测此类系统中的热-质输运与结垢行为。

Method: 采用基于持久主变量（persistent set of primary variables）——压力（pressure）、焓（enthalpy）和总盐质量分数（overall salt mass fraction）——的组分流模型，自然处理相变（phase transitions）而无需手动切换。模型集成离散裂隙-基质方法（discrete fracture-matrix approach），利用相关驱动的相行为线性化（correlation-based phase-behaviour linearisation）替代昂贵的实时相分离计算，并通过Kozeny-Carman关系动态模拟因石盐沉淀导致的孔隙度（porosity）和渗透率（permeability）降低。模型在开源框架PorePy中实现。

Result: 在一维盐溶解基准测试中，模型与已有关闭源模拟器CSMP++的结果高度一致，覆盖了单相区与多相区之间的转变。在二维石盐饱和裂隙储层的注采应用中，模型成功预测了石盐沉淀模式及其对渗透率损伤和能量采收的影响。数值结果进一步展示了模型在预测井筒堵塞（wellbore blockage）和裂隙连通性（fracture connectivity）作用方面的价值。

Conclusion: 该模型为分析高焓裂隙地热系统中伴有矿物结垢的复杂热-质输运问题提供了一个开源数值工具，能够有效预测石盐沉淀对储层性能及操作挑战的影响。

Abstract: Simulating high-enthalpy fractured geothermal reservoirs is challenging due to the complex coupled processes of non-isothermal, multiphase, multicomponent flow, strongly nonlinear thermodynamics, and the dominant role of fractures. These complexities are amplified by mineral scaling, such as halite precipitation, which can impair reservoir permeability and well productivity. To address this, we present a new compositional flow model based on a persistent set of primary variables (pressure, enthalpy, and overall salt mass fraction). The formulation naturally handles phase transitions without manual switching, enhancing numerical stability. The model integrates a discrete fracture-matrix approach and employs an efficient, robust correlation-based phase-behaviour linearisation of saltwater thermodynamics, replacing expensive on-the-fly phase separation calculations. It incorporates the Kozeny-Carman relation to dynamically model porosity and permeability reduction from halite precipitation. Implemented in the open-source PorePy framework, the model is verified through a 1D salt dissolution benchmark against the established closed-source simulator CSMP++, showing strong agreement across geothermal conditions involving transitions between single- and multi-phase regions. Application to a 2D halite-saturated fractured reservoir with injection and production demonstrates the model's capability to predict halite precipitation patterns and their impact on permeability damage and energy recovery. Numerical results further show the model's value in predicting operational challenges such as wellbore blockage and the role of fracture connectivity. The model thus provides an open-source numerical tool for analysing complex heat and mass transport with mineral scaling in high-enthalpy fractured geothermal systems.

</details>

# physics.ins-det [[Back]](#toc)

### [4] [Seeding and Matching algorithms for the first GPU-based High Level Trigger of the LHCb experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14480)
*Christina Agapopoulou,Lukas Calefice,Álvaro Fernández Casani,Vava Gligorov,Arthur Marius Hennequin,Louis Henry,Valerii Kholoimov,Brij Kishor Jashal,Arantza Oyanguren,Lorenzo Pica,Volodymyr Svintozelskyi,Da Yu Tou,Jiahui Zhuo*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文描述了LHCb实验第一级触发器中Seeding和Matching算法的GPU实现，这两种算法用于在40 MHz速率下重建长程且高度偏离的径迹，并在Run 3数据采集期间以高吞吐量运行，提升了实验的物理潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了在LHCb实验的第一级触发器（first level trigger）中，于40 MHz的高事件率下高效重建长程且高度偏离的带电粒子径迹（long and very displaced tracks），从而提升实验的物理发现能力。

Method: Seeding算法是一种独立的模式识别（pattern recognition）算法，用于在最前向径迹探测器（most forward tracker）中寻找带电粒子轨迹；随后Matching算法将这些轨迹向后外推（extrapolated backward），与第一径迹探测器中的击中点（hits）形成的短径迹（stubs）结合，构成Long径迹；之后搜索第二径迹探测器中的击中点以优化轨迹并改善动量分辨率。这种向后外推的方法与从第一探测器经磁场向前外推至前向径迹探测器的传统方法互补，提升了低横动量（transverse momenta）下的Long径迹效率。

Result: 该算法已在LHCb Run 3的完整数据采集期间运行，实现了极高的吞吐量（high throughput），并提高了关键物理衰变道的探测潜力。

Conclusion: Seeding和Matching算法的GPU实现成功应用于LHCb第一级触发系统，凭借高吞吐量和低横动量下更高的Long径迹效率，增强了实验的物理覆盖能力。

Abstract: We describe the GPU implementation of the Seeding and Matching algorithms, developed for the first level trigger of the LHCb experiment and key to reconstruct long and very displaced tracks at 40 MHz. The algorithms have been participating in the data taking during the full Run 3 of LHCb with a very high throughput, increasing the physics reach of the experiment.
  The Seeding is a standalone pattern recognition algorithm aiming at finding charged particle trajectories in the most forward tracker of LHCb. These trajectories are then extrapolated backward by the Matching algorithm which combines them with stubs formed from hits in the first tracker in order to form what we call Long tracks. Hits in the second tracker are then searched for to better define the trajectory and improve the track momentum resolution. This backward approach, complementary to the approach of extrapolating the stubs in the first detector to the forward tracker through the magnetic field, improves the Long track efficiency at low transverse momenta, increasing the potential of key physics decay channels.

</details>

# math.CA [[Back]](#toc)

### [5] [A remark on Chebyshev rational functions, multipoint Padé approximants and Noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13965)
*Maxim Derevyagin,Max Meynig*

Main category: math.CA

TL;DR: 本文受物理学界对多点Padé近似（multipoint Padé approximants）兴趣的启发，讨论了切比雪夫有理函数（Chebyshev rational functions），展示了它们如何以与切比雪夫多项式生成Padé近似相同的方式生成多点Padé近似。文中给出了切比雪夫有理函数的递推关系及底层的Thiele型（亦称R_{II}型）连分数，并提供了数值证据，表明噪声对该插值格式的影响以及Costin、Dunne和Meynig近期在Padé近似中观察到的现象在多点的情形下同样出现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物理学界近期对多点Padé近似产生了兴趣，但尚缺乏一套系统且高效的生成工具。本文旨在将切比雪夫多项式的经典构造思路推广到有理函数情形，从而为多点Padé近似提供统一的理论基础与递推算法。

Method: 从切比雪夫有理函数出发，通过类比切比雪夫多项式构造Padé近似的方式，建立其与多点Padé近似的对应关系；推导切比雪夫有理函数满足的递推关系（recurrence relations）及对应的Thiele型连分数（continued fraction of Thiele type）。

Result: 给出了切比雪夫有理函数的完整递推结构，并明确了该结构与R_{II}型连分数的内在联系。数值实验显示，该插值方案对噪声敏感，且多点Padé近似中再现了Costin、Dunne和Meynig在经典Padé近似中发现的类似现象。

Conclusion: 切比雪夫有理函数为多点Padé近似提供了一种与经典切比雪夫多项式-标准Padé近似平行且简洁的理论框架；噪声作用下该方案的数值行为表明，相关现象具有跨格式的普适性。

Abstract: Motivated by the recent interest in multipoint Padé approximants in the physics community, we discuss Chebyshev rational functions and show how they give rise to multipoint Padé approximants in exactly the same way that Chebyshev polynomials produce Padé approximants. We present recurrence relations for Chebyshev rational functions, as well as the underlying continued fraction of Thiele type (also known as $R_{II}$ type). Finally, we provide numerical evidence illustrating the effects of noise on this interpolation scheme and show that a phenomenon similar to that recently observed by Costin, Dunne, and Meynig for Padé approximants also occurs in the multipoint setting.

</details>

# hep-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [6] [Conformal calibration and look-elsewhere effect in anomaly detection for new-physics searches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13780)
*Jack Y. Araz,Michael Spannowsky*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于共形预测（conformal prediction）的校准层，可将任意机器学习异常检测分数转换为具有分布无关（distribution-free）和有限样本（finite-sample）保证的可辩护显著性，同时暴露并修正标准流程无法察觉的误校准问题，并在LHC Olympics数据上验证了其消除虚假信号的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于机器学习的异常检测在高能物理新物理搜寻中用途广泛，但其原始异常分数缺乏校准含义；扫描多个区域会放大look-elsewhere效应，且依赖渐近显著性（asymptotic significance）的方法无法处理异常检测器极易导致的背景误建模（background mismodelling）问题。

Method: 通过共形预测将异常分数转化为有效的局部p值（local p-value），并采用加权（weighted）和Mondrian变体修复共振搜寻中边带与信号区域的可交换性失效（exchangeability failure）；结合Gross-Vitells步骤得到考虑look-elsewhere效应的全局显著性（global significance）。

Result: 在LHC Olympics数据上，分类器产生的亚结构-质量关联导致边带校准的背景p值反保守（anti-conservative），仅由背景塑造造成～46σ的虚假信号，标签无关的加权修正恢复了真实的零假设；标准渐近方法和未加权方法在无信号窗口制造≥10σ和≈5σ的虚假信号，而共形校准层未产生误报。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个可审计、与检测器无关的路径，将未校准的分数转化为考虑多重试验因子（trials factor）的显著性，可直接应用于实验异常搜寻。

Abstract: Machine-learned anomaly detection is reshaping searches for new physics, but it has outrun the statistics used to interpret it. A raw anomaly score has no calibrated meaning, a model that scans many regions inflates the look-elsewhere effect, and the asymptotic significances the field relies on are blind to the background mismodelling that anomaly detectors are especially prone to. We propose a calibration layer, built on conformal prediction, that turns any anomaly score into a defensible significance with distribution-free, finite-sample guarantees. Conformal prediction converts scores into valid local p-values, weighted and Mondrian variants repair the sideband-to-signal-region exchangeability failures that resonant searches suffer, and a Gross-Vitells step carries the result through to a look-elsewhere-aware global significance. The layer does two things at once. It exposes miscalibration that the standard pipeline cannot see, and it corrects it without retraining the detector. On public LHC Olympics data, a classifier develops a substructure-mass correlation that makes sideband-calibrated background p-values anti-conservative. Taken at face value, this manufactures a $\sim 46σ$ excess from background sculpting alone, which the label-free weighted correction removes, restoring an honest null. When run as a blind wide-mass bump hunt, the standard asymptotic and unweighted procedures fabricate $\gtrsim10σ$ excesses and $\approx5σ$ excesses even in signal-free windows, while the conformal layer raises no false alarms and its global false-positive rate is verified on background-only pseudoexperiments. The result is an auditable, detector-agnostic path from an uncalibrated score to a trials-factor-aware significance, ready to be folded into experimental anomaly searches.

</details>


### [7] [Thermal dileptons to probe the baryon-rich QCD matter in the forward region of LHC energy heavy-ion collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14166)
*Motomi Oya,Nicholas J. Benoit,Chiho Nonaka,Azumi Sakai,Yorito Yamaguchi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用(3+1)维相对论流体动力学（relativistic hydrodynamics）框架，研究了在LHC能量下中心Pb-Pb碰撞中具有有限重子化学势（baryon chemical potential, μ_B）的夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma, QGP）的热双轻子（thermal dilepton）产生。研究发现前向快度区μ_B可超过500 MeV，并导致双轻子产额出现3-4%的压低；但双轻子有效温度仍与早期高温阶段强相关，表明前向快度双轻子仍是有效的QGP温度计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有的研究表明，即使在LHC能量下，前向快度（forward rapidity）区域也可能实现可观的重子密度。有必要在包含有限重子化学势的流体动力学框架中系统研究热双轻子产生，以评估重子密度对QGP探针的影响。

Method: 将有限重子化学势μ_B纳入(3+1)维相对论流体动力学模型，模拟中心Pb-Pb碰撞（√s_{NN}=5.02 TeV）中夸克-胶子等离子体的时空演化；在此基础上计算大快度范围内的热双轻子谱，并与无重子密度情形进行比较。

Result: 在介质演化过程中，前向快度区域（伪快度η_s ≈ 6）的μ_B可超过500 MeV；在前向快度区域5.2 < y < 7.2内，由于有限重子密度降低了夸克-反夸克数量，热双轻子产额出现3-4%的压低；在中间质量区域（1.2 < M_{ℓℓ} < 2.6 GeV），从双轻子质量谱提取的有效温度仍与底层流体动力学温度强相关，对QGP早期高温阶段保持敏感。

Conclusion: 前向快度区域的热双轻子在LHC能量下仍可作为有效的QGP温度计，同时具备对有限重子密度的灵敏性。

Abstract: We investigate thermal dilepton production from a quark-gluon plasma (QGP) with finite baryon chemical potential ($μ_{\text{B}}$) in central Pb-Pb collisions at $\sqrt{s_{\text{NN}}}=5.02~\text{TeV}$. Recent studies suggest that sizable baryon densities can be achieved at forward rapidity even at LHC energies. We incorporate finite $μ_{\text{B}}$ into a (3+1)-dimensional hydrodynamic framework and find that $μ_{\text{B}}$ exceeds 500 MeV around $η_\text{s} = 6$ during the medium evolution. Using this framework, we calculate thermal dilepton spectra over a wide rapidity range and evaluate the impact of finite $μ_{\text{B}}$ on dilepton production. A suppression of 3-4% is observed in the forward-rapidity region $5.2 < y < 7.2$ due to the reduced quark-antiquark abundance at finite baryon density. We further examine the effective temperature extracted from dilepton mass spectra in the intermediate-mass region $1.2 < M_{\ell \ell} < 2.6~\text{GeV}$ . The effective temperature remains strongly correlated with the underlying hydrodynamic temperature and retains sensitivity to the early high-temperature stage of the QGP evolution. These results demonstrate that forward-rapidity dileptons remain effective thermometers while providing sensitivity to finite baryon density at the LHC.

</details>


### [8] [Testing varying coupling constants through multi-Higgs production at the LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14303)
*Ulf Danielsson,Rikard Enberg,Gunnar Ingelman,Soumyadip Kundu,Tanumoy Mandal,Subhadip Mitra*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出“单标量理论”（One Scalar Theory, 1ST），用一个实单态标量场（real singlet scalar）动力学地生成希格斯自耦合（Higgs self-coupling）和顶-汤川耦合（top Yukawa coupling）。该框架锁定所有产生与衰变模式至单一基本尺度Λ₀，从而消除参数自由度，具有高度可预测性和独特实验信号。通过对ATLAS数据的再分析，论文给出Λ₀的TeV量级下界，并预言高亮度LHC（High-Luminosity LHC）可将探测范围扩展至4 TeV。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准模型（Standard Model）中希格斯自耦合和顶-汤川耦合的参数本质尚未被解释；现有portal模型引入过多自由参数，缺乏可检验的预测能力。该研究旨在构建一个最小化（minimalist）且高预测性的动力学产生机制，以填补这一空白。

Method: 采用1ST框架，通过单个实单态标量场（real singlet scalar）以动力学方式生成希格斯自耦合与顶-汤川耦合，并锁定所有过程至单一尺度Λ₀，消除额外参数。分析中利用2mₜ运动学阈值（kinematic threshold）将对撞机现象学划分为双希格斯共振区（di-Higgs regime）与双顶夸克共振区（di-top regime），并对现有ATLAS数据进行再分析（recasting）。

Result: 通过对ATLAS数据的再分析，获得Λ₀的TeV量级下界（lower bound）；高亮度LHC可将对该尺度的探测能力提升至4 TeV。

Conclusion: 1ST框架具有高度预测性和独特的实验信号，能够经受当前对撞机数据的检验。高亮度LHC有望对该动力学产生机制给出决定性检验（definitive test），从而揭示电弱扇区（electroweak sector）的动力学起源。

Abstract: We propose the One Scalar Theory (1ST), a minimalist framework where a single real singlet scalar field mediates the dynamical generation of the Higgs self-coupling and the top Yukawa coupling. Unlike generic portal models, the 1ST removes parametric freedom by locking production and decay modes to a single fundamental scale $Λ_0$, rendering the framework highly predictive with unique experimental signals. We demonstrate that the collider phenomenology is partitioned by the $2m_t$ kinematic threshold into di-Higgs and di-top resonance regimes. By recasting current ATLAS data, we set lower bounds on $Λ_0$ at the TeV scale and show that the High-Luminosity LHC will probe this scale up to $4$ TeV, providing a definitive test for the dynamical origin of the electroweak sector.

</details>


### [9] [The unintuitive SU(3) flavor and chiral limits of hadron resonances](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14634)
*José Ramón Peláez,Pablo Rabán,Jacobo Ruiz de Elvira*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文挑战了“强子共振态的极点会随对称性恢复而连续演化为简并态”这一直观预期，指出在SU(3)味对称（SU(3)_F）和手征极限（chiral limit）下，通常被忽略的“影子极点”（shadow poles）才是真正简并并表征共振态的极点。作者以光矢量介子（light-vector mesons）和光标量介子（light-scalar mesons）为例，利用单圈幺正化的QCD低能有效理论（QCD low-energy effective theory unitarized to one loop）找到了这些影子极点及其简并性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为，物理世界中用于严格定义强子共振态（hadron resonances）的极点会随着SU(3)_F和手征极限的恢复而连续演化为简并态。该论文旨在论证这一直觉是错误的，并揭示影子极点才是这些对称性极限下真正简并并刻画共振态的数学结构。

Method: 论文采用QCD低能有效理论（QCD low-energy effective theory），并施加单圈幺正化（unitarized to one loop）条件。首先以简单且熟知的光矢量介子为例进行说明，随后推广到被广泛讨论的光标量介子体系，通过该理论框架找出影子极点并分析其简并性。

Result: 结果表明，在SU(3)_F和手征极限下，用于定义物理共振态的通常极点并不连续演化为简并态；相反，那些通常被忽略的影子极点才是实现简并并表征共振态的关键对象。该结论具有一般性，在光矢量介子和光标量介子体系中均得到验证。

Conclusion: 论文提出了一种关于强子共振态极点演化行为的一般性新认识：影子极点而非常规极点，在对称性极限下成为简并态并决定共振态特征。这一发现修正了关于极点连续演化的朴素预期，并为理解QCD对称性极限下的共振态结构提供了新的视角。

Abstract: Contrary to naive expectations, poles used to define hadron resonances rigorously in the physical world may not evolve continuously to become degenerate in the SU(3)$_F$ and chiral limits of QCD. Instead, other shadow poles, usually ignored, may be the ones that degenerate and characterize the resonances in these limits. This feature is general, and we illustrate it first with the simple and familiar light-vector mesons, followed by the much-discussed light-scalar case. Their shadow poles and their degeneracy are found using the QCD low-energy effective theory unitarized to one loop.

</details>


### [10] [Dynamical Mass Growing of Fermion with Bare Mass in Two Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13724)
*Toyoki Matsuyama*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了二维时空中费米子通过与有质量矢量场耦合产生的动力学质量生成（dynamical mass generation），利用施温格-戴森方程（Schwinger-Dyson equations）在最低阶梯近似（lowest-ladder approximation）下通过解析和数值方法求解，发现了纯动力学质量（purely dynamical mass）与裸质量（bare mass）之间的依赖关系，并在特定耦合常数处观察到裸质量之间的对偶关系（duality relation）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究费米子通过与有质量矢量场耦合产生动力学质量的机制，旨在理解非微扰效应对费米子质量的影响，并厘清纯动力学质量与裸质量之间的关系。

Method: 采用施温格-戴森方程（Schwinger-Dyson equations）在最低阶梯近似（lowest-ladder approximation）下进行求解；使用近似解析方法与数值方法两种途径求解该方程。

Result: 定义了从总动力学质量中减去裸质量后剩余的纯动力学质量（purely dynamical mass）；阐明了纯动力学质量在不同耦合常数区域对裸质量的依赖关系；发现在特定耦合常数值处，不同裸质量对应的纯动力学质量趋于一致，此时满足裸质量之间的对偶关系（duality relation）。

Conclusion: 纯动力学质量与裸质量之间具有非平凡的依赖关系，且在特定耦合常数下存在裸质量对偶性，这为理解二维时空中费米子动力学质量生成的非微扰行为提供了新见解。

Abstract: We study dynamical mass generation of a fermion with and without a bare mass by coupling with a massive vector field in two-dimensional space-time. To estimate a non-perturbative effect on the fermion mass, we employ the Schwinger-Dyson equations in the lowest-ladder approximation, which are solved by an approximated analytical method and also by a numerical method. We define a purely dynamical mass as a remnant after subtracting the bare mass from a total dynamical mass. We clarify dependence of the purely dynamical mass on the bare mass of the fermion in various region of a coupling constant. Especially we find that the purely dynamical masses growing from the different bare masses coincide with each other at a specific value of the coupling constant where a kind of a duality relation on the bare masses is satisfied.

</details>


### [11] [Anomalies, Topology, and Hadron Structure in QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13908)
*Ismail Zahed*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文综述了量子色动力学（QCD）中由量子反常（anomalies）导致的对称性破缺的理论基础与物理后果，重点讨论了轴反常（axial anomaly）与迹反常（trace anomaly）如何联结真空拓扑结构、强子性质与部分子观测量，并特别关注了真空拓扑、味单态轴荷、拓扑屏蔽与质子自旋问题等最新进展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子色动力学（QCD）中的量子效应深刻地重塑了经典场论的对称性，但轴反常和迹反常如何从宏观上统一解释真空结构、强子质量起源以及部分子层面可观测量（如质子自旋结构）的内在联系，仍需提供一个系统性的统一视角来弥合非微扰动力学与微扰QCD之间的鸿沟。

Method: 本文采用综述性分析方法，系统梳理了反常Ward恒等式（anomalous Ward identities）、规范场拓扑结构（topological structure of gauge fields）、瞬子（instantons）、拓扑磁化率（topological susceptibility）以及QCD真空中手征对称性与标度对称性的实现等理论工具，并以此为基础讨论其在高能自旋物理与强子结构研究中的应用。

Result: 轴反常通过将手征性与规范场拓扑相连接，解决了U(1)_A问题；迹反常经由维度嬗变（dimensional transmutation）产生了QCD内禀标度，并贡献了强子（进而可见物质）的大部分质量。现代进展表明，真空拓扑、味单态轴荷与拓扑屏蔽机制在解释质子自旋问题中扮演关键角色。

Conclusion: 量子反常（quantum anomalies）在非微扰QCD与微扰QCD之间架起了桥梁，提供了一种将真空结构、强子性质与部分子可观测量统一起来的理论视角；真空拓扑与质子自旋结构的联系是当前及未来研究的重要方向。

Abstract: Quantum Chromodynamics (QCD) provides a remarkable realization of how quantum effects reshape the symmetries of a classical field theory. The axial anomaly links chirality to gauge-field topology and underlies the resolution of the $U(1)_A$ problem, while the trace anomaly generates the intrinsic QCD scale through dimensional transmutation and accounts for most of the mass of hadrons and hence visible matter. Together, these quantum effects reveal the central role of gluonic dynamics and vacuum structure in strong-interaction physics. In this review, we discuss the theoretical foundations and physical consequences of anomalous symmetry breaking in QCD. We examine anomalous Ward identities, the topological structure of gauge fields, instantons, topological susceptibility, and the realization of chiral and scale symmetries in the QCD vacuum. We review their role in the generation of hadron masses, the $η'$ mass, and the resolution of the $U(1)_A$ problem, and discuss their manifestations in polarized deep inelastic scattering, nucleon spin structure, and modern studies of hadron structure. Particular emphasis is placed on recent developments connecting vacuum topology, the flavor-singlet axial charge, topological screening, and the proton spin problem. Our aim is to provide a unified perspective on how quantum anomalies connect vacuum structure, hadron properties, and partonic observables, bridging nonperturbative dynamics and perturbative QCD.

</details>


### [12] [High-scale Mirror Standard Model Dark Matter, Dark Phase Transitions and Gravitational Waves Implications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14385)
*V. K. Oikonomou*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出一个由镜像标准模型（mirror Standard Model sector）构成的暗物质（dark matter）方案，该镜像扇区仅与普通扇区通过引力相互作用，但具有不同的能标和汤川耦合（Yukawa couplings）。研究发现，镜像世界相变（mirror world phase transition）在重子宇宙高温下发生，可为一级或二级相变，其中二级相变可能在随机引力波（stochastic gravitational waves）谱上留下直接印记。论文还探讨了镜像暗物质形成原子的可能性及其与子弹星团（Bullet cluster）和阿贝尔520星团（Abell 520 cluster）等观测矛盾的调和。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有暗物质模型面临观测与理论之间的冲突（如子弹星团与Abell 520星团的矛盾），因此需要一种既能解释暗物质成分又能调和不同观测结果的理论框架。作者假设存在一个与普通标准模型对称性相同但能标与汤川耦合不同的镜像标准模型扇区，以探索其能否作为暗物质候选者并解释宇宙演化中的相变现象。

Method: 假设镜像标准模型扇区仅通过引力与普通标准模型扇区相互作用，且镜像扇区的能标远高于普通扇区。同时设定镜像希格斯（mirror Higgs）与镜像费米子（mirror fermions）之间的汤川耦合与标准模型不同。基于这些假设，分析不同能标和汤川耦合对宇宙演化的影响，研究镜像世界相变的性质（一级或二级），并估算镜像暗物质的总状态方程（equation of state）。

Result: 镜像世界相变在重子宇宙高温下发生，且远早于真实世界的标准模型电弱相变（electroweak phase transition）。相变的阶次（一级或二级）取决于宇宙能标和汤川耦合的大小。二级相变可能在未来引力波探测器可探测的频率范围内的随机引力波谱上留下直接印记。在某些场景下，高能标镜像暗物质可以同时包含原子组分（atomic component）和亚原子粒子组分（subatomic particle component）。

Conclusion: 高能标镜像暗物质有望调和子弹星团与Abell 520星团等看似矛盾的观测结果。该模型为暗物质研究提供了一个可检验的理论框架，尤其是通过未来引力波探测器对二级相变产生的随机引力波信号的探测。

Abstract: We consider a scenario for dark matter in the Universe, according to which the dark matter sector is comprised by a dark Standard Model sector which interacts only gravitationally with the ordinary Standard Model sector. This dark Standard Model sector is assumed to have the same symmetries as the ordinary Standard Model, with the couplings and the scale of the mirror Standard Model sector being different than the ordinary Standard Model sector. Specifically, the scale of the mirror Standard Model sector will be assumed to be quite higher compared to the ordinary Standard Model. Also the Yukawa couplings among the mirror Higgs and the mirror fermions are assumed to be different from those of the Standard Model and we examine the effects of the different scale and of the different Yukawas on the evolution of the Universe. As we show, a mirror world phase transition occurs at high temperatures of the baryonic Universe, which can be first order or second order, depending on the scale of the Universe and the Yukawa couplings. These are dark phase transitions which occur quite earlier than the real world Standard Model electroweak phase transition. The case of a second order phase transition is quite interesting phenomenologically, since it can potentially have a direct imprint on the spectrum of stochastic gravitational waves for frequencies probed by the future gravitational wave detectors. Also we examine whether this mirror dark matter world can form atoms and as we show in some scenario the high scale mirror dark matter can have both atomic and subatomic particle components. We also give an approximation of the total equation of state of high scale mirror DM and we discuss how high scale mirror DM can reconcile contradicting observations like the Bullet cluster and the Abell 520 cluster.

</details>

### [13] [Mean First Passage Time for Persistent Random Walks in Annular Search Domains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13890)
*Fatemeh Saghafifar,Daniel Coombs*

Main category: q-bio.CB

TL;DR: 本文研究二维环形域中心小吸收目标被随机游走者首次通过的平均时间，其中外边界为镜面反射。以自然杀伤细胞向目标癌细胞的迁移为背景，采用速度跳跃过程（velocity-jump process）建模细胞运动，分别考虑基于von Mises转向核的关联随机游走（correlated random walk）和加入相移的偏置关联随机游走（biased correlated random walk），并结合解析方法与数值模拟分析方向持续性和趋化偏置对搜索效率的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量化免疫细胞（如自然杀伤细胞）到达目标癌细胞所需的时间，并分析方向持续性（directional persistence）和趋化偏置（chemotactic bias）如何影响搜索效率，从而为理解免疫细胞在受限二维空间中的靶向迁移提供理论框架。

Method: 采用速度跳跃过程建模细胞运动：首先基于von Mises转向核（von Mises turning kernel）构建关联随机游走模型，浓度参数控制方向持续性；进一步引入相移转向核（phase-shifted turning kernel）扩展为偏置关联随机游走，表征趋化梯度下的优先运动。分析方法包括：简单与偏置随机游走的闭合形式基准解、关联与偏置模型的输运方程傅里叶模态降阶、以及快速转向微扰展开（fast-turning perturbation expansion）对扩散极限平均首次通过时间（mean first-passage time）的解析修正。数值方法包括：径向-角坐标半拉格朗日求解器、处理偏置输运的稳态离散化方案，以及事件驱动蒙特卡洛模拟（event-driven Monte Carlo simulation）进行交叉验证。

Result: 解析结果与数值方法相互支撑，建立了方向持续性和偏置运动与受限二维域中靶向搜索时间之间的定量关系。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一个连接持续性与偏置免疫细胞运动与目标搜索时间的分析框架，适用于受限二维空间中的免疫靶向迁移问题。

Abstract: We study the mean first-passage time of a random walker to a small absorbing target at the center of a two-dimensional annulus with a specularly reflecting outer boundary. The problem is motivated by natural killer cell migration toward a target cancer cell, where the goal is to quantify how long it takes immune cells to reach the target and how search efficiency depends on directional persistence and chemotactic bias. Cell motion is modeled as a velocity-jump process. We first consider a correlated random walk with a von Mises turning kernel, with a concentration parameter controlling directional persistence. We then extend the model to a biased correlated random walk using a phase-shifted turning kernel that represents preferential motion, for example following a concentration gradient. Our analysis combines closed-form benchmarks for simple and biased random walks, Fourier-mode reductions of the transport equations for the correlated and biased correlated models, and a fast-turning perturbation expansion that gives an analytical correction to the diffusion-limit mean first-passage time for the random walker. Our analytical results are supported by numerical methods that include a semi-Lagrangian solver in radial and angular coordinates, a stationary discretisation designed to handle biased transport, and an event-driven Monte Carlo simulator for cross-validation. Together, our results provide a framework relating persistent and biased immune-cell motion to target-search times in confined two-dimensional domains.

</details>

### [14] [Finite-volume effects on smeared spectral densities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14349)
*Francesca A. Bresciani,Mattia Bruno,Maxwell T. Hansen*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文通过两种独立方法，推导了在周期性立方体积中，涂抹矢量-矢量谱密度（即涂抹的强子R比值）的有限体积效应的普适表达式，指出该效应具有指数抑制特征，并可用π介子形状因子（pion form factor）统一描述。研究为控制涂抹谱密度的L→∞外推提供了理论依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在格点量子色动力学（lattice quantum chromodynamics）中，涂抹谱密度（smeared spectral density）的有限体积效应（finite-volume effects）对于准确外推无穷大体积极限（L→∞）至关重要。现有研究缺乏对这类效应的普适解析描述，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 采用两种独立途径：其一，基于欧几里得两点关联函数（Euclidean two-point functions）有限体积效应的已有结果，推导涂抹核（smearing kernel）在特定类别下的指数抑制关系；其二，从Lellouch-Lüscher-Meyer表达式出发，对关联函数进行谱分解（spectral decomposition），导出相同表示。

Result: 得到了涂抹矢量-矢量谱密度（即涂抹强子R比值）在周期性立方体积中有限体积效应的普适表达式，其L依赖呈指数抑制，且领头阶效应可由π介子形状因子统一表达。通过多种核与粒子相互作用模型的数值估算验证了该框架。

Conclusion: 该结果为控制涂抹谱密度的L→∞外推提供了理论工具，可通过定义标度区域（scaling regime）使有限体积效应由大L展开的领头项主导。尽管聚焦于矢量流，该推导定义了一个可推广至其他通道的通用框架。

Abstract: Using two distinct approaches, we derive a universal expression for the leading finite-volume effects of the smeared vector-vector spectral density (proportional to the smeared hadronic $R$-ratio) in a periodic cubic spatial volume of side length $L$. First, building on the results of previous work for finite-volume effects on Euclidean two-point functions, we show that the $L$ dependence is exponentially suppressed for a certain class of smearing kernels, and that the leading effects can be expressed universally in terms of the pion form factor. The same representation is then derived starting from the Lellouch-Lüscher-Meyer expression for the spectral decomposition of the correlator. The results may prove useful for controlling the $L \to \infty$ extrapolation of smeared spectral densities, in particular by defining a scaling regime in which the finite-volume effects are dominated by the leading terms in a large $L$ expansion and thus can be reliably estimated. To illustrate this point, we also present numerical estimates based on various kernels and models of particle interactions. Despite focusing on the vector channel, our derivation defines a general framework applicable to other cases as well.

</details>

### [15] [Controlling Defects and Probing Dynamics in Active Nematics with Deep Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13721)
*Russ Islam,Kyogo Kawaguchi,Yuto Ashida*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文利用深度强化学习（deep reinforcement learning）在活性向列相（active nematics）中实现对+1/2拓扑缺陷（topological defect）的最短时间位置控制。通过时空模式化的活性应力场（activity stress）引导缺陷在微通道中运动，揭示了可达区域受指向矢各向异性（director anisotropy）、垂面锚定（homeotropic wall anchoring）和活性模式的影响；在受限几何中，缺陷对产生可以扩展有效可达集。强化学习控制器优于静态和规则基线，且可组合为元控制器（meta-controller）完成更复杂的迷宫导航任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑缺陷控制对于活性物质物理（active matter physics）、智能材料（smart materials）和微流控（microfluidics）具有重要应用价值。然而，目前尚缺乏通用的方法利用活性模式来有效控制缺陷的运动轨迹，尤其是实现最小时间控制。

Method: 采用混合晶格玻尔兹曼模拟（hybrid lattice Boltzmann simulations）模拟活性向列动力学，并将深度强化学习（deep reinforcement learning, RL）作为控制框架。通过时空模式化的活性应力（spatiotemporally patterned activity）作为控制场，训练RL控制器以最小化+1/2缺陷到达目标位置所需的时间。

Result: 局部活性模式可在自由域中引导缺陷运动，但在交叉口处失效；全局模式则可打开原本不可达的通道。在受限几何中，原始缺陷无法抵达某些目标，但通过受控的缺陷对产生（controlled pair creation）可以创造出新的+1/2缺陷，从而扩展有效可达集。训练好的RL控制器优于静态和基于规则的基线，且仅在简单交叉口上训练的控制器可以组合为元控制器，无需微调即可成功引导缺陷通过更大的测试迷宫。自由能可视化显示，被引导的缺陷在指向矢场（director field）中写入持久的、历史依赖的畸变，而-1/2缺陷可以部分擦除这些畸变。

Conclusion: 基于强化学习的控制方法揭示了受限条件、锚定、驱动几何和缺陷产生如何决定活性向列相中的可达运动，为软物质和活性物质中的其他控制任务提供了一个通用框架。

Abstract: Topological defects govern much of the flow behavior and orientational order in active nematics, making their control relevant for active matter physics, smart materials, and microfluidics. Applied activity patterns can induce self-propulsion of active nematic defects, but general-purpose methods for exploiting this effect to control defects remain largely unexplored. Here we use deep reinforcement learning (RL) to perform minimum-time position control of +1/2 defects in hybrid lattice Boltzmann simulations of active nematodynamics. Spatiotemporally patterned activity, implemented as a control field in the active stress, steers defects through microchannel geometries and reveals finite-time reachable regions of defect position space. Reachability is shaped by director anisotropy, homeotropic wall anchoring, and the allowed activity patterns: local patterns steer defects in free domains but fail in junctions, whereas global patterns open otherwise inaccessible channels. In constrained geometries, the original defect may be unable to reach some goals intact, but controlled pair creation enlarges the effective reachable set by transferring control to a newly created +1/2 defect. The trained RL controllers outperform static and rule-based baselines, and controllers trained only on simple junctions can be combined without fine-tuning into a meta-controller that successfully steers defects through a larger test maze. Free energy visualizations show that guided defects write persistent, history-dependent distortions into the director field that can later be partially erased by -1/2 defects. Thus, RL-based control uncovers how confinement, anchoring, actuation geometry, and defect creation determine reachable motion in active nematics, providing a framework for other control tasks in soft and active matter.

</details>


### [16] [Topology-defined computation in knitted textiles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14062)
*Daisuke S. Shimamoto*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于拓扑而非几何的机械计算架构，利用单一连续纱线编织的针织织物实现信息编码与逻辑运算。逻辑通过织物结构的拓扑（topology）定义，而非传统的几何形变。实验展示了通用逻辑门（NOT、AND、OR）和半加器（half-adder）的实现，并证明逻辑输出对几何变形具有鲁棒性（robustness）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机械计算（mechanical computation）系统中（如折纸、剪纸、力学超材料），逻辑状态和功能通常由几何与材料属性决定，因此对变形和缺陷敏感。本文旨在建立一种由拓扑而非几何定义逻辑的机械计算架构，以克服传统方案对几何变形的敏感性问题。

Method: 以单一连续纱线编织的针织织物作为计算电路。信息编码于针脚（stitch）的拓扑结构中，通过受控的解编织（unraveling）过程进行处理。将织物离散化为相互作用的单元晶格（lattice of interacting cells），构建拓扑传播规则（topological propagation rules），实现通用逻辑运算。

Result: 实验实现了NOT、AND、OR门以及半加器（half-adder）等通用逻辑运算。结果显示逻辑输出对几何变形保持鲁棒，而力学因素仅影响计算是否能够执行，而不影响逻辑结果的正确性。

Conclusion: 本文建立了一种由拓扑定义计算的模型，证明了在纺织品及其他可重构物理系统（reconfigurable physical systems）中，拓扑可作为信息处理的基础。

Abstract: Mechanical computation, in which logic functions are realized through deformation rather than electronics, has been demonstrated in systems such as origami, kirigami, and mechanical metamaterials. In these systems, logic states and functions are typically determined by geometry and material properties, making it sensitive to deformation and imperfections. Here we introduce a mechanical computing architecture in which logic is defined by topology rather than geometry. The circuit is realized as a knitted textile formed from a single continuous yarn, where information is encoded in the topology of stitches and processed through controlled unraveling. By discretizing the textile into a lattice of interacting cells, we construct topological propagation rules that implement universal logic operations, including NOT, AND, and OR gates, as well as a half-adder. Experiments demonstrate that the logical output is robust against geometric deformation, while mechanical factors affect only if the computation can be executed. These results establish topology-defined computation as a model for information processing in textiles and other reconfigurable physical systems.

</details>


### [17] [Field-selective criticality in 2D melting revealed by multi-field Lee-Yang zeros](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14075)
*Ling Liu,Fang-Cheng Wang,Qi-Jun Ye,Xin-Zheng Li*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文利用Lee-Yang零点（Lee-Yang zeros）结合增强采样（enhanced sampling）方法，研究纳米受限双层水的熔化行为，发现不同热力学驱动场（温度与侧向压力）对相变连续性的响应具有场选择性（field-selective），从而重新组织了关于二维熔化（two-dimensional melting）长期存在的争议性实验与模拟结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维固体如何熔化这一问题历经60年仍未解决，理论、模型系统、模拟和原子分辨实验不断提出矛盾图景；同一种相变在不同观测方式下既可表现为连续相变也可表现为突变，该歧义在受限水（confined water）中尤为突出。因此，作者不仅关注相边界的位置，更追问系统对驱动相变的两类场——温度（temperature）与侧向压力（lateral pressure）——的响应机制。

Method: 采用Lee-Yang零点方法结合增强采样，研究纳米受限条件下双层水（bilayer water）的熔化行为；通过分析系统对温度和侧向压力这两个驱动场的响应，识别相变的连续性特征，并通过增大模拟单元尺寸揭示潜藏的双模态焓分布（hidden bimodal enthalpy distribution）。

Result: 发现部分相边界具有场选择性：两种响应在连续性本身或有限体系中被展平（rounded）的程度上存在差异。固态-六角相（solid–hexatic）转变为场选择性一级相变（field-selective first-order），密度通道（density channel）异常地保持展平；六角相-液态（hexatic–liquid）转变在更大模拟单元中显现出潜藏的双模态焓分布，成为常规一级相变（conventional first-order transition）。

Conclusion: 该框架通过识别每种探测手段所“看见”的热力学通道（thermodynamic channel），将受限水模拟、硬圆盘模型（hard-disk models）和AgI实验之间表面上的分歧统一起来，为二维熔化争议提供了新的组织性理解。

Abstract: How a two-dimensional solid melts remains unsettled after 60 years of study, as theory, model systems, simulations, and atomic-resolution experiments continue to suggest conflicting scenarios. The same transition can appear continuous or abrupt depending on how it is observed, where this ambiguity is especially acute in confined water. Here we study bilayer water under nanoconfinement and ask not only where its phase boundaries lie, but how the system responds to the two fields that drive them: temperature and lateral pressure. Using Lee-Yang zeros together with enhanced sampling, we find that some phase boundaries are field-selective: the two responses can differ either in continuity itself, or in how strongly they are rounded in finite systems. This distinction changes the two-step melting picture. The solid--hexatic transition is field-selective first-order, with the density channel remaining unusually rounded, whereas the hexatic--liquid transition becomes a conventional first-order transition once larger cells reveal a hidden bimodal enthalpy distribution. This framework organizes the apparent disagreement among confined-water simulations, hard-disk models and AgI experiments by identifying which thermodynamic channel each probe sees.

</details>


### [18] [Thinning-by-spinning: shear rheology of dense chiral fluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14311)
*Lucio Mauro Carenza,Giuseppe Gonnella,Demian Levis,Giuseppe Negro*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过粒子模拟研究自旋密集手性流体的线性和非线性流变学，发现手性（chirality）可作为内在的波动与剪切源，导致流体化，并在有效温度框架下统一描述其粘度和剪切变稀行为，同时揭示了显著的手性不对称性流变机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解手性活性流体在密集状态下的流变学行为，特别是手性如何作为内在源影响系统的线性与非线性响应。

Method: 采用二维Lennard-Jones模型，引入横向相互作用（transverse interactions）实现手性粒子的自旋，并结合外部剪切，通过基于粒子的模拟（particle-based simulations）研究系统的流变性质。

Result: 在手性固体体系中，自旋导致流体化和六角序（hexatic order）减弱；在液体体系中，粘度可由类Green-Kubo关系通过手性依赖的有效温度定量描述；非线性响应中的流变曲线在施加剪切与自旋速率之比下坍塌，显示“自旋致稀”机制；在强驱动下，手性不对称凸显，当横向作用与剪切方向相反时形成弦状流通道。

Conclusion: 手性是一种通用的流体化机制，该工作为理解密集手性悬浮液的流变行为提供了统一的理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate the linear and nonlinear rheology of dense chiral fluids composed of self-spinning particles under external shear. Using particle-based simulations of a two-dimensional Lennard-Jones model with transverse interactions, we show that chirality acts as an intrinsic source of fluctuations and shear. In the solid regime, spinning fluidizes the system, weakening hexatic order. In the liquid regime, the viscosity is quantitatively described by a Green-Kubo relation upon replacing the temperature by a chirality-dependent effective temperature. Beyond linear response, flow curves collapse when expressed in terms of the ratio between imposed shear and spinning rates, revealing a thinning-by-spinning mechanism. At large forcing, this correspondence breaks down and a pronounced handedness asymmetry emerges: when transverse interactions oppose the imposed shear, stresses relax through the formation of string-like flow channels. Our results identify chirality as a generic mechanism for fluidization and provide a unified framework for understanding the rheology of dense chiral suspensions.

</details>


### [19] [Spherical metadensity functional learning for inhomogeneous classical fluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14370)
*Stefanie M. Kampa,Matthias Schmidt,Florian Sammüller*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了经典密度泛函学习（classical density functional learning）方法，在三维球形几何中处理具有截断对相互作用的流体。通过监督训练神经网络元密度泛函（neural metadensity functional），利用测试粒子路径（test particle route）从体相流体的径向分布函数（radial distribution function）中学习，实现对曲率效应和热缩放对势的建模。该方法可准确预测非均匀流体结构、验证热力学测试粒子求和规则（sum rules），并通过Henderson反演推断对势，在硬球流体中与标准神经密度泛函和基本测度理论（fundamental measure theory）的结果吻合良好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的经典密度泛函理论（classical density functional theory, DFT）在处理具有截断对相互作用的流体时，往往在弯曲几何或非均匀环境中面临建模困难。本文旨在发展一种数据驱动的神经元密度泛函方法，使其能够在不依赖固定对势形式的前提下，灵活捕捉空间曲率效应和热缩放对势的影响，从而扩展密度泛函理论在复杂几何系统中的应用能力。

Method: 本文提出**球形局域学习（spherical local learning）**方法，通过神经网络表示单体直接相关泛函（one-body direct correlation functional）。训练数据源自具有随机化排斥对势的流体体系的模拟结果，利用测试粒子路径从体相径向分布函数中提取监督信号。该方法同时引入元密度泛函（metadensity functional）依赖关系，将对势的热缩放依赖性纳入模型，并通过自动微分（automatic differentiation）获得两体直接相关泛函。

Result: 该框架高效获取了流体在弯曲溶质吸附和平板/球形空腔受限条件下的非均匀结构。测试粒子设置实现了体相流体对结构的准确预测，并通过泛函线积分验证了热力学测试粒子求和规则。应用元密度泛函进行Henderson反演，能够从体相径向分布函数中准确推断对势。对于硬球流体，该方法的预测结果与标准神经密度泛函（固定对势）以及基本测度理论的分析泛函结果一致，模拟结果进一步证实了该方法在广泛应用中的可靠性。

Conclusion: 本文发展的球形神经元密度泛函（spherical neural metadensity functional）框架成功地解决了具有截断对相互作用的流体在弯曲几何中的密度泛函建模问题。该方法不仅提供了对非均匀流体结构的准确描述，还通过Henderson反演实现了从结构信息逆向推断对势的可能性。研究结果表明，数据驱动的元密度泛函方法能够统筹兼顾对势依赖性与几何效应，为经典密度泛函理论在复杂流体系统中的应用开辟了新的路径。

Abstract: We develop classical density functional learning to address fluids with truncated pairwise interparticle interactions in three-dimensional spherical geometry. Simulation data for systems with randomized repulsive pair potentials provide the basis for supervised training of a neural metadensity functional, thereby making efficient use of results for radial distribution functions in the bulk fluid via the test particle route. Specifically, we develop spherical local learning in order to represent the one-body direct correlation functional in terms of a neural network, which captures spatial curvature effects as well as the metadensity functional dependence on the thermally scaled pair potential. The framework yields efficient access to inhomogeneous structuring and related physical phenomena that occur in fluids and general solvents when adsorbed against curved solutes and confined inside of spherical and planar cavities. Test particle setups facilitate accurate prediction of the bulk fluid pair structure and verification of thermodynamic test particle sum rules via functional line integration. Applying the metadensity functional for Henderson inversion allows one to infer accurately the pair potential from the bulk radial distribution function. We address implications of the geometrical setup for two-body quantities and obtain the two-body direct correlation functional from automatic differentiation. For the hard sphere fluid, we confirm metadensity functional predictions against results from a standard neural density functional with fixed pair potential as well as to an analytic functional as given by fundamental measure theory. Simulation results provide further reference and corroborate reliable results of the spherical neural metadensity functional across a broad range of applications.

</details>


### [20] [Bacterial adhesion to curved surfaces in fluid flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14543)
*Edwina F. Yeo,Benjamin J. Walker,Philip Pearce,Mohit P. Dalwadi*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过渐近分析方法研究了游动细菌在波纹二维通道中的扩散边界层传输与粘附行为，推导出细菌粘附速率的解析表达式，预测了细菌在曲面上的局部化粘附模式，且该模式随壁面剪切速率变化而发生峰值与谷值之间的偏好性转移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解细菌在非均匀流场中如何传输并粘附于复杂几何表面，对于在工业和医疗环境中最小化细菌表面粘附及后续生物膜（biofilm）形成具有重要意义。

Method: 采用基于流体流函数（streamfunction）的曲线坐标系，对高速流动中形成的扩散边界层（diffusive boundary layer）进行渐近分析，给出了扩散系数变化的扩散型方程（diffusivity-varying diffusion-type equation）的相似解（similarity solution），并由此推导出细菌粘附速率关于表面弧长（arclength）和空间变化壁面剪切率（wall shear rate）的解析表达式。

Result: 模型预测细菌粘附在弯曲表面上呈现局部化特征：在较低剪切速率下，细菌优先粘附于壁面“峰值（peaks）”；在较高剪切速率下，则优先粘附于壁面“谷值（valleys）”。

Conclusion: 由复杂几何产生的空间变化流场可导致局部化的细菌粘附，这一发现对增强或最小化生物膜形成具有潜在的应用意义。

Abstract: Minimising bacterial surface adhesion and subsequent biofilm formation in industrial and medical settings requires understanding how bacteria are transported and adhere to complex surface geometries in the presence of non-uniform flow. In this paper, we consider the transport of a dilute suspension of motile bacteria through a corrugated two-dimensional channel with perfectly adhesive walls. We asymptotically analyse the diffusive boundary layer that forms in high velocity flows using a curvilinear coordinate system based on the fluid streamfunction, presenting a similarity solution to the diffusivity-varying diffusion-type equation that arises. From this solution, we derive an analytical expression for the bacterial adhesion rate as a function of surface arclength and the spatially varying wall shear rate. Our model predicts that bacterial adhesion becomes localised on curved surfaces, with bacteria showing preferential adhesion to wall `peaks' at lower shear rates and preferential adhesion to wall `valleys' at higher shear rates. More broadly, our results highlight how spatially varying flows generated by complex geometries can lead to localised bacterial adhesion, with potential implications for both enhancing and minimising biofilm formation.

</details>


### [21] [On the physical meaning of latent track boundaries in swift heavy ion irradiated polymers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14547)
*Adil Tuleushev,Fiona Harrison,Maxim Zdorovets*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过分析多种实验技术（SAXS、XRD、化学蚀刻、电导率测量）探测潜径迹（latent track）边界的不同物理判据，解释了快重离子（swift heavy ion）在介电材料中产生的径迹尺寸估计差异的来源，并特别关注具有驻极体（electret）性质的聚合物薄膜中弱束缚电子再分布对径迹结构演化的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大量快重离子在介电材料中潜径迹的实验研究给出了差异很大的径迹尺寸估计，本文旨在探究这些估计的物理含义，理解不同实验方法为何得到不同的径迹边界测定结果。

Method: 通过比较四种实验技术——小角X射线散射（SAXS）、X射线衍射（XRD）、化学蚀刻（chemical etching）和电导率测量（conductometry）——所探测的不同物理判据，系统分析它们对径迹边界的不同定义方式。

Result: 不同实验方法探测的是离子诱导改性的不同物理方面：电子密度再分布、分子有序性、化学反应活性和电荷分离，因而导致对有效径迹边界（effective track boundaries）的不同测定结果。

Conclusion: 在具有驻极体性质的聚合物薄膜中，辐照后弱束缚电子的再分布可能对潜径迹结构的演化发挥重要作用。

Abstract: A large body of experimental studies of swift heavy ion latent tracks in dielectric materials has produced a wide range of estimates of track size. We investigate the physical meaning of these estimates by examining the different criteria of track boundary probed by various experimental techniques, including SAXS, XRD, chemical etching and conductometry. We show that different methods probe different physical aspects of ion induced modification, such as electron density redistribution, molecular ordering, chemical reactivity and charge separation, resulting in different determinations of effective track boundaries. Particular attention is paid to polymer films with electret-like properties, where post irradiation redistribution of weakly bound electrons may play an important role in the evolution of latent track structure.

</details>


### [22] [Percolation of a rod-like particle in a static bed of spheres: trapping and passing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14661)
*Juan C. Petit,Julio M. Ottino,Richard M. Lueptow,Paul B. Umbanhowar*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 通过数值模拟研究重力作用下独立无摩擦的胶合球棒状颗粒（glued-sphere rod-like particles）在无序静态大球床中的渗流（percolation）行为，发现了“捕获”（trapping）和“通过”（passing）两种截然不同的动力学相，并揭示了棒长如何通过几何约束（geometric constraints）主导相变、速度标度关系（scaling collapse）及非球形颗粒的分离机制（segregation mechanisms）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究形状各向异性（shape anisotropy）对于颗粒在无序介质中渗流行为的影响，特别是棒状颗粒与球形颗粒在动力学阈值、传输速度及其受困机制上的差异，进而理解非球形颗粒混合物中的分离现象。

Method: 采用数值模拟方法，在重力条件下让独立的无摩擦胶合球棒状颗粒通过由较大球体构成的无序静态床进行渗流，系统的变化参数包括棒长、棒直径以及床的孔隙结构几何约束。

Result: 发现了捕获与通过两个不同的动力学相；所有棒几何形状（包括单球极限）的渗流速度在按照重力加速度和床球直径标度后能够坍塌为一条统一曲线；短棒的渗流速度几乎是长棒的两倍；长棒更容易通过特定的接触构型（contact configurations）被捕获。

Conclusion: 形状各向异性通过几何约束引入了颗粒渗流中的动力学阈值（dynamical thresholds）与约束，该结果对预测非球形颗粒混合物中的分离行为具有启示意义。

Abstract: We numerically investigate percolation of independent frictionless glued-sphere rod-like particles under gravity through a disordered static bed of larger spheres. We identify two distinct regimes: a \emph{trapping} regime, where rods stop after percolating a limited distance in the bed and a \emph{passing} regime, where rods percolate continuously with constant mean velocity. The transition between these regimes is governed by the length of the rod and the geometrical trapping threshold for spherical particles based on the rod diameter and the minimum pore throat diameter defined by three touching large spheres. The percolation velocity for all rod geometries, including the single sphere limit, collapses onto a single curve when scaled with the gravitational acceleration and the bed sphere diameter. The results also demonstrate that short rods percolate nearly twice as fast as long rods due to the geometric constraints associated with the disordered pore structure of the static bed. Consequently, long rods are more susceptible to trapping via specific contact configurations with the bed spheres, which differ from those for short rods. These results reveal how shape anisotropy introduces dynamical constraints and thresholds in granular percolation, with implications for predicting segregation in mixtures of non-spherical particles.

</details>


### [23] [Interfacial mass transfer resistance at fluid-fluid interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14678)
*Hyeongjoo Row,Brandon J. Wallace,Joshua B. Fernandes,Kevin R. Wilson,Kranthi K. Mandadapu*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过扩展线性不可逆热力学（linear irreversible thermodynamics），识别出微尺度界面传质（interfacial mass transport）的界面限制区（interface-limited regime），并开发了一种结合微流控与光谱技术的实验方法，直接测量了表面活性剂稳定的水-油界面上的传质系数（约7 nm/s），从而建立了界面传质阻力作为微尺度传输控制机制的框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微纳尺度的复杂化学体系常受限于流体-流体界面（fluid-fluid interface）上的物质传输速率，但传统模型假设界面局部平衡（local equilibrium），在小尺度下可能失效。因此需要新的理论框架与实验手段来刻画微尺度下可能成为速率限制步骤的界面过程。

Method: 理论上，扩展线性不可逆热力学以描述非平衡界面传质，识别出由界面阻力（interfacial resistance）主导的界面限制区，该区呈现指数弛豫（exponential relaxation）行为。实验上，结合微流控技术与光谱技术，直接测量了界面传质系数（interfacial mass transfer coefficient）。以乙腈（acetonitrile）在表面活性剂稳定的水-油界面的传输为模型体系进行了验证。

Result: 实验测得模型体系的界面传质系数约为7 nm/s。该结果证实了界面传质阻力是微尺度传输的一种控制机制。

Conclusion: 本研究为预测、控制和测量微尺度多相体系（multiphase systems）中的质量传输提供了理论框架与实验方法，揭示了界面传质阻力在微尺度传输中的关键作用。

Abstract: Complex chemistry in nano- and microscale compartments is often governed by how quickly reagents transit a fluid-fluid interface. Mass transport across interfaces is commonly modeled by assuming local equilibrium, enforcing continuity of chemical potential across the interface. While adequate at large scales, this approximation may break down at the microscale, where interfacial processes can become rate-limiting. Here, we extend linear irreversible thermodynamics to describe nonequilibrium interfacial mass transport. We identify an interface-limited regime, in which transport is governed by interfacial resistance and exhibits exponential relaxation. Combining microfluidic and spectroscopic techniques, we introduce an experimental technique that explores this regime and provides a direct measurement of the interfacial mass transfer coefficient. For a model system consisting of acetonitrile transport across a surfactant-stabilized water-oil interface, we obtain an interfacial transport coefficient ${M \sim 7\,{\rm nm/s}}$. These results establish interfacial mass transfer resistance as a governing mechanism in microscale transport and provide a framework to predict, control and measure mass transport in multiphase systems at microscale.

</details>

### [24] [Licence to Bin: Accurate and Scalable Inference for Binary Neutron Stars in Next-Generation Gravitational-Wave Detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14197)
*Nir Guttman,A. Makai Baker,Paul D. Lasky,Eric Thrane*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种改进的降阶求积（reduced-order quadrature）构造方法，用于高效处理下一代引力波探测器（如Cosmic Explorer）观测到的长时间双中子星并合信号，首次在约2小时、低至5 Hz、信噪比2090的信号上实现了降阶贝叶斯推断（reduced-order Bayesian inference），使原本计算不可行的分析在128 CPU核上约48小时内完成，并展示了单探测器对信号的精确天空定位能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 下一代引力波探测器将观测到持续时间更长、信噪比更高、频带更宽的双中子星并合信号，这对贝叶斯参数估计（Bayesian parameter estimation）构成了重大计算挑战。现有的降阶求积标准构造方法在该场景下存在严重的内存和精度限制，因此需要开发新的实用构造方案。

Method: 该方法的构造包括三大改进：改进的自适应频率采样（improved adaptive frequency sampling）、基于磁盘的流式处理（disk-backed streaming）以及子带降阶求积构造（subbanded reduced-order quadrature construction）。这些技术共同实现了对包含时间依赖探测器响应（time-dependent detector response）和自由光谱范围（free-spectral range）效应的长时间双中子星信号的高效降阶建模。

Result: 首次在约2小时、低至5 Hz、信噪比2090的双中子星信号上成功实现了降阶贝叶斯推断，且降阶求积的精度足以满足实际推断需求。完整分析在128 CPU核心上约48小时内完成。此外，当包含时间依赖探测器响应效应时，单个Cosmic Explorer探测器可将该信号的90%置信天空区域（90% credible sky area）定位至约41 deg²。

Conclusion: 降阶方法能够使下一代双中子星信号的贝叶斯推断在计算上变得可行。该结果对多信使天文学（multimessenger astronomy）和宇宙学具有重要启示。

Abstract: Next-generation gravitational-wave observatories will observe binary neutron-star mergers with much higher signal-to-noise ratios, over much longer durations and across broader frequency bands than current detectors. These long-duration signals present a major computational challenge for Bayesian parameter estimation. Reduced-order quadrature is a promising approach for accelerating inference, but in this regime its standard construction encounters severe memory and accuracy limitations. We present a practical reduced-order quadrature construction for long binary neutron-star signals with time-dependent detector response and full effects of the observatories' free-spectral range. Our approach combines improved adaptive frequency sampling, disk-backed streaming, and subbanded reduced-order quadrature construction, enabling efficient and accurate reduced-order models for signals that were previously intractable. We demonstrate for the first time reduced-order Bayesian inference on an approximately 2 h binary neutron-star signal extending down to 5 Hz and with signal-to-noise ratio 2090. We show the resulting reduced-order quadrature remains sufficiently accurate for practical inference. The full analysis is carried out in about 48 h using 128 CPU cores. We also find that, when time-dependent detector-response effects are included, a single Cosmic Explorer detector can localize such a signal to a 90% credible sky area of approximately $41~\mathrm{deg}^2$, with important implications for multimessenger astronomy and cosmology. These results demonstrate that reduced-order methods can make next-generation binary neutron-star inference computationally feasible.

</details>


### [25] [Detecting classical nova-like explosions with LISA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14473)
*Ethan McKeever,Shu Yan Lau,Hang Yu,Neil J. Cornish*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文研究了密近双白矮星系统中的新星爆发对LISA引力波观测的影响，分析了新星的可探测性以及忽略新星效应时对物理参数估计造成的偏差，并提出了基于数据分割的模型无关探测方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究已关注稳态质量传输对引力波波形的影响，但极少考虑新星爆发（nova bursts）的作用，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 将新星爆发建模为吸积体（accretor）的快速质量损失导致的引力波频率突变；通过解析方法预测新星直接探测的信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio），并分析忽略新星时参数偏差超过统计不确定性的条件；提出对比LISA数据前后两半段的模型无关探测方法。

Result: 给出了新星爆发直接探测的信噪比解析预测，确定了误建模偏差超过统计不确定性的参数区间；模型无关的数据分割方法可用于识别新星事件。

Conclusion: 该工作对识别和分类单个新星事件、约束全银河系新星爆发率具有意义，这在光学巡天中是一项具有挑战性的任务。

Abstract: Gravitational waves from close binary white dwarfs will form the bulk of measurements obtained by the Laser Interferometer Space Antenna (LISA). Previous studies have highlighted the importance of including the effects of steady-state mass transfer in waveform models as many individually resolvable white dwarf binaries will be interacting during the LISA observation window. However, few studies have considered the effect of novae on gravitational wave observations and parameter estimations. We fill in this gap by analyzing the detectability of novae in these systems and the biases in physical parameters when these bursts are not considered. We model a nova burst as a rapid loss of mass from the accretor that suddenly shifts the gravitational wave frequency. We analytically predict the signal-to-noise ratios for direct detection of the nova and where bias from mismodeling becomes greater than the statistical uncertainty. We also consider comparison of two halves of future LISA data to detect bursts in a model agnostic way. Our work has implications for identifying and classifying individual nova events as well as constraining the galactic nova rate throughout the entire galaxy, a challenging task for optical surveys.

### [26] [Linear Gravitational Wave Memory Through the Window of Core-Collapse Supernovae](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14670)
*Colter J. Richardson,Anthony Mezzacappa,Haakon Andresen,Michele Zanolin*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低频引力波（<50 Hz）在核坍缩超新星研究中日益重要，但其理论生成机制与检测方法尚需系统梳理，该文旨在填补这一综述空白。

Method: 采用综述方法，结合一个15倍太阳质量（15 $M_{\odot}$）太阳金属丰度前身星模型展示线性引力波记忆的生成结果，并利用线性预测滤波与匹配模板组合方法分析其在当前探测器中的检测能力。

Result: 示例结果表明，中微子各向异性发射是低频引力波记忆的主要来源；在当前引力波探测器中，结合线性预测滤波与匹配模板可实现一定程度的检测。

Conclusion: 低频引力波记忆有望在下一代探测器——宇宙探险家（Cosmic Explorer）、爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope）、激光干涉空间天线（Laser Interferometer Space Antenna）以及月球引力波天线（Lunar Gravitational-wave Antenna）中得到更有效的探测。

Abstract: Low-frequency gravitational waves ($\lessapprox$ 50 Hz) from core-collapse supernovae are becoming more important for current and future gravitational wave studies. This frequency region is dominated by the global morphology of the explosion and the anisotropic emission of neutrinos from the event. This paper serves as a brief review of both theory and detection (prospects) for gravitational waves in the low-frequency region. We discuss the generation of the linear gravitational wave memory sourced from neutrino emission and show results from an example 15 $M_{\odot}$ Solar metallicity progenitor. We also discuss the detection of the linear gravitational wave memory in current detectors, utilizing a combination of a linear predictive filter and matched templating. Finally we will discuss detection prospects in future detectors such as Cosmic Explorer, Einstein Telescope, the Laser Interferometer Space Antenna, and the Lunar Gravitational-wave Antenna.

### [27] [The Good, the Bad, and the Ugly -- Living with Priors in Bayesian confirmation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14281)
*Niels Linnemann,Christian Wüthrich*

Main category: physics.hist-ph

TL;DR: 该论文通过引力波研究案例，从物理学实践角度探讨了贝叶斯确认（Bayesian confirmation）中的先验问题（prior problem），分析了在先验敏感（prior sensitivity）情况下如何判断其认识论上的合理性，并提供了对“类比确认（analogue confirmation）”的更清晰诊断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 贝叶斯确认面临一个经典问题：初始先验（initial priors）从何而来？在数据充足且重复更新的情形下，不同先验趋于收敛至相同的后验（posterior）。但在前沿研究中，这种收敛往往失败，导致确认对先验敏感。该论文旨在探讨物理实践如何处理此类情况，并从规范层面判断先验敏感何时在认识论上构成问题。

Method: 采用实践导向（practice-based）的分析方法，以引力波研究为具体案例，考察物理学界处理先验问题的实际做法。该进路在关于贝叶斯主义（Bayesianism）的哲学文献中此前尚付阙如。

Result: 提出了一个基于物理学实践的、关于先验问题的系统性解释。该分析有助于对所谓的“类比确认”做出更清晰的诊断。

Conclusion: 在先验敏感的情形下，物理学实践的考察可以揭示哪些先验敏感性在认识论上是有问题的，哪些是合理的。该研究填补了贝叶斯主义哲学文献中实践维度的空白。

Abstract: Bayesian confirmation faces a classic problem: where do initial priors come from? In cases with abundant data and repeated updating, different priors tend to converge to the same posterior. However, in frontier research this convergence often fails, and confirmation remains sensitive to priors. We examine how physics practice in the case of gravitational wave research deals with such cases and, normatively, when prior sensitivity should be regarded as epistemically problematic. We offer a practice-based account of the prior problem, so far absent from the philosophical literature on Bayesianism. One upshot is a clearer diagnosis of so-called 'analogue confirmation'.

</details>

### [28] [Optimal binning of $D\rightarrow K_{\mathrm S}^0π^+π^-$ and $D\rightarrow K_{\mathrm S}^0K^+K^-$ phase space for experimental measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13948)
*Marcelo Bovill,Nathan Jurik,Sneha Malde*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 Dalitz 图分箱方案在测量 CKM 弱相位 γ 时灵敏度有限，且未能充分考虑与其他物理参数的简并性（degeneracy）以及本底（background）的精确处理；同时，针对粲夸克混合观测量 x_CP 和 Δx 的专用分箱方案尚付阙如。

Method: 设计了一种新的品质因子进行优化，该指标相比以往指标能更好地表征对 γ 的灵敏度；优化过程纳入了与其他物理参数的简并性考量以及更精确的本底处理。对粲夸克混合观测量，首次进行了专用优化，同时考虑了统计灵敏度（statistical sensitivity）和因探测器分辨率（detector resolution）导致的 bin 迁移（migration of events）效应。

Result: 利用 B± → DK± 衰变并结合 D → K⁰_S π⁺π⁻，预期将 γ 测量精度提升约 5%。对于粲夸克混合观测量，新方案使统计灵敏度提升约 20%，同时 bin 迁移引入的偏差（bias）维持在现有方案的水平。

Conclusion: 所提出的新分箱方案在 γ 测量和粲夸克混合观测量两方面均能带来可观的灵敏度提升，且对实验本底和探测器效应具有更好的鲁棒性（robustness）。

Abstract: New binning schemes for the Dalitz plots of $D \rightarrow K^0_{\mathrm S}π^+π^-$ and $D \rightarrow K^0_{\mathrm S} K^+ K^-$ decays are presented. These are determined using a new figure of merit for optimisation that better represents the sensitivity to $γ$ than previous metrics. Further augmentation comes from including consideration of degeneracy with other physics parameters determined simultaneously and a more accurate treatment of relevant backgrounds. The overall expected improvement in the precision of $γ$ measurements using $B^\pm\to DK^\pm$ decays, followed by $D \rightarrow K^0_{\mathrm S}π^+π^-$, is estimated at around 5$\%$. In addition, the first dedicated optimisation is performed for the observables relevant to charm mixing, $x_{CP}$ and $Δx$, in $D \rightarrow K^0_{\mathrm S}π^+π^-$ decays. This procedure accounts for both statistical sensitivity and the migration of events between bins due to detector resolution. The resulting binning scheme leads to an estimated gain of approximately 20$\%$ in statistical sensitivity, while maintaining the bias due to bin migration at a level comparable to the currently used scheme.

Yamazumi,C. Yanagisawa,Y. Yang,T. Yano,N. Yershov,U. Yevarouskaya,M. Yokoyama,Y. Yoshimoto,N. Yoshimura,R. Zaki,A. Zalewska,J. Zalipska,G. Zarnecki,J. Zhang,X. Y. Zhao,H. Zheng,H. Zhong,T. Zhu,M. Ziembicki,E. D. Zimmerman,M. Zito,S. Zsoldos*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文详述了T2K实验中离轴近探测器ND280在约束中微子通量和中微子-原子核相互作用截面方面的方法论与结果，展示了通过新的截面模型和通量预测拟合数据来控制系统不确定性的过程，并通过稳健性研究验证了方法的可靠性，最后预测了升级后的ND280对未来振荡测量的改进潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在T2K实验的中微子振荡测量中，系统不确定性是影响振荡参数拟合精度的关键因素。ND280近探测器的基本作用在于约束入射中微子通量（neutrino flux）和中微子-原子核相互作用截面（neutrino-nucleus interaction cross sections），从而实现对系统误差的稳健控制。本文旨在系统阐述这些约束的最新方法论与结果。

Method: 研究提出了一种新的中微子截面模型（neutrino cross-section model）并改进了通量预测（flux prediction），将其参数化后与ND280新事件选择（event selection）中的数据进行拟合。同时进行了广泛的稳健性研究（robustness studies），包括替代相互作用模型的拟合、与公开截面测量数据的一致性检查以及p值评估（p-value evaluations）。最后，通过灵敏度研究（sensitivity study）评估了升级后的ND280对未来约束的增强效果。

Result: 新的模型和通量参数化与ND280数据拟合后，有效约束了系统不确定性。稳健性研究表明所采用的方法论具有可靠性和稳健性。灵敏度研究结果显示，升级后的ND280因具有更好的接收度（acceptance）和更低的强子阈值（hadron threshold），可能进一步增强约束并减少振荡测量中的系统不确定性。

Conclusion: 本文所提出的约束方法能够在T2K最新中微子振荡分析中实现对系统不确定性的稳健控制，并且未来的ND280升级有望进一步提升这一能力，从而推动中微子振荡参数的精确测量。

Abstract: In the context of neutrino oscillation measurements from the T2K experiment, the off-axis near detector ND280 plays a crucial role in constraining the incoming neutrino flux and neutrino-nucleus interaction cross sections. The result is a robust control over systematic uncertainties in the fit of neutrino oscillation parameters to the data at the T2K far detector, Super-Kamiokande. This paper details the methodology and results of these constraints in the context of the latest neutrino oscillation analysis from T2K. It describes how a new neutrino cross-section model and refined flux prediction are parameterized and fit to data in new ND280 event selections. Additionally, this work reports the results of extensive robustness studies, including fits with alternative interaction models, consistency checks against publicly available cross-section measurements, and \textit{p}-value evaluations, to demonstrate the reliability and robustness of our methodology. Finally, we present a sensitivity study demonstrating that the upgraded ND280, with improved acceptance and a lower hadron threshold, may enhance future constraints and further reduce systematic uncertainties in oscillation measurements.

</details>

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 利用BESIII探测器在$\sqrt{s}=3.773$~GeV处收集的$20.3~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$数据样本，首次发现了强子跃迁过程$ψ(3770) \to π^0 J/ψ$，测量了其分支比并排除了部分理论预言，支持介子圈（meson loop）效应的解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索$ψ(3770)$的强子衰变过程，特别是等旋破缺（isospin-violating）的$ψ(3770) \to π^0 J/ψ$跃迁，以检验不同理论模型的预言能力。

Method: 基于BESIII探测器在质心能量$\sqrt{s}=3.773$~GeV处采集的$20.3~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$数据样本，对$e^+ e^- \to π^{0}J/ψ$过程进行统计显著性分析，并解耦$ψ(3770)$的直接贡献与$ψ(3686)$可能的干涉效应。

Result: 首次报告强子跃迁$ψ(3770) \to π^0 J/ψ$的证据，统计显著性为$4.5σ$；测量辐射修正后（dressed）的$e^+e^- \to π^0 J/ψ$反应截面为$(249 \pm 44 \pm 15)~\text{fb}$，分支比$\mathcal{B}(ψ(3770) \to π^0 J/ψ)=(2.08 \pm 0.36 \pm 0.21\pm 0.25) \times 10^{-5}$。

Conclusion: 该分支比显著低于四夸克模型（tetraquark model）的预言，但与考虑介子圈效应（meson loop effects）的计算相符，为理解$ψ(3770)$衰变中的等旋破缺机制提供了关键实验约束。

Abstract: We report the first evidence for the hadronic transition $ψ(3770) \to π^0 J/ψ$ using a data sample of $20.3~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$ collected at $\sqrt{s} = 3.773$~GeV with the BESIII detector. The $e^+ e^- \to π^{0}J/ψ$ process is observed with a statistical significance of $6.1σ$, while the significance specifically attributed to $ψ(3770) \to π^{0}J/ψ$ is $4.5σ$. We measure the dressed cross section for $e^+e^- \to π^0 J/ψ$ to be $(249 \pm 44 \pm 15)~\text{fb}$ and determine the branching fraction $\mathcal{B}(ψ(3770) \to π^0 J/ψ) = (2.08 \pm 0.36 \pm 0.21\pm 0.25) \times 10^{-5}$, where the first uncertainty is statistical, the second is systematic, and the third due to a possible interference with the $ψ(3686) \to π^{0}J/ψ$ decay. This is the first determination of this branching fraction. It lies significantly below tetraquark model predictions but aligns with calculations that incorporate meson loop effects, providing crucial insight into the isospin-violating nature of $ψ(3770)$ decays.

</details>


### [31] [Determining Neutrino Mass Ordering with NOvA and Upcoming JUNO Measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14121)
*NOvA Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文评估了JUNO实验对反应堆中微子质量平方差|Δm²₃₂|的预期测量，将如何提升NOvA实验对中微子质量顺序（neutrino mass ordering）的判定能力，发现在未来五年内，结合JUNO数据可在3σ置信水平上支持正常质量顺序（normal ordering）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: NOvA利用十年数据并结合反应堆实验的外部约束（external constraints）已报告了质量顺序判定的显著性；JUNO即将提供更精确的基于反应堆的|Δm²₃₂|约束。本研究旨在探索该预期测量对NOvA确定中微子质量顺序的潜在影响。

Method: 该研究通过数值分析方法，将JUNO对|Δm²₃₂|的预期测量结果作为外部约束，与NOvA的十年数据联合拟合（joint fit），评估在不同JUNO测量可能性下NOvA对正常质量顺序的发现能力。

Result: 研究发现，在未来五年内，对于多种合理的JUNO测量结果，NOvA均可在3σ置信水平上获得支持正常质量顺序（normal ordering）的证据。

Conclusion: JUNO对|Δm²₃₂|的精确测量可显著增强NOvA判定中微子质量顺序的能力，在合理预期下，正常质量顺序有望在数年内达到3σ的证据水平。

Abstract: NOvA has reported a significance of mass ordering determination using ten years of data together with external constraints from reactor-based experiments. The JUNO collaboration is poised to provide a more precise reactor-based constraint on $|Δm^2_{32}|$. In this Letter, we explore the potential impact of this anticipated measurement on the determination of the neutrino mass ordering by NOvA. We find that $3σ$ evidence of the normal ordering is achievable over a range of plausible JUNO measurements within the next five years.

</details>


### [32] [A Novel Approach to Short Baseline Oscillation Searches Using Neutrino Tagging with nuSCOPE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14263)
*Adrien Blanchet,César Jesús-Valls,Animesh Chatterjee,Stephen Dolan,Pierre Granger,Laura Munteanu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文首次研究了基于标记中微子束流（tagged neutrino beamline）的短基线中微子振荡搜索，以CERN拟议的nuSCOPE设施作为基准案例，展示了标记束流通过逐事件精确确定中微子味、能量和传播距离，在探测非标准中微子振荡方面的强大潜力，能够在单一实验中覆盖多个味转换通道并显著降低对通量预测的依赖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统短基线中微子振荡实验受到中微子通量预测不确定性的严重限制，且难以在同一实验中同时探测不同味转换通道（flavor transitions）以及出现（appearance）和消失（disappearance）两种模式。因此有必要探索新的实验手段来提升灵敏度并拓展参数空间覆盖范围。

Method: 以CERN拟议的nuSCOPE设施为基准案例，采用标记中微子束流（tagged neutrino beam）技术，逐事件精确测定中微子味、能量和传播距离。在$ν_μ$消失、$ν_μ\rightarrow ν_e$出现以及$ν_e$消失三个通道中评估对惰性中微子（sterile neutrino）诱导振荡的灵敏度。

Result: 标记束流能够在单一实验中同时探测多种味转换通道以及出现和消失两种模式，对质量平方劈裂（mass-squared splittings）的灵敏度跨越数个量级，同时大幅降低对中微子通量预测的依赖。nuSCOPE可以探测现有异常（anomalies）所激励的广泛参数空间区域，并将覆盖范围延伸到此前未探索的区域。

Conclusion: 标记中微子束流为精确振荡物理（precision oscillation physics）提供了强有力的新实验途径，具备显著提升短基线中微子振荡搜索能力的潜力。

Abstract: We present the first study of short-baseline neutrino oscillation searches using a tagged neutrino beamline, taking the proposed nuSCOPE facility at CERN as a benchmark. In this Letter we demonstrate that tagged neutrino beams, where the neutrino flavor, energy, and propagation distance are determined with exceptional event-by-event precision, provide a new experimental approach to search for non-standard neutrino oscillations. We evaluate the sensitivity to sterile-neutrino-induced oscillations in the $ν_μ$ disappearance, $ν_μ\rightarrow ν_e$ appearance, and $ν_e$ disappearance channels, demonstrating the ability to probe multiple flavor transitions and both appearance and disappearance modes within a single experiment. Our results show that tagged beams enable sensitivity improvements to mass-squared splittings spanning several orders of magnitude while substantially reducing the dependence on neutrino flux predictions that limits conventional searches. We find that nuSCOPE can probe a broad region of parameter space motivated by existing anomalies and extend coverage into previously unexplored territory, demonstrating the strong potential of tagged neutrino beams for precision oscillation physics.

</details>


### [33] [Search for dark photons from Higgs boson decays in the gluon-gluon fusion channel in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}=13.6$ TeV with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14362)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文利用ATLAS探测器在Run 3期间采集的135 fb⁻¹数据，搜索半可见希格斯玻色子衰变到光子和缺失横动量的末态（H → γγ_d），通过增强决策树（BDT）和基于数据的方法处理本底，未观测到显著超出标准模型预期的信号，在95%置信水平下给出H → γγ_d分支比的上限为1.4%（预期1.2%），并结合Run 2结果将上限改进至0.9%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索希格斯玻色子到暗光子（dark photon, γ_d）的衰变过程H → γγ_d，以寻找超出标准模型（Standard Model）的新物理信号，填补对半可见衰变模式（semi-visible Higgs decays）的搜索空白。

Method: 采用胶子-胶子融合（gluon-gluon fusion）产生道，利用2023年部署的新型触发条件（光子p_T > 50 GeV、缺失横动量p_T^miss > 70 GeV，且横质量m_T > 80 GeV）。使用增强决策树（boosted decision tree, BDT）识别误重建的主顶点（primary vertices），通过数据驱动方法（data-driven methods）估计喷注（jets）和电子误判为光子的本底，而真实光子本底由蒙卡模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）给出并经缪子控制区数据归一化。最后对m_T分布进行分箱最大似然拟合（binned maximum-likelihood fit）。

Result: 未观测到显著超出标准模型预期的信号，在95%置信水平下得到H → γγ_d分支比的观测（预期）上限为1.4%（1.2%）。与Run 2搜索结果合并后，观测（预期）上限改进至0.9%（0.9%）。

Conclusion: 当前数据与标准模型预言一致，未发现希格斯玻色子衰变到光子和暗光子的证据，给出了目前最严格的H → γγ_d分支比上限，并为未来更高统计量的搜索提供了参考基准。

Abstract: This paper presents a search for semi-visible Higgs boson decays in final states with a photon ($γ$) and missing transverse momentum $p_T^{miss}$. The analysis is optimised for the gluon-gluon fusion production channel and exploits a novel trigger deployed in 2023, with reduced thresholds down to 50 GeV on the photon transverse momentum ($p_T^γ$) and 70 GeV on the $p_T^{miss}$, in combination with a selection on the transverse mass of the $p_T^{miss}$-$γ$ system ($m_T$) above 80 GeV. The results are interpreted in terms of Higgs boson decays into a $γ$ and a dark photon $γ_d$ ($H \to γγ_d$). The analysis is performed using 135 fb$^{-1}$ of Run 3 data collected by ATLAS in 2023 and 2024. A boosted decision tree is used to identify events with misreconstructed primary vertices, which can affect the $p_T^{miss}$ calculation. Data-driven methods are employed to estimate the backgrounds from jets and electrons misidentified as photons, while the backgrounds with genuine photons are taken from Monte Carlo simulations, normalised to data in control regions with muons. A binned maximum-likelihood fit to the $m_T$ distribution is performed to evaluate the compatibility of the observed data with the Standard Model expectation. No significant excess is observed over the Standard Model prediction, and an observed (expected) upper limit on the branching ratio of $H \to γγ_d$ of 1.4% (1.2%) is obtained at 95% confidence level. Combining this result with previous Run 2 searches improves the observed (expected) upper limit to 0.9% (0.9%).

</details>


### [34] [Machine-learned particle flow as a foundation model for collider physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14373)
*Farouk Mokhtar,Joosep Pata,Michael Kagan,Javier Duarte*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文证明，将粒子碰撞事件重建（event reconstruction）构建为机器学习问题，能自然产生连接底层探测器数据与高层分析任务的共享表示（shared representation）。通过复用为粒子流重建（MLPF）训练的模型所习得的逐粒子潜表示（per-particle latent representations），在喷注味识别、喷注能量回归和缺失动量回归三项分析任务上显著超越仅使用运动学特征的基线方法。单个线性层仅依靠潜表示即可在多数任务上达到与先进基线可比的性能，并在缺失动量回归上以约1/35参数量超越基线，表明MLPF可作为基础模型（foundation model）迈向端到端分析管线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统粒子碰撞事件重建流程各步骤模块化且彼此割裂，缺乏连接底层探测器数据与高层物理分析任务的统一表示。本文旨在通过机器学习方法生成共享表示，实现从重建到分析任务的协同与迁移。

Method: 复用为粒子流重建（MLPF）训练的机器学习模型，提取其习得的逐粒子潜表示（latent representations）。将该潜表示作为额外输入特征接入三项下游分析任务：喷注味识别（jet flavor identification）、喷注能量回归（jet energy regression）和缺失动量回归（missing momentum regression），并与仅使用运动学特征的基线进行比较。此外，还评估仅用潜表示训练单个线性层的性能。

Result: 加入潜表示后，所有三项下游任务的性能均显著优于仅使用运动学特征的基线。仅用潜表示训练的单个线性层在性能上与先进基线架构可比，并在缺失动量回归任务上超越基线，参数量减少约35倍。

Conclusion: 重建过程中习得的潜表示编码了下游物理分析所需的本质信息，将MLPF确立为基础模型（foundation model），为从探测器数据到物理分析的端到端管线提供了具体可行的一步。

Abstract: The workflow from particle collision to physics analysis passes through a series of reconstruction steps that are traditionally modular and disconnected, with no shared representation linking low-level detector data to high-level analysis tasks. We show that casting event reconstruction as a machine learning problem naturally produces such a shared representation. We repurpose a machine learning model trained for particle-flow reconstruction (MLPF) to perform three distinct analysis tasks: jet flavor identification, jet energy regression, and missing momentum regression. By appending the per-particle latent representations learned during reconstruction as additional input features, we substantially improve over baselines that use kinematic features alone. We further demonstrate that a single linear layer trained using only the latent representations achieves competitive performance against state-of-the-art baseline architectures, and outperforms the baseline for missing momentum regression with approximately 35 times fewer parameters. These results demonstrate that the latent representations learned during reconstruction encode essential physics information needed for downstream analysis, establishing MLPF as a foundation model and offering a concrete step toward an end-to-end pipeline from detector data to physics analysis.

</details>


### [35] [Measurement of the muon neutrino charged-current cross section with SND@LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14669)
*The SND@LHC Collaboration,:,D. Abbaneo,S. Ahmad,R. Albanese,A. Alexandrov,F. Alicante,F. Aloschi,K. Androsov,L. G. Arellano,C. Asawatangtrakuldee,M. A. Ayala Torres,N. Bangaru,C. Battilana,A. Bay,A. Montesi,D. Morozova,L. Mozzina,F. L. Navarria,W. Nuntiyakul,K. Obayashi,S. Ogawa,M. Ovchynnikov,G. Paggi,M. Pentella,A. Perrotta,N. Polukhina,F. Primavera,A. Prota,A. Quercia,S. Ramos,A. Reghunath,F. Ronchetti,N. Rossolino,T. Rovelli,O. Ruchayskiy,T. Ruf,Z. Sadykov,V. Scalera,W. Schmidt-Parzefall,O. Schneider,D. Schoerling,G. Sekhniaidze,A. Serban,N. Serra,M. Shaposhnikov,T. Shchedrina,L. Shchutska,H. Shibuya,C. Silano,G. P. Siroli,G. Sirri,T. E. Smith,G. Soares,J. Y. Sohn,O. J. Soto Sandoval,M. Spurio,A. Tarek,J. Tesarek,I. Timiryasov,V. Tioukov,B. Turk,E. Ursov,G. Vankova-Kirilova,G. Vasquez,V. Verguilov,N. Viegas Guerreiro Leonardo,C. Vilela,R. Wanke,S. Yamamoto,Z. Yang,C. Yazici,S. M. Yoo,C. S. Yoon,E. Zaffaroni,J. Zamora Saá*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文报道了利用SND@LHC实验电子探测器测量中微子（muon neutrino）在钨靶上的带电流（charged-current, CC）相互作用截面。基于LHC Run 3期间在质心能量13.6 TeV下收集的68.6 fb⁻¹质子-质子对撞数据，筛选出31个ν_μ CC候选事件，在背景期望5.0±1.1个事件下测得信号强度为1.09^{+0.72}_{-0.37}，并确定中微子与反中微子联合CC截面为(37^{+24}_{-12})×10⁻³⁵ cm²（中位能量228 GeV）。此外还基于专用测试束流校准数据进行了强子能量的量热测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大型强子对撞机（Large Hadron Collider, LHC）前沿能区，高能中微子相互作用截面的精确测量对于检验标准模型预测和解释超高能宇宙线中微子观测具有重要意义。钨靶因其高原子序数可增强中微子相互作用率，但此前缺乏基于LHC数据的直接测量结果。

Method: 利用SND@LHC实验的电子探测器系统，选择LHC Run 3在2022–2023年采集的质心能量√s=13.6 TeV的质子-质子对撞数据（积分亮度68.6 fb⁻¹）。通过带电电流（charged-current, CC）相互作用拓扑特征筛选ν_μ CC候选事件，并利用专用测试束流校准数据对候选事件中的强子能量进行量热测量。

Result: 共筛选出31个ν_μ CC候选事件，背景期望为5.0±1.1个事件，信号期望为24^{+10}_{-9}个事件。测得的信号强度为\hatμ=1.09^{+0.72}_{-0.37}，中微子与反中微子联合CC截面为σ(ν_μ+ \barν_μ)=(37^{+24}_{-12})×10⁻³⁵ cm²，中位能量为228 GeV。

Conclusion: 测量结果在误差范围内与标准模型预期一致，验证了SND@LHC实验在LHC环境下的中微子探测能力。该工作提供了首个基于LHC数据的钨靶中微子CC截面测量，并为后续利用LHC高能中微子源进行精确截面测量奠定了基础。

Abstract: We report a measurement of the muon neutrino charged-current (CC) interaction cross section on tungsten using the electronic detectors of the SND@LHC experiment at the CERN Large Hadron Collider. The analysis uses proton--proton collision data at a centre-of-mass energy of $\sqrt{s} = 13.6$ TeV, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of $68.6 ~\text{fb}^{-1}$ collected during LHC Run 3 in 2022 and 2023. A total of 31 $ν_μ$ CC candidates are selected against an expected background of $5.0 \pm 1.1$ events, consistent with a signal expectation of $24^{+10}_{-9}$ events. The signal strength is measured to be $\hatμ = 1.09^{+0.72}_{-0.37}$, and the combined muon neutrino and anti-neutrino CC cross section on tungsten is determined to be $σ(ν_μ+ \barν_μ) = (37^{+24}_{-12})\times 10^{-35}~\text{cm}^2$ at a median energy of $228$ GeV. In addition, a calorimetric measurement of the hadronic energies of the neutrino candidate events is performed, making use of calibration data from dedicated test-beam campaigns.

</details>
