### [36] [Trap-Quenched Matter-Wave Optics for Dual Species Lensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14577)
*Gabriel Müller,Timothé Estrampes,Claudia Puertas González,Jannik Ströhle,David B. Reinhardt,Dana Codruta Marinica,Ethan R. Elliott,Jason R. Williams,Nathan Lundblad,Eric Charron,Ernst M. Rasel,Matthias Meister,Wolfgang P. Schleich,Naceur Gaaloul,Nicholas P. Bigelow*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种阱淬冷准直技术（trap-quenched collimation technique），利用集団模（collective modes）的阱内激发，可在国际空间站（International Space Station）冷原子实验室（Cold Atom Laboratory）上实现超冷原子膨胀能的极低控制。实验在$^{87}$Rb单种凝聚体上观测到长达700毫秒的自由膨胀时间，二维膨胀能低至$k_B \cdot 78\pm 9\;\mathrm{pK}$；经磁场诱导动力学建模后，沿凝聚体本征轴（eigenaxes）的等效二维膨胀能约为$k_B \cdot 15^{+12}_{-5}\;\mathrm{pK}$。理论研究表明，将该方案应用于$^{41}$K-$^{87}$Rb混合物，可同时实现满足$10^{-15}$精度水平自由落体普适性检验（Universality of Free Fall, UFF）要求的膨胀能条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 空间双种原子干涉仪（dual-species atom interferometry）有望以随失重状态下延长干涉时间而二次增长的灵敏度检验自由落体普适性（UFF）。这类检验要求对两种凝聚体源（condensed sources）的膨胀能及其质心相对动力学（differential center-of-mass dynamics）实现极精确控制，现有技术难以满足这一需求。

Method: 提出一种阱淬冷准直技术（trap-quenched collimation technique），通过阱内激发集団模（collective modes）来压缩原子云的膨胀速率，并与现有原子芯片（atom-chip）装置兼容。实验在NASA国际空间站冷原子实验室上进行，以$^{87}$Rb单种玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）为对象，实施该准直方案并测量其自由膨胀行为。此外，对$^{41}$K-$^{87}$Rb双种混合物进行理论研究，预测该方案的同时准直效果。

Result: 在$^{87}$Rb单种凝聚体上实现了长达700毫秒的自由膨胀时间，二维膨胀能（two-dimensional expansion energy）在成像平面内测量为$k_B \cdot 78\pm 9\;\mathrm{pK}$。基于磁诱导动力学（magnetically-induced dynamics）详细模型的解释表明，沿凝聚体两条本征轴（eigenaxes）的等效二维膨胀能约为$k_B \cdot 15^{+12}_{-5}\;\mathrm{pK}$。对于$^{41}$K-$^{87}$Rb混合物，理论预测可实现同时准直（simultaneous collimation），膨胀能达到满足$10^{-15}$精度水平UFF检验的要求。

Conclusion: 阱淬冷准直技术可在空间微重力环境下实现超冷原子的极低膨胀能控制，实验证实该技术对单种凝聚体有效，理论分析表明其可用于双种混合物，为在$10^{-15}$精度水平上开展空间自由落体普适性检验奠定了关键实验基础。

Abstract: Dual-species atom interferometry in space promises precise tests of the Universality of Free Fall (UFF), with a sensitivity that grows quadratically with the extended interrogation time accessible in weightlessness. These tests demand exquisite control over the expansion energies of both condensed sources as well as over their differential center-of-mass dynamics. We propose a trap-quenched collimation technique featuring in-trap excitations of collective modes compatible with state-of-the-art atom-chip setups. Using NASA's Cold Atom Laboratory aboard the International Space Station, we demonstrate it on a single-species $^{87}$Rb condensate. By controlling the center-of-mass release dynamics we observe free expansion times up to 700 ms and measure a two-dimensional expansion energy of $k_B \cdot 78\pm 9 \;\mathrm{pK}$ in the imaging plane. A detailed model of the magnetically-induced dynamics indicates that this corresponds to a two-dimensional expansion energy of about $k_B \cdot 15^{+12}_{-5}\; \mathrm{pK}$ along two of the condensate's eigenaxes. Finally, we theoretically study this trap-quenched collimation scheme for a $^{41}$K-$^{87}$Rb mixture, predicting a simultaneous collimation that meets the expansion energy requirements for a state-of-the-art UFF test at the $10^{-15}$ accuracy level.

</details>

### [37] [Electrostatic Charge Model for Dual-Layer Oxide Thin-Film Transistors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13765)
*Måns J. Mattsson,John F. Wager,Matt W. Graham*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个简单的静电双方程模型，用于描述双层薄膜晶体管（TFT）的工作特性。该模型通过分配顶层与底层半导体层之间的静电荷，准确模拟了双層 a-IGZO/a-IZO TFT 的实验转移曲线和迁移率曲线。模型进一步给出了一个解析表达式，将高迁移率 a-IZO 底层中的电荷限制与 a-IGZO 顶层厚度及导带偏移（conduction-band offset）联系起来。结合电荷分配与氧空位陷阱密度（oxygen vacancy trap density）的厚度依赖性竞争效应，模型预测 a-IGZO 层的最佳厚度为 9 至 12 nm。该通用静电模型可推广至大多数双层 TFT 系统，并计算出顶层半导体层的开启电压（turn-on voltage）如何随导带偏移和层厚发生急剧变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的双层薄膜晶体管（thin-film transistor, TFT）模型缺少对静电电荷分布的简单解析描述，难以直观分析电荷限制效应与层间导带偏移（conduction-band offset）之间的关联。本文旨在建立一个简洁的静电双方程模型（two-equation model）以填补这一缺口。

Method: 基于静电学构建双方程模型，将总电荷分配至顶层（a-IGZO）与底层（a-IZO）半导体层；引入解析表达式映射电荷限制（charge confinement）与顶层厚度及导带偏移的关系；同时考虑氧空位陷阱密度（oxygen vacancy trap density）随厚度的竞争效应。

Result: 该模型生成的转移曲线（transfer curve）和迁移率曲线（mobility curve）与实验双层 a-IGZO/a-IZO TFT 数据吻合；预测 a-IGZO 层最佳厚度为 9 至 12 nm；且揭示顶层开启电压（turn-on voltage）随导带偏移和厚度发生急剧变化。

Conclusion: 所提出的静电双方程模型不仅适用于 a-IGZO/a-IZO 系统，还可推广至大多数双层 TFT 系统，为优化器件结构和理解电荷分配机制提供了通用分析工具。

Abstract: A simple electrostatic two-equation model for dual-layer thin-film transistor (TFT) operation is developed. The model distributes electrostatic charge between the top and bottom semiconductor layers, and the resulting transfer and mobility curves accurately simulate experimental dual-layer a-IGZO/a-IZO TFT operation. The model further provides an analytic expression that maps charge confinement in the high-mobility a-IZO bottom semiconductor layer with the a-IGZO top-layer thickness and the conduction-band offset. By considering both a-IGZO/a-IZO layer charge partition and competing thickness-dependent oxygen vacancy trap density effects, the model suggests an optimal a-IGZO layer thickness of 9 to 12 nm. Importantly, this general electrostatic model extends to most dual-layer TFT systems and calculates how the top semiconductor layer TFT turn-on voltage changes sharply with the conduction band offset and layer thickness.

</details>


### [38] [Combining Frozen Trajectory Excitation and TACAW for in silico Time-Resolved Vibrational Electron Energy Loss/Gain Spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13831)
*Wojciech Marciniak,Joanna Marciniak,José Ángel Castellanos-Reyes,Ján Rusz*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合冻结轨迹激发（FTE）与辅助波函数时间自相关（TACAW）的计算框架，用于模拟超快振动电子能量损失谱（EELS），能够直接与（扫描）透射电子显微镜EELS实验（(S)TEM-EELS）进行对比，并以fcc-Ni和3C-SiC为例，展示了非平衡晶格动力学弛豫过程中的声子模式耦合与谱分布变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超快（皮秒时间尺度）振动电子能量损失谱（EELS）预计很快将能在实验上实现，但目前缺乏从计算物理视角提供深刻洞察的理论框架。作者希望建立一种能够直接与实验可比的方法，用于研究非平衡晶格动力学的时间依赖谱响应。

Method: 该框架结合了冻结轨迹激发（FTE）与辅助波函数时间自相关（TACAW）两种技术：先用FTE在平衡分子动力学轨迹中引入特定的声子激发，然后对后续弛豫过程中的原子位置进行短时TACAW分析，在不同泵浦-探测延迟时间下获取动量分辨和能量分辨的电子散射信号。

Result: 在fcc-Ni和3C-SiC两种材料上的演示表明，该方法能够获得弛豫过程中带有声子印记的动量-能量分辨电子散射信号，超越了仅依赖时间分辨漫散射强度的传统分析，并揭示了声子模式耦合及弛豫过程中的谱分布变化。

Conclusion: 所提出的计算框架能够有效模拟超快振动EELS实验中的非平衡晶格动力学响应，且结果可直接与(S)TEM-EELS实验对比，为理解声子弛豫过程中的模式耦合与能量再分配提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: Seeing that ultrafast (picosecond timescale) vibrational electron energy loss spectroscopy (EELS) should soon be experimentally realizable, we present in silico approach capable of providing insight from the computational physics perspective. We present a framework that combines frozen trajectory excitation (FTE) with time auto-correlation of auxiliary wavefunctions (TACAW) to study the time-dependent spectral response of non-equilibrium lattice dynamics in a way comparable directly to experiment - (scanning) transmission electron microscope EELS, (S)TEM-EELS. In this approach, a selected phonon excitation is first introduced into an equilibrium molecular dynamics trajectory using FTE, after which the atomic positions during subsequent relaxations are treated with short-time TACAW analysis performed at different pump-probe delays. This yields momentum- and energy-resolved electron-scattering signals bearing a phonon imprint during the relaxation process, going beyond time-dependent diffuse-scattering intensities alone. We demonstrate the approach for fcc-Ni and 3C-SiC and discuss the observed phonon mode coupling and spectral redistribution during phonon relaxation.

</details>


### [39] [Machine-learned dynamics of surface polarons at reduced oxide surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13833)
*Luca Leoni,Cesare Franchini*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本论文利用机器学习辅助的极化子动力学方法，在纳秒尺度上模拟了缺氧金红石TiO₂(110)表面的小极化子（small polaron）动力学，发现表面极化子迁移率比体相材料低数个数量级，并揭示了其受限的跳跃路径和氧空位对自由能景观的重塑机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可还原氧化物（reducible oxides）中过量电子形成的小极化子对电荷传输和表面化学至关重要，但有限温度下的表面极化子动力学从第一性原理（first principles）角度难以获取。传统从头算分子动力学（ab initio molecular dynamics）仅能覆盖皮秒时间尺度，无法对极化子跳跃动力学进行统计上有意义的采样。

Method: 将机器学习辅助极化子动力学（machine-learning-assisted polaron dynamics）方法扩展到氧化还原活性氧化物表面，以缺氧金红石TiO₂(110)为范例，在多个温度下获取数纳秒尺度的动力学轨迹。

Result: 表面小极化子迁移率相比体相材料被抑制了数个数量级，为多孔金红石TiO₂中电子迁移率低于单晶样品的现象提供了微观解释。抑制源于有利跳跃路径的缺失：表面极化子运动主要限制在第二顶层内的平面行间轨迹，层间跳跃事件极为罕见。氧空位作为过量电子的吸引中心，重塑极化子自由能景观（free-energy landscape），使极化子分布偏向附近的Ti位点，并偶尔促进电荷转移至最外层表面。

Conclusion: 这些结果建立了一种可迁移的机器学习策略，用于研究可还原氧化物中的极化子动力学。

Abstract: Reducible oxides exhibit a rich interplay of electronic, structural, and chemical properties that underpins applications in catalysis, photovoltaics, batteries, and energy storage. This interplay is strongly shaped by excess electrons, often introduced by oxygen vacancies, that localize as small polarons and influence charge transport and surface chemistry. At surfaces, these polarons play a central role in charge localization, mobility, and reactivity, yet their finite-temperature dynamics remain difficult to access from first principles. Ab initio molecular dynamics is typically limited to picosecond time scales, precluding statistically meaningful sampling of polaron hopping dynamics. To overcome this limitation, we extend machine-learning-assisted polaron dynamics [V. Birschitzky et al., Phys. Rev. Lett. 134, 216301 (2025)] to redox-active oxide surfaces, using oxygen-deficient rutile TiO2(110) as a paradigmatic case. By accessing several nanoseconds of dynamics over a range of temperatures, we show that small-polaron mobility at the reduced rutile TiO2(110) surface is suppressed by several orders of magnitude relative to the corresponding bulk material, providing a microscopic interpretation of the lower electron mobilities observed in porous rutile TiO2 compared with single-crystal samples. This suppressed mobility arises from the loss of favorable hopping pathways: surface polaron motion is largely confined to planar inter-row trajectories within the second topmost layers, with only rare interlayer hopping events. Oxygen vacancies further reshape the polaron free-energy landscape by acting as attractive centers for excess electrons, biasing the polaron distribution toward nearby Ti sites and promoting occasional charge transfer to the outermost surface layer. These results establish a transferable machine-learning strategy for investigating polaron dynamics in reducible oxides.

</details>


### [40] [Closed-loop discovery of out-of-distribution processing protocols by evolutionary search and uncertainty-aware learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13859)
*Yu Liu,Stanislav Udovenko,Ching-Che Lin,Jaegyu Kim,Lane W. Martin,Susan Trolier-McKinstry,Sergei V. Kalinin*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种结合进化搜索（evolutionary search）与不确定性感知深度核学习（uncertainty-aware deep kernel learning）的闭环工作流，用于在波形（waveform）或样本历史等高维控制空间中自动发现新材料处理协议。在铁电薄膜实验中，该方法通过优化扫描探针针尖偏压波形，成功识别出能通过“去老化”（de-aging）增强材料非线性响应的波形族，并揭示了性能差异的微观机制——最优波形选择性激活弱钉扎畴壁段，而非最优波形则引发长程不可逆翻转。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多材料和化学系统表现出依赖于历史（history-dependent）的响应，其功能结果不仅由最终状态变量决定，还受操作过程中施加的场、温度或化学势的时变序列（time-dependent sequence）控制。发现新的处理协议因此成为一个高维搜索问题，控制变量是整个波形或样本历史，而传统策略要么局限于保守的插值族，要么因测量强度过高而不可行。

Method: 引入一种闭环工作流（closed-loop workflow），将紧凑波形表示上的进化搜索（evolutionary search）与不确定性感知深度核学习（uncertainty-aware deep kernel learning）相结合，以生成、排序并实验验证候选协议。在铁电薄膜中的应用以扫描探针针尖偏压波形为协议，非线性机电响应为奖励（reward）。

Result: 该工作流发现了能通过去老化（de-aging）薄膜来增强非线性的波形族。空间分辨的前后测量表明，性能最佳的波形选择性地激活了预先存在的弱钉扎畴壁段（weakly pinned domain-wall segments），而最差的波形驱动了长程不可逆翻转（long-range irreversible switching）。

Conclusion: 该框架将协议调优重新定义为分布外发现（out-of-distribution discovery），可推广至合成与退火轨迹、电池形成协议（battery formation protocols）及其他高维控制问题。

Abstract: Many materials and chemical systems exhibit history-dependent responses, where functional outcomes are governed not only by final-state variables but by the time-dependent sequence of fields, temperatures, or chemical potentials applied during operation. Discovering new processing protocols is therefore a high-dimensional search problem in which the control variable is an entire waveform or sample history, and conventional strategies either remain confined to conservative interpolative families or become prohibitively measurement intensive. Here, a closed-loop workflow is introduced that couples evolutionary search over a compact waveform representation with uncertainty-aware deep kernel learning to generate, rank, and experimentally validate candidate protocols. Applied to ferroelectric thin films, with the scanning-probe tip-bias waveform as the protocol and the nonlinear electromechanical response as the reward, the workflow discovers waveform families that enhance nonlinearity by de-aging the film. Spatially resolved before/after measurements show that the best-performing waveforms selectively activate pre-existing, weakly pinned domain-wall segments, whereas the worst drive long-range irreversible switching. This framework reframes protocol tuning as out-of-distribution discovery, generalizable to synthesis and annealing trajectories, battery formation protocols, and other high-dimensional control problems.

</details>


### [41] [DFTB coupled with NEGF study of the structural, electronic and transport properties of goldene 2D material](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13869)
*Taoufik Sakhraoui,František Karlický*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究利用密度泛函紧束缚（density functional tight-binding, DFTB）方法和非平衡格林函数（non-equilibrium Green's functions, NEGF）技术，报道了金烯（goldene）二维材料的结构、电子和输运性质。研究发现金烯具有动态和热稳定性、良好弹性以及金属性电流-电压特性。此外，硅（Si）掺杂可在金烯单层中诱导局部磁态，磁矩为0.63 μB。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索金烯（goldene）二维材料的结构、电子、输运性质，并研究硅（Si）掺杂对其电子结构和磁性的影响。

Method: 采用密度泛函紧束缚（density functional tight-binding, DFTB）方法进行结构、电子和弹性性质计算；电子输运计算结合了非平衡格林函数（non-equilibrium Green's functions, NEGF）技术。

Result: Au二维材料具有动态和热稳定性以及良好弹性；金烯在低电势下呈现电流-电压线性关系，表明其金属性；电流-电势曲线与透射函数及费米能级附近的电子态密度（density of states）相关联；Si掺杂可在金烯单层中诱导局部磁态，磁矩为0.63 μB。

Conclusion: 金烯是一种稳定、具良好弹性且呈金属性的二维材料；通过Si掺杂可引入局部磁性，为金烯在自旋电子学等领域的应用提供了可能。

Abstract: We report the structural, electronic, and transport properties of the goldene 2D material using the density functional tight-binding (DFTB) method. Electronic transport calculations were conducted in conjunction with the non-equilibrium Green's functions (NEGF) technique. Our study reveals that the Au 2D material is dynamically and thermally stable, and it possesses good elastic properties. On the other hand, goldene has a linear relationship between current and voltage at low potentials, indicating its metallic character. The calculated current-potential curve correlates well with transmission functions and the electronic density of states around the Fermi level. We also investigated the electronic structure and magnetic properties of silicon (Si)-doped Au 2D material. Our results show that the Si atom can induce a local magnetic state in the goldene monolayer. The resulting magnetic moment is 0.63 $μ_B$.

### [42] [Dynamical multiferroicity in framework materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13874)
*Marek Matas,Carl P. Romao*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理（ab initio）计算，研究了无机和有机框架材料中的动态多铁性（dynamical multiferroicity），发现金属-有机框架材料 Zn(NH₄)(formate)₃ 中由圆极化声子（circularly polarized phonons）产生的磁矩几乎是 SrTiO₃ 的两倍，归因于 NH₄⁺ 氢离子的高旋磁比（gyromagnetic ratio）圆运动，并指出框架材料的复杂结构与柔性有助于角动量局域化并提升光致磁化上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动态多铁性已确立为利用光学控制磁性的机制，但尚未系统地寻找能由光产生更大磁场的材料。本文旨在通过第一性原理计算，识别能够产生大磁场的新型无机和有机框架材料。

Method: 采用第一性原理（ab initio）计算方法，对无机和有机框架材料中的动态多铁性进行模拟，计算圆极化声子模式产生的磁矩，并评估其光致磁化强度。

Result: 发现金属-有机框架（metal-organic framework）材料 Zn(NH₄)(formate)₃ 的某些声子模式具有几乎两倍于 SrTiO₃ 的磁矩；这些模式涉及 NH₄⁺ 氢离子的高旋磁比圆运动。

Conclusion: 框架材料的复杂结构与柔性能够实现角动量局域化（angular momentum localization），并根据林德曼熔化判据（Lindemann melting criterion）提高光致磁化的上限，为光学控制磁性材料的设计提供了新方向。

Abstract: Dynamical multiferroicity, which describes the magnetic fields generated by circularly polarized phonons in materials, is an established mechanism for optical control of magnetism. Here we perform ab initio calculations of dynamical multiferroicity in inorganic and organic framework materials, with the goal of identifying materials which enable the generation of large magnetic fields by light. We find the metal--organic framework material Zn(NH$_4$)(formate)$_3$ to have modes with magnetic moments almost twice that of SrTiO$_3$; these modes involve circular motions of NH$_4^+$ hydrogen ions with high gyromagnetic ratios. The complex structure and flexibility of framework materials can allow such angular momentum localization, and also increase the maximum light-induced magnetization permitted by the Lindemann melting criterion.

</details>


### [43] [Towards Atom-by-Atom Fabrication: Mechanosynthetic donation and abstraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13876)
*Brandon Blue,Mathieu Morin,Alex Inayeh,Rosemary Cranston,Cameron J. Mackie,Marc Savoie,Adam Bottomley,Christian J. Maley,Michael Marshall,Terry McCallum,Ralph Merkle,Matthew Moses,Jonathan Myall,Ryan Plumadore,Adam Powell,Henry Rodriguez,Sam Rohe,Luis Sandoval,Khalil Sayed-Akhmad,Benjamin Scheffel,Kashif Tanveer,Bheeshmon Thanabalasingam,Denis A. Method: 采用倒置模式扫描隧道显微镜（inverted-mode scanning tunneling microscopy, IM-STM）作为实验平台，结合功能化分子工具，在原子级洁净且晶态的Si(100)表面上进行位置可控的原子加成与移除操作。

Result: 成功在Si(100)表面实现了碳原子的机械合成加成和硅原子的机械合成移除，且这些操作具有位置可控性。这是首次在三维空间中对特定原子和基团实现位置调控的自由基化学操作的实验演示。

Conclusion: 通过对比原子捐赠型与原子移除型分子工具的行为差异，揭示了对选择性、可靠性机械合成功能导向的分子工具设计的一般性原则。

Abstract: Enabled by inverted-mode scanning tunneling microscopy (IM-STM) and the use of functionalized molecular tools, we demonstrate positionally-controlled mechanosynthetic addition (donation) of carbon and subtraction (abstraction) of silicon atoms on a model build site: atomically clean and crystalline Si(100). The resulting structures represent the first demonstrations of an emerging ability to manipulate radical chemistry with positional control of specific atoms and moieties in 3D. Furthermore, by comparing the behavior of molecular tools designed for atomic donation versus abstraction, we highlight general principles governing molecular tool design for selective and reliable mechanosynthetic functionality.

Abstract: Autonomous synthesis platforms integrating machine learning with in situ diagnostics have the potential to revolutionize thin-film growth by enabling real-time process optimization and reducing the need for manual tuning. However, their application to molecular beam epitaxy (MBE) remains underdeveloped. Here, we present a machine learning-guided framework for MBE growth of GaSe films, leveraging reflection high-energy electron diffraction (RHEED) as an in situ diagnostic alongside ex situ characterization via X-ray diffraction and atomic force microscopy. Unsupervised learning on RHEED patterns reveals a well-defined boundary between high- and low-quality samples, capturing physically meaningful features. Mutual information analysis shows a strong correlation between RHEED embeddings and rocking curve full-width at half-maximum (fwhm), while the correlation with AFM root-mean-square (RMS) roughness is weak. Among key growth conditions, growth rate most strongly influences fwhm, whereas the Se/Ga flux ratio primarily affects RMS roughness and the RHEED embeddings. Supervised learning models trained to predict fwhm and RMS roughness demonstrate moderate accuracy, with significant improvement achieved by incorporating RHEED embeddings. Furthermore, anomaly detection via residual analysis in supervised learning aligns well with unsupervised classification from RHEED, reinforcing the reliability of the predictive models. This study establishes a data-driven framework for machine learning-assisted MBE, paving the way for real-time process control and accelerated optimization of thin-film synthesis.

This report presents a unique approach for the growths of uniform and single-crystalline Mn2In2Se5 vdW layers using MBE, and potentially opens a pathway for synthesis of ternary vdW chalcogenides by intercalation of new atomic species in binary vdW chalcogenides.

Abstract: Metastable states and their minimum energy pathways (MEPs) are central to understanding transformations and phase stability in complex materials, yet mapping transition pathways between competing states remains computationally demanding and experimentally challenging. Here, we introduce a hybrid solid-state nudged elastic band (SSNEB) framework that integrates two pretrained machine learning models, EquiformerV2 (eqV2) and the equivariant Smooth Energy Network (eSEN), with DFT for energy, force, and stress evaluations. Applied to three solid-state systems, CsPbI$_3$, GaN, and TiO$_2$, our framework achieves up to a 7-fold speedup while converging to the same pathways predicted by first-principles calculations. Moreover, the hybrid SSNEB framework enables systematic benchmarking of existing ML models, providing both efficiency and reliability for predicting MEPs across various materials.

### [47] [Oxygen deficiency and valency reconstruction in multiferroic V-doped HfO$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13950)
*Vincenzo Fiorentini*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该论文通过第一性原理计算研究了氧空位与钒多价态在V掺杂HfO₂多铁材料中的相互作用机制。计算表明氧空位向V⁴⁺提供电子将其还原为V³⁺，并导致形成能降低、局域磁化和屏蔽效应发生变化。V³⁺/V⁴⁺比例仅在还原条件下与实验XPS数据吻合，表明原子层沉积（ALD）生长条件下可能存在额外电子库。类似机制也适用于Cr掺杂HfO₂中观察到的多铁性。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），分析V掺杂HfO₂中氧空位（oxygen vacancy）与钒离子价态变化的电子结构关系，并结合计算得出的V芯能级偏移（core-level shifts）与实验X射线光电子能谱（XPS）进行对比验证。

Result: 低能V主隙态（low-lying V majority gap states）从氧空位施主接受电子，降低了氧空位的形成能，并将名义上的V⁴⁺中心转化为V³⁺。计算得到的V³⁺/V⁴⁺种群比例仅在还原条件下与实验XPS结果一致，表明ALD生长条件下可能存在其他电子库。

Conclusion: 氧空位与钒多价态的耦合是理解V掺杂HfO₂中多铁性的关键。类似机制也适用于Cr掺杂HfO₂中观察到的多铁性，氧缺乏是生长技术固有的特征。

Abstract: The interplay of oxygen deficiency and vanadium multiple valency in the candidate multiferroic V-doped $Pca2_1$ hafnia HfO$_2$ is studied by first-principles calculations. Low-lying V majority gap states accept electrons from oxygen-vacancy donors, reducing their formation energy, and converting nominal V$^{4+}$ centers into V$^{3+}$. The resulting local magnetization and screening changes are reflected in the calculated V core-level shifts, which are consistent with the experimentally observed XPS signatures. The calculated V$^{3+}$/V$^{4+}$ population ratio determined by oxygen vacancies only matches experiment in reducing conditions, suggesting that additional electron reservoirs may contribute under ALD growth conditions. A similar scenario also seems to apply to the recently observed multiferroicity in Cr-doped hafnia, where oxygen deficiency is intrinsic to the growth technique.

### [48] [XRDiff: Crystal Structure Prediction from Powder X-Ray Diffraction Data Using Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14003)
*Nofit Segal,Mingda Li,Benjamin Kurt Miller,Rafael Gómez-Bombarelli*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出 XRDiff，一种基于扩散模型（diffusion model）的晶体结构解析方法，能够从粉末 X 射线衍射（PXRD）图谱中恢复晶体结构，并通过基于峰描述符（peak descriptors）的编码显著提升对实验数据的泛化能力，实现了从模拟到实验的零样本（zero-shot）结构求解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从粉末 X 射线衍射（PXRD）图谱确定晶体结构是材料科学中的核心挑战。由于衍射数据中相位信息（phase information）的丢失，恢复原子结构需要求解一个欠定（underdetermined）逆问题。现有方法难以在高性能要求下区分同组成的不同多晶型物（polymorphs），且模拟到实验的差距（simulation-to-experiment gap）尚未得到有效解决。

Method: 提出 XRDiff，一种扩散模型，通过模拟结构-谱图配对数据学习从 PXRD 图谱到晶体结构的映射。模型支持两种输入设置：给定化学计量比（stoichiometry），或在更具挑战性的设置中仅给定元素组成（elemental constituents）与单胞总原子数。为提升对实验数据的泛化能力，比较了全谱（full-spectrum）编码与基于峰描述符（peak descriptors）的编码；后者通过对实验噪声分布进行增强训练来学习对噪声和伪影鲁棒的表示。

Result: 在模拟基准上，XRDiff 实现了较高的结构恢复率（structure recovery rates），表明模型学到了足够精确的谱图到结构的映射以区分不同多晶型物。在泛化到实验数据时，基于峰描述符的编码显著优于全谱编码，甚至超过了在全谱上加入针对实验噪声分布增强训练的模型。

Conclusion: 对真实 PXRD 中噪声和伪影鲁棒的表示（如峰描述符编码）提供了一条实用且可扩展的路径，用于弥合模拟与实验之间的差距，使得在给定完整或部分化学成分输入的情况下，能够从实验 PXRD 中实现零样本晶体结构求解（zero-shot crystal structure solution）。

Abstract: Determining the crystal structure of a material from its powder X-ray diffraction (PXRD) pattern is a central challenge in materials science. PXRD is an accessible and widely used characterization technique, yet recovering the atomic structure from diffraction data requires solving an underdetermined inverse problem due to the loss of phase information. Generative modeling can provide a prior over atomic structure and learn the mapping from PXRD patterns to crystal structures via simulated structure-spectrum pairs. We present XRDiff, a diffusion model that recovers crystal structures from PXRD given either the stoichiometry or, in a more challenging setting, the elemental constituents and total number of atoms in the unit cell. We evaluate on datasets where each stoichiometry has multiple polymorphs and all polymorphs of a given composition are held out together, ensuring that high performance reflects genuine use of the diffraction signal. XRDiff achieves strong structure recovery rates on simulated benchmarks, indicating that the model learns a spectrum-to-structure mapping precise enough to differentiate between polymorphs. To address generalization to experimental data, we compare a full-spectrum encoding against an encoding based on peak descriptors. The peak-based encoding generalizes substantially better, outperforming even a model trained on full spectra with augmentations fitted to the experimental noise distribution. These results demonstrate that representations robust to the noise and artifacts present in real-world PXRD offer a practical and scalable path toward closing the simulation-to-experiment gap, enabling zero-shot crystal structure solution from experimental PXRD with full or partial chemical composition input.

</details>

Method: 通过对称性分析（symmetry analysis）系统分类开关算符（switching operators），建立群论框架，实现电极化（electric polarization）与非相对论性自旋分裂（nonrelativistic spin splitting）的同时翻转。

Here, we develop a group-theoretical framework for achieving ferroelectric control of spin splitting in collinear antiferromagnets, including altermagnets and compensated ferrimagnets. ### [50] [Probing Structure and Ionic Transport in Molten Lithium Carbonate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14118)
*Debsundar Dey,Abhirup Patra,Anand Narayanan Krishnamoorthy,Gopalakrishnan Sai Gautam*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文利用等变图神经网络机器学习势（MACE和NequIP）对熔融Li₂CO₃进行大规模分子动力学模拟，发现MACE在预测精度和迁移性上优于NequIP，并揭示熔融LC中Li⁺输运主要由协同运动主导，且在1000 K时呈现各向异性、高度协同的扩散行为，在1400 K时转变为各向同性、协同性较低的扩散。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 熔融Li₂CO₃ (LC) 是高温熔融碳酸盐燃料电池、电化学碳捕集和锂基电池等清洁能源技术中的关键材料，但熔融态下结构-输运性质的多体相互作用难以被精确描述——从头算方法（ab initio methods）计算成本过高，而经典力场（force fields）精度有限。

Method: 采用两种等变图神经网络机器学习势（equivariant graph-based machine learned interatomic potentials）架构——多原子团簇展开（MACE）和神经等变原子间势（NequIP），基于熔融淬火（melt-quench）从头算分子动力学数据训练，并通过大尺度分子动力学仿真对熔融LC的结构与输运性质进行研究。

Result: 基准测试表明MACE在预测能量和力的精度及迁移性（transferability）上优于NequIP。MACE模型成功复现实验测量的静态结构因子（static structure factor）和剪切粘度（shear viscosity），并发现Haven比值（Haven's ratio）显著低于1（0.20-0.40），表明Li⁺输运由协同运动（concerted motion）主导。此外，观察到从1000 K时由氧中心Voronoi笼（oxygen-centered Voronoi cages）支撑的各向异性、高度协同的Li输运，向1400 K时各向同性、协同性较低的扩散的温度驱动转变。

Conclusion: 本文不仅提供了熔融LC的结构与输运性质的基础见解，还建立了一个稳健且可扩展的框架，有助于加速熔盐电解质和离子液体的设计。

Abstract: Li$_2$CO$_3$ (LC) is a cornerstone material for clean energy technologies, including high-temperature molten carbonate fuel cells, electrochemical carbon capture, and lithium-based batteries. However, capturing the complex, many-body interactions governing the structure and transport in LC in its molten state has remained a challenge, constrained by the computational cost of \textit{ab initio} methods and the accuracy limitations of classical force fields. To address this gap, we deploy equivariant graph-based machine learned interatomic potentials, specifically, the multi atomic cluster expansion (MACE) and neural equivariant interatomic potential (NequIP) architectures that are trained on melt-quench \textit{ab initio} molecular dynamics data. Our benchmarking demonstrates that MACE provides superior transferability and precision in predicting energies and forces compared to NequIP. Subsequently, we use the optimized MACE model to perform large-scale molecular dynamics simulations to probe the properties of molten LC. Besides describing the structural features, such as the dominant presence of C-O pair correlations under molten conditions, our MACE model reproduces experimentally-measured static structure factors and shear viscosity values. Further, our simulations indicate that Li transport in LC is fundamentally dominated by concerted motion, as evidenced by Haven's ratios being significantly below unity (0.20-0.40). Notably, we identify a temperature-driven transition from anisotropic (and highly concerted) Li transport, supported by persistent oxygen-centered Voronoi cages at 1000~K, to isotropic (and less concerted) diffusion at 1400~K. Thus, we provide fundamental insights into the structural and transport properties of molten LC and also demonstrate a robust and scalable framework for the accelerated design of molten salt electrolytes and ionic liquids.

</details>

With the collective effect of the surface equilibration mechanism and template growth on an aligned substrate, macroscopic biaxial alignment is achieved in depositions as much as 180 K below the clearing point $T_{LC-iso}$ (and 50 K below the glass transition temperature $T_g$ ) with single-component disk-like (phenanthroperylene ester) and rod-like (itraconazole) mesogens. ### [53] [$p$-wave magnet and hedgehog-type Berry curvature in helimagnetic MnAu$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14246)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 共线补偿磁体中的交变磁性（altermagnetism）具有偶宇称自旋织构，而非共线补偿磁体可呈现奇宇称自旋织构，但迄今尚未发现可在室温下工作的金属性非共线交变磁体候选材料。因此，寻找兼具室温稳定性和金属性的非共线 p 波磁体成为关键问题。

Method: 采用基于平移算符与自旋旋转相结合的能带展开（band-unfolding）方案，对 MnAu₂ 进行第一性原理（first-principles）计算，分析其电子结构、自旋织构与贝里曲率。

Result: 计算揭示 MnAu₂ 在 $\tilde{M}$ 点附近存在由单个电子口袋构成的非常规费米面，具有 p 波自旋织构（p-wave spin texture）；螺旋自旋序诱导出大自旋劈裂；同时，自旋扭转引发拓扑非平凡的 hedgehog 贝里曲率，与非线性霍尔效应及自旋霍尔效应相关联。

Conclusion: 由于实验测得的居里温度 T_C = 335–370 K，MnAu₂ 可作为理想的室温金属 p 波磁体，为多功能自旋电子学应用提供重要候选材料。

Abstract: Recently discovered altermagnetism in collinear compensated magnets shows even-parity spin texture in momentum space. Beyond the collinear spin ordering, unique odd-parity spin textures emerge in noncollinear compensated magnets. The noncollinear candidates, however, remain unexplored toward a room-temperature metallic altermagnet. Here, we demonstrate that MnAu2 exhibits metallic p-wave magnetism and large spin splitting induced by helical spin ordering. By adapting the band-unfolding scheme based on the translation operators combined with spin rotations, first-principles calculations reveal an unconventional Fermi surface around the $\tilde{M}$-point composed of a single electron pocket with $p$-wave spin texture. Moreover, the spin twist in the helimagnet triggers topologically non-trivial hedgehog Berry curvature, which links to the nonlinear Hall effect and spin Hall effect. Considering the experimental T$_C$ = 335 to 370 K, MnAu$_2$ could establish itself as an ideal candidate for a room-temperature metallic $p$-wave magnet, promising for versatile spintronic applications.

### [54] [Pronounced in-plane anomalous Hall effect with vanishing out-of-plane response in Cr1.2Te2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14272)

Conclusion: 该非常规反常霍尔区间无法仅由内禀贝里曲率机制解释，外禀散射过程（如杂质散射、边跳等）在产生八极霍尔响应中起关键作用，为理解磁序与拓扑输运的耦合提供了新视角。

Abstract: We report an unconventional anomalous Hall regime in the van der Waals ferromagnet Cr1.2Te2, in which the anomalous Hall effect (AHE) is present for in-plane magnetization but absent for out-of-plane magnetization. In this purely in-plane regime, the anomalous Hall signal exhibits a threefold angular dependence during both in-plane and out-of-plane rotations of the magnetization, which cannot be accounted for by the conventional dipolar contribution but instead requires an octupolar contribution. Although the octupolar term qualitatively captures the observed behavior, the experimentally extracted octupole differs quantitatively from first-principles calculations based solely on the intrinsic Berry-curvature mechanism, indicating an essential role for extrinsic scattering processes.

### [55] [Multistate Manipulation of Charge-Spin Conversion in Two-Dimensional Ferroelectric Bilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14378)
*Weiyi Pan,Xinyuan Jiang,Jaroslav Fabian*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出在二维铁电双层（two-dimensional ferroelectric bilayers）中通过层间平行与反平行极化构型共存，实现对Edelstein效应（EE）和自旋霍尔效应（SHE）的非易失多态操控，并在金属铁电双层PtBi2中通过第一性原理计算验证了该机制，为电可编程电荷-自旋转换提供了全平台方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过对称性分析（symmetry analysis）建立层间平行与反平行极化构型对EE和SHE的调控规则；采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）在金属铁电双层PtBi2中验证该机制，计算了EE系数和本征SHE系数，并分析了自旋贝里曲率（spin Berry curvature）的贡献。

Result: 在层间平行态中，总极化反转可切换EE符号；转为层间反平行构型后EE被抑制为零，实现三种不同状态间的电可切换电流诱导自旋积累，适用于三值逻辑运算（ternary logic operations）。SHE的大小可通过层间平行与反平行构型切换进行调节。PtBi2双层中两种极化构型均能量稳定；EE系数来源于费米面附近电子和空穴口袋（electron- and hole-pocket）的竞争贡献；本征SHE系数源于极化构型变化和费米能级调控可重塑的自旋贝里曲率。

Conclusion: 铁电双层可作为电可编程电荷-自旋转换的一体化平台（all-in-one platform），为高密度自旋电子存储器和多态逻辑器件提供了新的物理机制与材料方案。

Abstract: Achieving nonvolatile and multistate manipulation of charge-spin conversion, including the Edelstein effect (EE) and spin Hall effect (SHE), is crucial for high-density spintronic memory. Here, we propose a mechanism to simultaneously control both EE and SHE in two-dimensional ferroelectric bilayers, where interlayer-parallel and interlayer-antiparallel polarization configurations can coexist. Symmetry analysis shows that in the interlayer-parallel states, reversal of the total polarization switches the sign of the EE, whereas changing to an interlayer-antiparallel configuration suppresses the EE to zero, enabling electrically switchable current-induced spin accumulation among three distinct states, which could be used for ternary logic operations. Meanwhile, the magnitude of the SHE can be tuned by switching between two different classes of polarization configurations, namely interlayer-parallel and interlayer-antiparallel configurations. Using first-principles calculations, we demonstrate this mechanism in bilayer metallic ferroelectric PtBi2, where both interlayer-parallel and interlayer-antiparallel polarization configurations are energetically stable. The EE coefficient in interlayer-parallel states, which can be reversed by polarization switching, arises from competing electron- and hole-pocket contributions near the Fermi surface. The intrinsic SHE coefficients originate from spin Berry curvature that can be reshaped by polarization configuration variation and Fermi-level tuning. Our results establish ferroelectric bilayers as an all-in-one platform for electrically programmable charge-spin conversion.

Collectively, these insights highlight the need for reproducible workflows, shared data standards, realistic benchmarks, and a research culture that prepares scientists to work across paradigms. ### [57] [Modifying Electrochemical Doping in Light-Emitting Electrochemical Cells with Gold Nanoparticles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14402)
*Ajay K. Poonia,Anton Kirch,Joan Ràfols-Ribé,Lucrezia Catanzaro,Anish Rao,Karol Kołątaj,Vittorio Scardaci,Giuseppe Compagnini,Guillermo P. Acuna,Ludvig Edman,Nicolò Maccaferri*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在发光电化学池（LEC）的阳极界面分别引入无包覆的裸金纳米颗粒（neat non-capped Au-NPs）和柠檬酸钠包覆的金纳米颗粒（Au-NPs capped with sodium citrate），通过对比两种处理对p-n结掺杂结构及发射区位置的影响，研究界面纳米颗粒对电化学掺杂轮廓（doping profile）的调控作用。

Abstract: Electrochemical doping offers dynamic control of the electronic properties of organic semiconductors, and it is the enabling feature of a range of technologies, including electrochemical transistors, energy-storage devices, light-emitting electrochemical cells (LECs), and bioelectronics. Electrochemical doping is commonly controlled by the selection of the constituents in the active material of the device or the applied voltage bias, but herein we report that the incorporation of Au nanoparticles (Au-NPs) at an electrode interface can constitute an alternative control parameter. The LEC features balanced p- and n-type electrochemical doping that forms a p-n junction doping structure in its active material, and we find that it is possible to reshape this doping profile by incorporating Au-NPs at an electrode interface. Specifically, we establish that the inclusion of neat non-capped Au-NPs at the anodic interface shifts the p-n junction (i.e., the emission zone) away from the anode. In contrast, the inclusion of Au-NPs capped with sodium citrate is found to reverse this behavior, so that the emission zone is instead moved towards the anode. We utilize this control parameter to shift the emission zone towards a position of constructive (destructive) interference, as manifested in a strong increase (decrease) of the LEC emission efficiency. Our findings establish an interfacial strategy for modulating the spatial profile of electrochemical doping and tuning device performance without altering the chemistry of the active material, relying instead on the surface modification of one electrode. This approach is important because it provides a versatile and minimally invasive route to optimize electrochemical devices while preserving the intrinsic properties and formulation of the active material.

### [58] [First-principles calculations of internal conversion processes in spin defects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14545)
*Stefano Paolo Villani,Yu Jin,Giulia Galli*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个基于多体波函数（many-body wavefunctions）和全声子模式（all-phonon-mode）贡献的预测性理论框架，用于精确计算光学活性自旋缺陷（optically active spin defects）的内转换（IC）速率，解决了传统近似低估IC速率数个数量级的问题，并在NV⁻中心和SiC双空位体系中得到了实验验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光学活性自旋缺陷是量子技术的基础，但现有常用近似方法对内转换（internal conversion, IC）速率的估算低估了数个数量级，亟需一个更精确的预测性理论框架来弥合理论与实验之间的差距。

Method: 该框架结合了含时密度泛函理论（TDDFT）中的多体波函数（many-body wavefunctions）以纳入多组态效应（multi-configurational effects），并通过解析非绝热耦合（analytical non-adiabatic couplings）引入所有声子模式（all-phonon-mode）的贡献。

Result: 该方法成功解决了与实验之间的差异：在金刚石NV⁻中心（NV⁻ center in diamond）实现了定量吻合，并在SiC的双空位三重态寿命（divacancy triplet lifetime in SiC）中识别出一个此前被忽视的非辐射通道（non-radiative channel）。

Conclusion: 所提出的框架显著提升了IC速率的计算精度，为理解和预测自旋缺陷的非辐射动力学提供了可靠的理论工具，有助于推动量子技术的发展。

Abstract: Optically active spin defects are foundational for quantum technologies, yet common approximations underestimate their internal conversion (IC) rates by orders of magnitude. We propose a broad, predictive framework to compute IC rates that incorporates multi-configurational effects via many-body wavefunctions in TDDFT, and includes all-phonon-mode contributions via analytical non-adiabatic couplings. Our approach resolves discrepancies with experiment, achieving quantitative agreement for the NV$^-$ center in diamond, and identifying a previously overlooked non-radiative channel in the divacancy triplet lifetime in SiC.

</details>


### [59] [Lattice dynamics and the spectroscopic signatures of H-bond disorder in $δ$-AlOOH](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14590)
*Chenxing Luo,Sangjoon Lee,Hongjin Wang,Zhen Zhang,Renata Wentzcovitch*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过结合简谐声子计算、基于SCAN的深度势能分子动力学（deep-potential molecular dynamics）和声子准粒子分析（phonon quasiparticle analysis），在300K下研究了δ-AlOOH中与氢键对称化（H-bond symmetrization）相关的拉曼和红外异常。研究发现，有限温度动力学效应和谱相干性逐渐丧失是这些光谱特征的根本原因，从而解释了为何异常在比静态简谐理论预测低得多的压力下出现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将简谐声子计算（harmonic phonon calculations）与基于强约束且恰当归一化泛函（strongly constrained and appropriately normed, SCAN）的深度势能分子动力学（deep-potential molecular dynamics）以及声子准粒子分析（phonon quasiparticle analysis）相结合，在300 K下提取随温度和压力变化的频率和寿命，并纳入准粒子重整化（quasiparticle renormalization）和方向性纵向-横向光学分裂（longitudinal-optical-transverse-optical, LO-TO splitting）效应。

Result: 该框架成功捕捉到了无序区域（disordering regime）中分支重组（branch reorganization）和线宽快速增长的典型特征。在考虑准粒子重整化和方向性LO-TO分裂后，与常压下OH伸缩拉曼多重峰（OH-stretching Raman multiplet）实现了近定量吻合。

Conclusion: 有限温度动力学效应（finite-temperature dynamical effects）和谱相干性逐渐丧失（progressive loss of spectral coherence）是δ-AlOOH中氢键对称化光谱特征的根本起源。

Abstract: Raman and infrared anomalies associated with H-bond symmetrization in $δ$-AlOOH, including mode softening and linewidth broadening at 5-10 GPa, occur at significantly lower pressures than predicted by static harmonic theory. To resolve this discrepancy, we combine harmonic phonon calculations with strongly constrained and appropriately normed (SCAN)-based deep-potential molecular dynamics and phonon quasiparticle analysis at 300 K. This framework extracts temperature- and pressure-dependent frequencies and lifetimes from long-time trajectories, capturing the branch reorganization and rapid linewidth growth characteristic of the disordering regime. Incorporating quasiparticle renormalization and directional longitudinal-optical-transverse-optical (LO-TO) splitting further yields near-quantitative agreement with the ambient-pressure OH-stretching Raman multiplet. These results identify finite-temperature dynamical effects and the progressive loss of spectral coherence as the origin of the spectroscopic signatures of H-bond symmetrization.

### [60] [Uniform Asymptotics of the Pseudo Wigner-Ville Distribution for Nonlinear Chirps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13702)
*Vincenzo Pierro,Maurizio Feo,Maurizio Ricciardi,Rocco P. Croce,Theo Demma,Innocenzo M. Pinto,Paolo Addesso*

Main category: eess.SP

TL;DR: 本文为伪魏格纳-维尔分布（Pseudo Wigner Ville Distribution, PWVD）在处理非线性啁啾信号时建立的严格数学框架，利用含驻点相合（coalescing stationary points）的振荡积分理论导出了以对称不完全艾里函数（symmetric incomplete Airy functions）表达的均匀渐近展开式，统一了启发式信号处理与半经典几何方法，并在引力波天文学和雷达脉冲压缩两个实例中验证了其对干涉结构预测和峰值频率估计偏差分析的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PWVD虽具有优越的分辨率，但其固有的二次非线性（quadratic nonlinearity）会在相空间中产生复杂的干涉伪影和交叉项（cross terms），尤其是在非线性啁啾信号中这些伪影可能掩盖信号的物理特征，亟需一个严格的数学框架来描述和量化这些效应。

Method: 利用含驻点相合的振荡积分（oscillatory integrals with coalescing stationary points）理论，推导了适用于一般加窗非线性啁啾信号的PWVD均匀渐近展开式，该展开以对称不完全艾里函数（symmetric incomplete Airy functions）为闭式表达，实现了从启发式信号处理到半经典几何方法（Berry和弦构造，Berry's chord construction）的桥梁。

Result: 在引力波天文中并合双星（coalescing binaries）的高精度非线性啁啾信号和雷达非线性啁啾脉冲压缩两个实例中，解析结果成功预测了干涉图样的结构，并量化了基于峰值的频率估计（peak-based frequency estimation）中的系统偏差（systematic bias）。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了非线性数学分析与精密实验物理之间的系统桥梁，验证了PWVD在高信噪比（high signal to noise regimes）条件下作为信源精细表征（source characterization）鲁棒工具的有效性。

Abstract: The analysis of non stationary signals in complex physical systems often relies on Time Frequency distributions. Among these, the Pseudo Wigner Ville Distribution (PWVD) stands out for its superior resolution but is mathematically challenging due to its inherent quadratic nonlinearity. This nonlinearity generates complex interference artifacts and cross terms in the phase space, potentially obscuring the physical features of the signal, particularly for nonlinear chirps. In this work, we establish a mathematically grounded framework for the PWVD for general windowed nonlinear chirps. By leveraging the theory of oscillatory integrals with coalescing stationary points, we derive a uniform asymptotic expansion that bridges the gap between heuristic signal processing and semiclassical geometric approaches (Berry's chord construction). The resulting closed form representation, expressed in terms of symmetric incomplete Airy functions, provides a unified description of the nonlinear transform's behavior, regularizing the transition across the instantaneous frequency caustics. While the framework is general, we show its power on two illustrative examples: the high precision nonlinear chirps of coalescing binaries in gravitational-wave astronomy and
  radar nonlinear chirps for pulse compression applications. The analytical results successfully predict the structure of interference patterns and quantify the systematic bias in peak based frequency estimation. Therefore, this study establishes a systematic bridge between nonlinear mathematical analysis and precision experimental physics, validating the PWVD as a robust tool for detailed source characterization in high signal to noise regimes.

### [61] [Beyond the Unruh vacuum: multi-time correlations in black hole collapse and evaporation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13383)
*Konstantinos Xenos,Charis Anastopoulos,Andreas F. Terzis*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞信息悖论源于霍金辐射（Hawking radiation）的热性（thermal character）似乎会抹去坍缩物质的信息。然而，热性仅约束单一时间定义的观测量，时间量子关联的结构在很大程度上未被探索。

Method: 使用二维引力坍缩与蒸发模型，分析晚期多时间关联是否完全由Unruh真空（Unruh vacuum）再现。

Result: 晚期多时间关联不完全由Unruh真空再现；其中包含一个明确依赖于坍缩前状态参数的贡献，尽管渐近辐射具有热性。

Conclusion: 可测量的多时间关联（multi-time correlations）是霍金辐射中信息的载体；仅基于单时间观测量的黑洞信息悖论表述是不完整的。

Abstract: The black hole information paradox originates from the thermal character of Hawking radiation, which appears to erase information about the collapsing matter. However, thermality constrains only observables defined at a single time and leaves the structure of temporal quantum correlations largely unexplored. Here we show that multi-time quantum-field correlations provide a concrete mechanism for the survival of pre-collapse information in black hole evaporation. Using a two-dimensional model of gravitational collapse and evaporation, we demonstrate that late-time multi-time correlations are not fully reproduced by the Unruh vacuum. In particular, they contain a contribution that depends explicitly on parameters characterizing the pre-collapse state, despite the thermal character of the asymptotic radiation. Our results identify measurable multi-time correlations as carriers of information in Hawking radiation and suggest that formulations of the black hole information paradox based solely on single-time observables are incomplete.

### [62] [Resolving the Edge of a Quantum Pyramid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14698)
*Alvan Arulandu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文证实了Englert和Řeháček提出的量子金字塔猜想（quantum pyramids conjecture），即等角等概率纯态系综（ensemble of equiangular equiprobable pure states）的全局信息最优测量方案，通过证明Holevo和Utkin提出的剩余熵不等式（entropy inequalities），并针对钝角金字塔（obtuse pyramids）和平顶金字塔（flat pyramids）分别给出了严格证明和紧致ℓᵖ不等式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证Englert和Řeháček在arXiv:0905.0510中提出的量子金字塔猜想——该猜想断言存在对于等角等概率纯态系综的全局信息最优测量方案。此前Holevo和Utkin已在arXiv:2506.06700中提出了部分熵不等式，但剩余部分仍未证明，阻碍了猜想的最终确认。

Method: 针对钝角金字塔情形，核心贡献是严格证明局部极小化子（local minimizers）对应的熵不等式不可能具有三个不同坐标值，并进一步将这一排除过程约化为一个关于Lambert W函数（Lambert W function）分支的代数倒数不等式（algebraic reciprocal inequality）。针对平顶金字塔情形，采用对称不等式中的等变量方法（equal variables method），证明了Holevo和Utkin最近猜想、在d=3维度上解析验证并对于d≤200经数值验证的紧致ℓᵖ不等式（tight ℓᵖ inequality）对所有d≥2成立。

Result: 成功证明了剩余的所有熵不等式，从而完整确认了量子金字塔猜想，即获得了等角等概率纯态系综的全局信息最优测量方案。对于钝角金字塔，证明了局部极小化子不能拥有三个不同坐标值；对于平顶金字塔，对所有维度d≥2证明了紧致ℓᵖ不等式。

Conclusion: 量子金字塔猜想被最终证实，这意味着等角等概率纯态系综的信息最优测量方案已有严格的理论保证。所发展的代数倒数不等式方法和等变量方法可能具有独立的方法学价值，可推广至其他信息论或量子测量问题。

Abstract: Standing on the shoulders of giants, we resolve the quantum pyramids conjecture, confirming the globally information-optimal measurement for an ensemble of equiangular equiprobable pure states, as conjectured by Englert and Řeháček (arXiv:0905.0510). We do so by proving the remaining entropy inequalities of Holevo and Utkin (arXiv:2506.06700), which certify optimality for obtuse and flat pyramids. For obtuse pyramids, our key contribution is a rigorous proof that local minimizers of the corresponding entropy inequality cannot have three distinct coordinate values. We show that eliminating this family can be reduced to a neat algebraic reciprocal inequality relating branches of the Lambert $W$ function, which may be of independent interest. For flat pyramids, we prove a tight $\ell^p$ inequality for zero-sum vectors that was recently conjectured, proved analytically in dimension $d=3$, and computationally verified for $d\leq 200$ by Holevo and Utkin (arXiv:2603.24017). We prove this bound for all $d\geq 2$ via a technique in symmetric inequalities known as the equal variables method.

</details>


### [63] [Universal Crossovers of Stabilizer Entropy Beyond Criticality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13810)
*Reyhaneh Khasseh,E. A. Ramirez Trino,M. A. Rajabpour*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文针对有限范围自旋链中的稳定子Rényi熵（Stabilizer Rényi entropy）建立了精确的有限尺寸标度理论，揭示了从临界到非临界行为的普适交叉行为，并展示了系统尺寸与关联长度之间的竞争如何控制标度结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稳定子Rényi熵作为量子多体系统中非稳定子性（nonstabilizerness）的探针已受到关注，但其在临界点之外的标度结构相比纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）仍理解不足。最近的场论方法表明稳定子熵包含普适临界数据和边界敏感项，这引出了一个核心问题：这些结构如何延拓到质量区（massive regime）和交叉区（crossover regime）。

Method: 针对Rényi指标为二分之一（one-half）的一类有限范围自旋链，推导了全周期链和无限链中有限区间两种几何构型下的精确有限尺寸公式（finite-size formulas）。通过精确的稳定子熵对应关系，将标度理论推广到内部XY约化、有限范围自旋链及Cluster-Ising代表模型。

Result: 在周期几何中，熵在远离临界点时服从体积律（volume law），并呈现出由系统尺寸与关联长度（correlation length）竞争控制的普适有限尺寸交叉行为。大尺度稳定子Rényi熵密度在场调谐临界线上出现尖点（cusp），而XX端点则受饱和点控制的独立标度区支配。在子系统几何中，区间熵将体临界行为与由有限区域切割无限链产生的边界贡献分离，交叉行为由边界常数和关联长度控制的普适函数编码。

Conclusion: 研究结果为稳定子熵在孤立共形点（conformal points）之外的量子场论描述提供了精确的晶格基准，使得从临界到非临界行为的普适交叉在解析上变得可处理。

Abstract: Stabilizer Rényi entropy has emerged as a probe of nonstabilizerness in quantum many-body systems, but its scaling structure beyond critical points remains poorly understood compared with entanglement entropy. Recent field-theory approaches indicate that stabilizer entropy contains universal critical data and boundary-sensitive terms, raising the question of how these structures extend into massive and crossover regimes. We address this problem for a broad class of finite-range spin chains at Rényi index one-half. We derive exact finite-size formulas for both full periodic chains and finite intervals of the infinite chain, making the universal crossover from critical to noncritical behavior analytically accessible. In periodic geometry, the entropy obeys a volume law away from criticality and exhibits a universal finite-size crossover controlled by the competition between system size and correlation length. We also show that the large-scale SRE density develops a cusp across the field-tuned critical line, while the XX endpoint is governed by a distinct scaling regime associated with the saturation point. In the subsystem geometry, the interval entropy separates bulk critical behavior from boundary contributions generated by the way the finite region cuts the infinite chain. The crossover from critical to massive behavior is then encoded in boundary constants and universal functions controlled by the correlation length. Through exact stabilizer-entropy correspondences, the scaling theory extends to internal XY reductions, Finite-range spin chains, and Cluster--Ising representatives. Our results provide an exact lattice benchmark for the emerging QFT description of stabilizer entropy beyond isolated conformal points.

</details>


### [64] [No classical particle limit for massless quanta](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14632)
*Riccardo Falcone,Simon Fuchs*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过建立公理性的粗粒化运动学框架，证明了相对论性无质量经典粒子不可能作为无质量量子的经典极限出现，因为庞加莱群协变性与经典性操作条件不相容；该定理排除了经典光子或引力子，但允许电磁场或引力场等场论极限的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究相对论性无质量经典粒子是否可能作为无质量量子的经典极限而涌现，并试图在与具体动力学、环境或指针基无关的普适层面上回答该问题。

Method: 发展了一个公理化的纯运动学框架（axiomatic and purely kinematical framework），用于粗粒化方法（coarse-graining approach）。在该框架中，候选经典相空间被取为某个POVM（positive operator-valued measure，正算子值测度）的结果空间，仅受极小经典性条件及相关时空对称群下的协变性约束。将该框架应用于庞加莱群（Poincaré group）。

Result: 证明了无质量粒子的不可行定理（no-go theorem）：庞加莱群协变性要求与经典性操作条件不相容。该定理排除了经典无质量粒子（如经典光子或引力子）的涌现可能，但允许无质量量子的场论极限（如经典电磁场或引力场）的存在。

Conclusion: 无质量经典粒子不能从无质量量子的经典极限中涌现，但无质量量子的场论极限仍是开放的，这为理解经典场与量子场之间的关系提供了新的约束条件。

Abstract: We investigate whether relativistic massless classical particles may emerge as the classical limit of massless quanta. To address this question independently of any specific dynamics, environment, or pointer basis, we develop an axiomatic and purely kinematical framework for the coarse-graining approach. In this formulation, a candidate classical phase space is taken as the outcome space of a POVM subject only to minimal classicality and covariance under the relevant spacetime symmetry group. Applying this framework to the Poincaré group, we prove a no-go theorem for massless particles: the covariance requirement is incompatible with the operational conditions for classicality. The theorem leaves open field-like limits of massless quanta, for example the emergence of electromagnetic or gravitational fields, while ruling out classical massless particles, such as classical photons or gravitons.

</details>

*Evgeniy V. Zikiy,Nikita S. Smirnov,Stanislav A. Kotenkov,Ilya A. Stepanov,Julia A. Agafonova,Daria A. Moskaleva,Aleksei R. Matanin,Anton I. Ivanov,Dmitry O. Moskalev,Julia A. Kurochkina,Aleksander V. Andriyash,Ilya A. Rodionov*

Conclusion: 文章指出了若干待解决的开放问题，包括β相杂质（β-phase impurities）的作用、氢氟酸（hydrofluoric acid）溶液对链特性的影响，以及α-钽链（α-tantalum chains）在低温下的反常行为。

Abstract: The performance of superconducting integrated circuits for quantum applications is fundamentally limited by material-related losses. Tantalum, as an emerging material for next-generation quantum circuits, has attracted considerable attention in recent years after demonstrating breakthrough performance in both superconducting microwave resonators and qubits. Concurrently, a growing body of work is devoted to the operation of tantalum-based circuits and related fabrication techniques. This interest is further stimulated by tantalum thin films polymorphism resulting in a variety of its crystalline structure, superconducting properties, coherence, etc. Furthermore, tantalum circuits exhibit distinctive features in cryogenic experiments, which have not been observed in aluminum- or niobium-based ones. In this review, we summarize the recent research of tantalum thin films growth and phase selection mechanisms on various substrates, key aspects of fabrication and performance of superconducting circuit, including a material first-principles theoretical study. In conclusion, we address a number of open issues, including the role of \b{eta}-phase impurities, the effect of hydrofluoric acid solutions on chain characteristics, and the anomalous behavior of α-tantalum chains at cryogenic temperatures.

### [66] [Local correlations in long-range dual-unitary kicked Hamiltonian chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13857)
*Vladimir Al. Osipov,Marc Cedric Spyra,Jana Carolina Schumann,Thomas Guhr,Boris Gutkin*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 基于阿达马矩阵对（Hadamard matrix pair）构建了一类具有长程相互作用（long-range interactions）的双幺正（dual-unitary）自旋链模型，放宽了精确时空对称性（exact space-time symmetry）对仅允许最近邻相互作用的限制。在该模型中，局域两点关联函数（local two-point correlations）沿光锥边界（light-cone edges）|n| = r|t| 传播（r为相互作用程），且可对局域支撑算子（local support）解析求解，并以次近邻相互作用的 kicked Ising 自旋链为例进行了说明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多体 Floquet 模型（如 kicked Ising 自旋链）虽因精确时空对称性而具备双幺正动力学，但该对称性要求极为严格，仅允许最近邻相互作用（nearest-neighbor interactions），限制了模型的适用范围。

Method: 利用一对阿达马矩阵（Hadamard matrices）构造了一族具有长程相互作用的双幺正 kicked 自旋链。

Result: 在该类模型中，局域两点关联函数沿光锥边界 |n| = r|t| 传播（r为相互作用程），且可针对局域支撑算子（local support）获得解析表达式。

Conclusion: 所构造的模型将双幺正动力学推广到了长程相互作用情形，并通过次近邻相互作用的 kicked Ising 自旋链实例验证了该方法的可行性。

Abstract: Many-body Floquet models with exact space--time symmetry, such as the kicked Ising spin chain (KIC), provide natural examples of systems with dual-unitary dynamics. The requirement of exact space--time symmetry is, however, highly restrictive, as it permits only nearest-neighbor interactions. Based on a pair of Hadamard matrices, we construct a wide family of dual-unitary kicked spin chains with long-range interactions. We show that local two-point correlations in such models propagate along the light-cone edges \( |n| = r|t| \), where \(r\) is the interaction range, and can be derived analytically for operators with local support. This approach is illustrated using the example of a kicked Ising spin chain with next-to-next-neighbor interactions.

</details>

Abstract: We present a custom-designed ultrahigh vacuum (UHV) cluster tool developed for studying shallow nitrogen-vacancy (NV) centers in diamond, enabling in situ diamond surface preparation, characterization, and single NV center dynamics measurements within a single connected platform. The system combines a surface science chamber for controlled surface modification and analysis with a cryogenic confocal microscope chamber dedicated to NV spin and optical measurements. This integrated approach enables a direct correlation between diamond surface chemistry and the resulting NV spin and charge properties. The instrument provides a versatile platform for systematic studies of surface-induced decoherence mechanisms and charge dynamics for shallow NV centers, and establishes a pathway toward reproducible surface engineering for quantum sensing applications.

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明蒸馏、误差缓解和动态去耦等量子误差操控技术是量子纠错（quantum error correction）最一般框架的特例，通过将量子纠错扩展到状态自适应、信道自适应及多级编码场景实现统一视角，并基于此提出了自校正量子存储器（self-correcting quantum memory）模型。

  <summary>Details</summary>

### [69] [Dynamically frozen long-distance entanglement via non-Hermitian PT-symmetric systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14177)
*Sejal Ahuja,Keshav Das Agarwal,Aditi Sen De*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了分布式量子网络中，有效PT对称非厄米自旋1/2体（bulk）与两个量子链路弱耦合时，非厄米性如何影响长距离纠缠（LDE）的动态形成。通过解析和数值方法发现，在破缺区间的异常点（exceptional points）附近，初始可分离态可动态演化为高纠缠链路态，且弱虚磁场和弱体-链路耦合下可实现近单位时间平均纠缠，这一特性在厄米系统中无法实现。此外，非厄米动力学在异常点附近表现出纠缠冻结现象，且长程相互作用可在某些参数区间超越最近邻模型的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在分布式量子网络中，自旋体（spin bulk）可介导远距离节点间高纠缠链路的生成。本文旨在探究有效PT对称非厄米（non-Hermitian）自旋1/2体在弱耦合两个量子链路的条件下，非厄米性对长距离纠缠（long-distance entanglement, LDE）动态形成的影响机制。

Method: 采用有效非厄米最近邻（nearest-neighbor, NN）Su-Schrieffer-Heeger（SSH）模型，以受虚交错磁场（imaginary staggered magnetic fields）作用的量子XX体为范例模型，通过解析方法确定由体-链路相互作用导致的异常点（exceptional points），并结合解析与数值方法分析动力学演化过程。

Result: 初始完全可分离态可在破缺区间（broken regime）的异常点附近动态演化为高纠缠链路态；在弱虚磁场和弱体-链路耦合下可实现近单位时间平均纠缠，该特性在相应厄米系统中无法达到。非厄米动力学在异常点附近表现出高纠缠冻结现象，这一特征在厄米系统中不存在。此外，长程相互作用模型在某些参数区间可产生比最近邻模型更高的时间平均纠缠，且长距离纠缠在稳态下仍然保持。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，工程化的非厄米动力学在量子网络中实现鲁棒且冻结的纠缠链路方面具有重要潜力。通过合理调控虚磁场和体-链路耦合，可在非厄米系统中获得厄米系统无法达到的高纠缠性能，为分布式量子网络的纠缠生成提供了新途径。

Abstract: In distributed quantum networks, interacting spin systems can mediate the generation of highly entangled links between distant nodes. We investigate the role of effective parity-time (PT)-symmetric non-Hermitian spin-1/2 bulks weakly coupled to two quantum links, obtained due to the environmental interactions affecting both the bulk and the links. Focusing on effective non-Hermitian nearest-neighbor (NN) Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) models, we analyze how non-Hermiticity influences the dynamical formation of long-distance entanglement (LDE). For a paradigmatic model consisting of a quantum XX bulk subjected to imaginary staggered magnetic fields, we analytically determine the exceptional points arising from the resulting bulk-mediated interactions between the links. Combining analytical and numerical methods, we demonstrate that an initially fully separable state can dynamically evolve into highly entangled link states near these exceptional points in the broken regime. Further, after optimizing over time and system parameters, near-unit time-averaged entanglement between the links emerges under weak imaginary magnetic fields and bulk-link couplings, which cannot be attained in the corresponding Hermitian systems. Moreover, the non-Hermitian dynamics exhibit a freezing of high entanglement in the vicinity of exceptional points, a feature absent in Hermitian counterparts. We also identify regimes of long-range interaction strengths that yield a higher time-averaged entanglement than the corresponding NN models. Furthermore, we establish that LDE persists in the stationary regime, highlighting the promise of engineered non-Hermitian dynamics for realizing robust and frozen entangled links in quantum networks.

</details>


### [70] [Dissipation-induced superradiance in matter coupled to a self-interacting cavity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14526)
*Sebastian Schmid,Matteo Soriente,Oded Zilberberg,Javier del Pino*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究在Dicke模型框架下引入光子Kerr非线性，发现负Kerr非线性可诱导低阈值超辐射相（superradiant phase）并伴随自旋反转（spin inversion）；尽管该相在封闭系统中不稳定，腔耗散（cavity dissipation）能将其稳定，为激光产生和浴工程相（bath-engineered phases）开辟新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光-物质相互作用的超辐射相变阈值通常过高或受抗磁项（diamagnetic term）抑制而难以实验实现，亟需探索降低阈值的新机制。

Method: 在Dicke模型（Dicke model）框架中引入光子自相互作用，以光子Kerr非线性（photonic Kerr nonlinearity）建模，分析负Kerr非线性对超辐射相变的影响。

Result: 负Kerr非线性能够产生低阈值的超辐射相，并伴随自旋反转（spin inversion）现象；然而该相在封闭系统中不稳定，腔耗散（cavity dissipation）可以将其稳定化。

Conclusion: 腔耗散能稳定负Kerr非线性诱导的低阈值超辐射相，为激光器设计和浴工程相（bath-engineered phases）的实现提供了新的可能性。

Abstract: Light-matter interactions are often modeled via the Dicke model, namely, by two-level systems coupled to a cavity mode. Alas, the threshold for superradiance is often experimentally inaccessible or hindered by light's diamagnetic term. Here, within the Dicke setting, we consider self-interacting light in a cavity, modeled by a photonic Kerr nonlinearity. We show that negative Kerr nonlinearity gives rise to a low-threshold superradiant phase with spin inversion. While unstable in a closed system, cavity dissipation stabilizes this lit phase, opening avenues for lasing and bath-engineered phases.

### [71] [Enhancement of spin current in Fe$_{85}$Co$_{15}$/Ni$_{80}$Fe$_{20}$ bilayers via interlayer ferromagnetic coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13805)
*A. A. Pérez Martínez,D. Velázquez Rodríguez,D. Goijman,T. Torres,M. H. Aguirre,J. Gómez,A. Butera,E. De Biasi,J. Milano*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了Fe$_{85}$Co$_{15}$/Ni$_{80}$Fe$_{20}$双层膜中层间磁耦合强度对自旋波行为的影响，通过实验表征与基于Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert方程的双层膜模型计算，发现坡莫合金层的磁化进动椭球面积在特定交换常数下达到最大值，表明可通过调节层间交换常数、饱和磁化强度或激发频率来优化注入自旋电流。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 面内磁滞回线显示起源于磁晶各向异性的立方磁各向异性，易轴沿Fe-Co的[100]晶向，难轴沿[110]晶向；坡莫合金层的磁化进动椭球面积在特定交换常数处出现最大值。

Conclusion: 该进动面积最大化效应可用于优化注入自旋电流，且可通过改变双层膜系统的层间交换常数、材料饱和磁化强度或激发频率进行调控。

Abstract: We present a detailed study on how the strength of the interlayer magnetic coupling on Fe$_{85}$Co$_{15}$/Ni$_{80}$Fe$_{20}$ bilayers modifies the spin wave behavior of this system. A series of Fe$_{85}$Co$_{15}$/Ni$_{80}$Fe$_{20}$ bilayers deposited on MgO[100] substrates were grown by magnetron sputtering. Magnetic characterization of the samples was performed using a vibrating sample magnetometer and magneto-optical Kerr effect. The in-plane hysteresis loops reveal a cubic magnetic anisotropy of magnetocrystalline origin, with easy and hard axis along the [100] and [110] Fe-Co crystallographic directions, respectively. Ferromagnetic resonance measurements were performed to analyze the in-plane angular dependence of the resonance field, and also the resonance field at several frequencies was determined along the hard axis. By using a bilayer model in the frame of the Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert magnetization equation of motion, the magnetization precession components were calculated, as well as the dependence of precession area on the Fe-Co layer thickness and the ferromagnetic interlayer coupling. We observe a maximum in the area of the ellipsoid generated by the magnetization precession of the permalloy layer at a certain exchange constant, showing that this effect could be used to maximize the injected spin currents, which could be tuned by changing the interlayer exchange constant in bilayer systems, the saturation magnetization of the materials, or the excitation frequency.

### [72] [A Collective-Spin Derivation of the Uniform Magnon Hamiltonian in Cavity Magnonics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13830)
*Tomas Aguiar,Marcos Cesar de Oliveira*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文从集体自旋（collective spin）出发，直接推导了腔体磁子学（cavity magnonics）中常用的有效均匀模哈密顿量，无需引入格点分辨的玻色子算符，并揭示了主导非线性修正会导致有效磁子-光子耦合的占据数依赖降低，即有限自旋饱和（finite-spin saturation）效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有腔体磁子学的有效均匀模哈密顿量通常通过引入格点分辨的玻色子算符（site-resolved bosonic operators）再取均匀极限来推导，过程较为繁琐。作者希望建立一条更直接、物理图像更清晰的推导路径，并揭示该推导中隐含的物理效应。

Method: 从最近邻海森堡铁磁体（Heisenberg ferromagnet）与长波长磁场耦合的模型出发，将相关动力学限制在全对称自旋扇区（fully symmetric spin sector），从而使交换相互作用仅贡献一个常数能移，铁磁体等效为一个长度为$Ns$的大自旋（macrospin）。接着直接对总自旋应用Holstein-Primakoff变换（Holstein-Primakoff transformation），得到均匀磁子模（uniform magnon mode）及其主导非线性修正。

Result: 得到了不含格点分辨算符的有效均匀模哈密顿量，并明确该推导将铁磁体解释为一个合成的大自旋原子（synthetic large-spin atom）。物理上，主导非线性修正导致有效磁子-光子耦合随磁子占据数增加而降低，这是强均匀模驱动下有限自旋饱和的简单信号。

Conclusion: 该集体自旋推导为驱动和Floquet腔体磁子学中的有效哈密顿量提供了一条紧凑的推导路径，并自然揭示了有限自旋饱和这一可观测的非线性效应。

Abstract: We present a direct collective-spin derivation of the effective uniform-mode Hamiltonian used in cavity magnonics. Starting from a nearest-neighbor Heisenberg ferromagnet coupled to long-wavelength magnetic fields, we show that the relevant dynamics can be restricted to the fully symmetric spin sector, where the exchange interaction contributes only a constant energy shift and the ferromagnet behaves as a macrospin of length $Ns$. Applying the Holstein--Primakoff transformation directly to this total spin yields the usual uniform magnon mode and its leading nonlinear corrections without first introducing site-resolved bosonic operators. This collective formulation makes explicit the interpretation of the ferromagnet as a synthetic large-spin atom and provides a compact route to the effective Hamiltonians used in driven and Floquet cavity magnonics. As a physical consequence, the leading nonlinear correction produces an occupation-dependent reduction of the effective magnon--photon coupling, providing a simple signature of finite-spin saturation under strong uniform-mode driving.

</details>


### [73] [Strain- and doping-tunable optical resonance in Kekulé-Y graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14424)
*Yawar Mohammadi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究Kekulé-Y石墨烯在单轴应变和载流子掺杂下的光学响应，发现应变会重塑低能电子结构并诱导Van Hove奇点，产生强烈各向异性共振，为Kekulé-Y相提供明确光学标识，并确立应变工程为调控谷依赖光学特性的有效途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索Kekulé-Y石墨烯在应变和掺杂下的光学响应特性，寻找用于实验识别Kekulé-Y相的光学标识。

Method: 采用低能有效哈密顿量（low-energy effective Hamiltonian）描述电子结构，基于Kubo形式论（Kubo formalism）计算光导率（optical conductivity），并结合解析推导分析低能光导率和Drude权重（Drude weight）。

Result: 应变重塑了Kekulé-Y相的低能电子结构，诱导出远低于原始石墨烯能量的Van Hove奇点（Van Hove singularities）。光导率中呈现出多个各向异性带间特征，其中由应变诱导的Van Hove奇点产生的共振强烈各向异性，且对中等热展宽和无序具有鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 应变工程可有效调控Kekulé-Y石墨烯中源于狄拉克谷（Dirac valleys）Kekulé耦合的谷依赖光学特性；所发现的强各向异性共振可作为Kekulé-Y相的清晰光学信号，为其实验识别提供了可行的光学探测手段。

Abstract: We investigate the optical response of Kekulé-Y graphene under uniaxial strain and carrier doping. Using a low-energy effective Hamiltonian, we show that strain reshapes the low-energy electronic structure of the Kekulé-Y phase and induces Van Hove singularities at energies well below those of pristine graphene. Within the Kubo formalism, we calculate the optical conductivity and identify multiple anisotropic interband features, with a pronounced resonance arising from strain-induced Van Hove singularities. The pronounced resonance is strongly anisotropic and robust against moderate thermal broadening and disorder, providing a clear optical signature of Kekulé-Y ordering. We further derive analytical expressions for the low-energy optical conductivity and the Drude weight, providing a detailed characterization of the strain- and doping-dependent optical response. Our results establish strain engineering as an effective route for controlling valley-dependent optical properties in Kekulé-Y graphene, originating from the Kekulé-induced coupling of the Dirac valleys, and suggest feasible optical probes for the experimental identification of the Kekulé-Y phase.

### [74] [On-chip superconducting GHz RF reflectometry of the capacitance response in bilayer graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14431)
*Sung Jin An,Minseo Cho,Minjun Park,Dohun Kim,HyeonJeong An,Seung-Bo Shim,Hakseong Kim,Sunghun Lee,Myoung-Jae Lee,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Jungpil Seo,Myunglae Jo,Youngwook Kim,Minkyung Jung*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过在双层石墨烯（bilayer graphene）器件上集成超导LC谐振器，利用射频反射测量（RF reflectometry）同时提取直流输运（DC transport）和电容响应（capacitive response），观察到与位移场诱导能隙（field-induced gap）相一致的电容最小值与电子-空穴不对称性（electron-hole asymmetry）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在双栅双层石墨烯中，垂直位移场会打开一个带隙（band gap），同时改变沟道电导（channel conductance）和电子压缩率（electronic compressibility），因此需要在同一器件上同时测量电阻性（resistive）和电容性（capacitive）响应，以获得更完整的物理图像。

Method: 将六方氮化硼（hBN）封装的双层石墨烯异质结与片上超导铌（Nb）集总元件LC谐振器集成，在约4.25 GHz下进行射频反射测量（RF reflectometry）；同时在相同器件上进行直流输运和有限偏压谱学（finite-bias spectroscopy）作为输运参考。

Result: DC和RF栅极映射（gate maps）显示出相同的栅极依赖特征；有限偏压测量表明，电导抑制区的偏压范围随位移场增大而增大，符合场诱导能隙行为；栅极依赖的谐振频率偏移经等效电路模型（equivalent-circuit model）转换为有效电容，该电容在电导抑制区附近出现最小值，并表现出电子-空穴不对称性。

Conclusion: 片上配置可探测双栅范德瓦尔斯异质结（van der Waals heterostructure）的栅极依赖导纳（admittance），提供与直流输运互补的电容敏感信息，有望在单一器件中实现输运与电容响应的联合表征。

Abstract: In dual-gated bilayer graphene, a perpendicular displacement field opens a band gap that modifies both the channel conductance and the electronic compressibility, motivating measurements that resolve resistive and capacitive responses on the same device. We integrate an hBN-encapsulated bilayer graphene heterostructure with an on-chip superconducting Nb lumped-element LC resonator and carry out RF reflectometry near 4.25 GHz. DC transport and finite-bias spectroscopy on the same device provide a transport reference. Top and bottom gates independently set the carrier density and displacement field. The DC and RF gate maps share the same gate-dependent features, with finite-bias measurements revealing a region of suppressed conductance whose bias extent grows with the displacement field, consistent with a field-induced gap. The gate-dependent resonance-frequency shift is converted to the effective capacitance seen by the resonator using an equivalent-circuit model. The capacitance shows a minimum near the conductance-suppressed region, consistent with reduced electronic compressibility in the gapped bilayer graphene, and exhibits an electron-hole asymmetry. The on-chip configuration probes the gate-dependent admittance of a dual-gated van der Waals heterostructure, providing capacitance-sensitive information that complements DC transport within a single device.

</details>


### [75] [Spin-orbit coupling by design in quantum state engineering of atomically defined quantum dots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14487)
*Hermann Osterhage,Julian H. Strik,Ivan Ado,Anna M. H. Krieg,Daniel Wegner,Mikhail Titov,Alexander A. Khajetoorians*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过原子级精度的限域势（confinement potential）设计，在半导体量子点（quantum dots）中实现了对自旋-轨道哈密顿量（spin-orbit Hamiltonian）及其量子态的精确调控。利用扫描隧道显微镜/谱学（STM/STS）在锑化铟表面构筑Cs离子量子点结构，实验证明了能级结构（包括零场分裂）可通过局域电场几何设计来定制，并提出了超越传统Bychkov-Rashba描述的限域诱导自旋-轨道耦合哈密顿量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的调控对于在受限半导体纳米结构中控制自旋和电荷至关重要，但通常难以实现真正的可控性。本文旨在通过原子级精度的限域势设计，实现自旋-轨道哈密顿量及其量子态的可控性，从而填补这一技术空白。

Method: 采用扫描隧道显微镜和谱学（scanning tunnelling microscopy and spectroscopy）技术，在锑化铟（indium antimonide）表面将单个Cs离子图案化成为设计的量子点结构，使来自二维电子气（two-dimensional electron gas）的电子在选定的面内电场梯度（in-plane electric-field gradients）下被限域。随后通过空间分辨电子态的轨道特征及其磁场演化，定量分析原子级能级结构。

Result: 实验证明，包括诱导零场分裂（zero-field splitting）在内的能级结构可通过局域电场的几何设计来定制。该效应可用一个超越传统Bychkov-Rashba描述（Bychkov-Rashba description）的哈密顿量来一致描述，该哈密顿量基于多能带k·p模型（multiband k.p model）推导，并考虑了相关物理参数的能量依赖性。

Conclusion: 这种在半导体量子点中对自旋-轨道耦合的精确控制，对量子技术（quantum technologies）和自旋电子学技术（spintronic technologies）具有重要的应用价值。

Abstract: Tuning spin-orbit coupling is essential in controlling both spin and charge in confined semiconductor nanostructures, yet it is rarely a truly controllable parameter. Here, we show control over the spin-orbit Hamiltonian in quantum dots and the resulting quantum states by tailoring the confinement potential with atomic-scale precision. Using scanning tunnelling microscopy and spectroscopy, we pattern individual Cs ions into designer quantum dot structures on the surface of indium antimonide, in which electrons from a two-dimensional electron gas are confined with chosen in-plane electric-field gradients. We then quantify the atomic level structure, both spatially resolving the orbital character of the electronic states and their magnetic-field evolution. We demonstrate that the level structure, including the induced zero-field splitting, can be tailored by the designed geometry of the local electric fields. These effects can be described using a Hamiltonian that allows consistent treatment of the confinement-induced spin-orbit coupling beyond the conventional Bychkov-Rashba description. This Hamiltonian is derived from a multiband k.p model and takes the energy dependence of the relevant physical parameters into account. Such precise control of spin-orbit coupling in semiconductor quantum dots is relevant to quantum and spintronic technologies.

</details>


### [76] [Quantum geometrical description of hole spin qubits far away from the $Γ$-point](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14683)
*Zoltán György,Dmitry Miserev,Jelena Klinovaja,Daniel Loss*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过非微扰方法推导了空穴自旋量子比特（hole spin qubits）的有效哈密顿量，揭示了二维空穴气（2DHG）的量子几何结构自然涌现，并指出二维空穴气的自旋轨道耦合（SOI）与面内约束产生的SOI形式不同、无法同时消除，从而破坏了自旋比特的完美自旋轨道开关功能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 空穴自旋量子比特因其本征自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit interaction, SOI）可实现快速电学操控，是自旋量子计算的重要平台。然而，平面量子点中的SOI此前主要聚焦于二维空穴气（two-dimensional hole gas, 2DHG）的本征SOI，面内约束所产生的SOI尚未被充分研究。本文的动机在于系统研究由面内约束产生的SOI对空穴自旋量子比特的影响。

Method: 通过非微扰（non-perturbative）方法数值推导空穴自旋量子比特的有效哈密顿量。利用对称性方法构建了四种低维空穴系统的有效哈密顿量：(i) SiGe/Ge/SiGe异质结构中的重空穴（heavy-hole），(ii) SnGe/Ge中的轻空穴（light-hole），(iii) SiGe/Ge/SiGe中栅极定义的纳米线（gate-defined nanowire），(iv) Ge/Si核壳纳米线（core/shell nanowire）中的空穴。

Result: 研究发现二维空穴气的量子几何结构（quantum geometry）自然涌现，给出了远离Γ点（Γ-point）时仍有意义的非微扰赝自旋（pseudospin）定义。2DHG的SOI与面内约束产生的SOI具有不同形式，无法同时关闭，从而破坏了自旋量子比特的完美自旋轨道开关功能。非微扰有效哈密顿量与完整哈密顿量的计算结果高度一致。

Conclusion: 非微扰有效哈密顿量能够准确描述空穴自旋量子比特在远离Γ点区域的物理行为。面内约束产生的SOI与2DHG本征SOI的不可同时消除性，对自旋量子比特的操控设计具有重要限制意义。该方法的精确性为后续空穴自旋量子器件的理论建模提供了可靠工具。

Abstract: Hole spin qubits provide one of the leading platforms for spin-based quantum computing due to their large intrinsic spin-orbit interaction (SOI), which enables fast electrical manipulation. The SOI of planar quantum dots has mostly been investigated in theoretical studies by examining the SOI already present in the two-dimensional hole gas (2DHG). Here, we study the SOI created by the in-plane confinement by deriving non-perturbative effective Hamiltonians numerically for hole spin qubits. We find that the quantum geometry of the 2DHG naturally emerges, leading to a meaningful non-perturbative definition of pseudospin valid far away from the $Γ$-point. The SOI of the 2DHG and of the in-plane confinement have different forms; therefore, they cannot be turned off simultaneously, ruining the perfect spin-orbit switch functionality of spin qubits. We construct effective Hamiltonians using the symmetry approach for various low-dimensional hole systems: (i) a heavy-hole confined in a SiGe/Ge/SiGe heterostructure, (ii) a light-hole confined in SnGe/Ge, (iii) a gate-defined nanowire in SiGe/Ge/SiGe, and (iv) a hole confined in a Ge/Si core/shell nanowire. The non-perturbative effective Hamiltonians provide results with excellent agreement with the full Hamiltonians.

Method: 在单片魔角扭曲双层石墨烯（MATBG）架构中，通过静电约束（electrostatic confinement）与可调超导性的组合，在同一器件中构建了超导岛（superconducting island）和邻近化量子点（proximitized quantum dot）两种互补的混合系统。

Result: 超导岛表现出2e周期输运，显示超导能隙（gap）保护良好，可抵抗准粒子中毒（quasiparticle poisoning）。邻近化量子点中观察到亚能隙安德烈夫态（subgap Andreev state），并伴随强宇称调制（parity-modulated）的超电流。

Conclusion: 该工作展示了一种在单一晶体内同时实现超导岛和邻近化量子点的新型量子器件架构，为研究平带超导与强关联电子竞争、以及开发可重构超导量子电路提供了平台。

Abstract: Gate-tunable superconductivity in magic-angle twisted bilayer graphene (MATBG) has enabled the realization of superconducting devices, such as Josephson junctions, within a single crystal. This interface-free platform provides a reconfigurable and scalable architecture that overcomes limitations of conventional superconducting-semiconducting systems. Incorporating single-electron control enables access to regimes in which flat-band superconductivity competes with strong Coulomb repulsion, providing a platform for studying correlated physics phenomena. Here, we report a new class of quantum devices that combines electrostatic confinement with tunable superconductivity in a monolithic MATBG architecture. Within a single device, we demonstrate two complementary hybrid systems: superconducting islands and proximitized quantum dots. The superconducting island exhibits $2e$-periodic transport, indicating a well-defined gap protected against quasiparticle poisoning. The proximitized quantum dot hosts subgap Andreev states together with a strongly parity-modulated supercurrent.

### [78] [Extreme-Scale Atomistic Simulation of Real-Temperature Magnetic Skyrmion Dynamics by Coupled Spin-Lattice Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14073)

TL;DR: 本文提出一种结合自旋约束密度泛函理论训练的神经进化势与结构保持自旋-晶格积分器的机器学习框架，在LineShine超算上实现了134万亿原子与同等数量自旋的耦合自旋-晶格拓扑磁动力学模拟，加速此前自旋感知方法达七个数量级，直接解析了实际温度下的斯格明子成核与重组过程。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将自旋约束密度泛函理论（spin-constrained density-functional theory）训练的神经进化势（neuro-evolution potential）与结构保持自旋-晶格积分器（structure-preserving spin-lattice integrator）整合在同一机器学习框架中。通过架构特定优化、内核融合（kernel fusion）、SVE2向量化（SVE2 vectorization）及NUMA感知数据布局（NUMA-aware data layout）实现加速。在LineShine百亿亿次超算（exascale supercomputer）上部署。

Result: 整体加速达此前自旋感知方法的七倍数量级（seven orders-of-magnitude）。在LineShine上扩展至1245万CPU核心，弱扩展效率89.7%，实现134万亿原子与同等数量自旋的模拟，双精度性能达48.5 PFLOPS。直接解析了此前无法触及尺度下的实际温度斯格明子成核（skyrmion nucleation）与重组（reorganization）过程。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了耦合自旋-晶格拓扑磁动力学预测性模拟的新范式（new regime），表明机器学习与高性能计算结合可突破器件相关尺度下真实温度磁动力学模拟的计算瓶颈。

Abstract: Real-temperature topological magnetic dynamics in functional materials is governed by coupled lattice and spin evolution, yet remains inaccessible to predictive simulation at device-relevant scales. As a flagship example, thermally driven helix-to-skyrmion transformation in FeGe requires atomistic resolution, explicit lattice motion, and micrometer-scale domains to resolve device-scale topological texture formation. We combine a spin-constrained density-functional-theory-trained neuro-evolution potential with a structure-preserving spin-lattice integrator within one machine-learned framework. Architecture-specific optimizations, kernel fusion, SVE2 vectorization, and NUMA-aware data layout deliver a seven orders-of-magnitude speedup over prior spin-aware methods. Deployed on LineShine exascale supercomputer, the full application scales to 12.45 million CPU cores with 89.7% weak-scaling efficiency, enabling simulations of 1.34 trillion atoms and an equal number of spins while reaching 48.5 PFLOPS in double precision. The simulations directly resolve real-temperature skyrmion nucleation and reorganization at previously inaccessible scales, establishing a new regime for predictive simulation of coupled spin-lattice topological magnetic dynamics.
