### [79] [Non-Markovian Memory-Induced Effects in Quantum Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13716)
*Aarav Shah,Paulo Moniz,Oem Trivedi,Meet J. Vyas*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 通过引入因果记忆核（causal memory kernel）扩展半经典 Wheeler-DeWitt 框架，在亚主导阶实现非局域量子宇宙学，并推导出对原初功率谱（primordial power spectrum）的 $k^{3/4}$ 修正及其在 CMB 各向异性、非高斯性和结构形成中的可观测效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准半经典 Wheeler-DeWitt 框架仅在局域形式下有效，无法描述量子引力中可能存在的非局域记忆效应。本文旨在系统性地引入记忆效应，而非直接假设分数阶导数，从而给出更底层的动力学描述。

Method: 在半经典 Wheeler-DeWitt 框架中，于亚主导阶引入一个因果记忆核（causal memory kernel），以此产生非局域动力学（nonlocal dynamics），并证明分数阶时间演化（fractional time evolution）在其中作为有效的低能描述出现。

Result: 在 de Sitter 时空的宇宙学扰动中，原初功率谱获得特征性的 $k^{3/4}$ 标度修正，主要影响高温 CMB 各向异性；非高斯性的双谱（bispectrum）产生标度依赖修正，可能偏离标准 squeezed 极限一致性关系；记忆系数需要一定调节以避免对结构形成产生不可接受的效应。

Conclusion: 该框架基于记忆效应实现了分数阶量子宇宙学（fractional quantum cosmology）的具体构造，并指出非局域量子引力动力学可能在 CMB 观测和结构形成中留下可探测的特征；循环扩展的 Hawking-Hartle 无边界提议（no-boundary proposal）可能允许记忆强度在宇宙历史中演化。

Abstract: We study memory effects in quantum cosmology by extending the semiclassical Wheeler-DeWitt framework beyond its usual local form. The main idea is to introduce a causal memory kernel at sub leading order, rather than imposing fractional derivatives directly by hand. In this setting, fractional time evolution appears as an effective description of the underlying nonlocal dynamics. We apply the framework to cosmological perturbations in de Sitter space and find a correction to the primordial power spectrum with a characteristic $k^{3/4}$ scaling. This contribution mainly affects high $l$ CMB temperature anisotropies, in contrast with standard semiclassical quantum gravitational corrections, which are strongest at large angular scales. We also discuss how the same memory-dependent dynamics may affect primordial non-Gaussianity, producing scale dependent corrections to the bispectrum and possible deviations from the usual squeezed limit consistency relation. Since the memory coefficient controls short scale power, it may also influence structure formation and could require some tuning in order to give phenomenologically acceptable astrophysical environments. Finally, we suggest that a cyclic extension of the Hawking-Hartle no-boundary proposal may provide a setting in which the effective memory strength can evolve across successive cosmological histories. In this way, the framework gives a concrete realization of fractional quantum cosmology based on memory effects and also points to possible observational signatures of nonlocal quantum gravitational dynamics.

</details>


### [80] [Decoding the Gravitational Geometry and Stellar Photometric Profiles of Galaxy NGC 7331](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13718)
*Aritra Sanyal Bikramarka S. Choudhury Farook Rahaman*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 基于NGC 7331的旋转曲线与WISE W1测光数据，在广义相对论框架下构建静态球对称各向异性物质模型，发现恒星质量在中等至大半径处不足以解释总引力质量，证实暗物质主导地位，并验证了模型的能量条件、因果性和轨道稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用星系旋转曲线（galaxy rotation curves）作为探测旋涡星系质量分布的有力探针，并尝试在广义相对论（general relativity）框架下对NGC 7331进行自洽的物理分析，以更精确地约束其质量分布并检验暗物质的存在。

Method: 采用静态球对称时空（static, spherically symmetric spacetime）与各向异性物质（零径向压强）假设；利用观测旋转曲线和WISE W1 3.4 μm测光数据约束恒星质量分布；对运动学数据拟合修正的指数方位角速度律（modified exponential azimuthal velocity law），重构度规函数并导出包围质量、能量密度和切向压强分布。

Result: 恒星质量在中等至大半径处低估了总引力质量，表明暗物质（dark matter）占主导地位；通过与标准Navarro–Frenk–White暗物质晕轮廓的比较，验证了模型的合理性；该相对论模型满足能量条件（energy conditions）、因果性约束（causality constraints）以及圆形轨道稳定性（stability of circular orbits）。

Conclusion: 将旋转曲线数据与测光恒星质量估计相结合，并在广义相对论框架下进行分析，能够为NGC 7331这类旋涡星系提供一致且物理上合理的质量分布描述。

Abstract: Galaxy rotation curves provide a powerful probe of mass distributions in spiral galaxies. We present a general relativistic analysis of NGC 7331 using its observed rotation curve and WISE W1 (3.4 $μ$m) photometry to constrain the stellar mass profile. Adopting a static, spherically symmetric spacetime with anisotropic matter (vanishing radial pressure), we fit a modified exponential azimuthal velocity law to kinematic data, reconstructing metric functions and deriving enclosed mass, energy density, and tangential pressure profiles. The stellar mass underpredicts the total gravitating mass at intermediate-to-large radii, indicating dominant dark matter. The physical viability of the resulting relativistic model is examined through energy conditions, causality constraints, and the stability of circular orbits. A comparison with the standard Navarro--Frenk--White dark matter profile has been done. Overall, this study demonstrates that combining rotation-curve data with photometric stellar mass estimates within a general relativistic framework provides a consistent and physically viable description of the mass distribution in spiral galaxies such as NGC~7331.

### [81] [High-Precision Relativistic Time Scales for Mars Surface and Orbital Clocks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13726)
*Slava G. Turyshev*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个火星中心后牛顿框架（Mars-centered post-Newtonian framework），用于关联各种火星相关时间尺度（如质心坐标时、火星中心坐标时、火星表面时及固有时间），并在1e-18频率精度和0.1皮秒累积定时精度下评估了多种火星轨道时钟的相对论效应，为未来的火星时间历表（Mars Time Ephemeris）提供了参考系统和模型保留框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着火星探测任务（如轨道器、着陆器和中继通信卫星）对高精度时间同步与深空导航需求的提升，需要在后牛顿相对论框架下统一质心系与火星系之间的时间尺度转换，并评估不同轨道高度和构型下的相对论时钟偏差。

Method: 基于国际天文学联合会（IAU）的质心天球参考系/质心坐标时（BCRS/TCB）形式体系，引入火星中心坐标时（Areocentric Coordinate Time, TCA），将每个时钟变换分解为长期漂移率（secular rate）与零均值周期项（zero-mean periodic terms）。只保留分数频率振幅超过5×10⁻¹⁸或单向累积定时振幅超过0.1 ps的项；数值实现采用GMM-3火星重力场（阶次至120阶）、移除原点与偶极项的太阳/火卫一/火卫二质点潮汐模型。

Result: 相对于火星表面时尺度，300 km近极轨道时钟每天慢4.56微秒，火卫一同步轨道（areostationary）和火卫二距离轨道时钟分别每天快9.13和9.52微秒。火星J₂项导致的定时线（timing line）在300 km高度约为87 ps，在倾斜或天平动的准同步轨道半径附近仍保持数ps；近日点标度太阳潮汐项在高椭圆中继轨道中保留为亚ps量级。

Conclusion: 该框架是参考系统和模型保留框架，而非最终可运行的火星时间历表。要真正实现亚皮秒级系统，还需选定行星历表、火星定向与季节性重力模型、航天器定轨、校准链路延迟和协方差分析；季节性的CO₂交换导致的低阶重力场时变是火星表面时实现中的主要修正项，在声称亚ps精度前必须建模、监测或经验约束。

Abstract: We develop a Mars-centered post-Newtonian framework for relating barycentric coordinate time, Mars-centered coordinate time, a conventional Mars surface time scale, and the proper times of landed and orbiting clocks. The construction follows the International Astronomical Union BCRS/TCB formalism, introduces Areocentric Coordinate Time (TCA), and writes each clock transformation as a secular rate plus zero-mean periodic terms. Terms are retained when their fractional-frequency amplitude exceeds 5e-18 or their one-way accumulated timing amplitude exceeds 0.1 ps. The numerical realization uses the GMM-3 Mars gravity field through degree and order 120, point-mass tides from the Sun, Phobos, and Deimos with origin and dipole terms removed, and bounds on omitted local c^-4 and external-perturber terms. Representative low-Mars-orbit, areostationary, Phobos-/Deimos-distance, and highly elliptical relay regimes are evaluated. Relative to the adopted Mars surface scale, a 300 km near-polar clock is slower by 4.56 microseconds per day, while areostationary and Deimos-distance clocks are faster by 9.13 and 9.52 microseconds per day. The leading Mars-J2 timing line is about 87 ps at 300 km altitude and remains several ps near areostationary radius for inclined or librating areosynchronous cases; perihelion-scaled solar tides become retained sub-ps terms in high relay orbits. The result is a reference-system and model-retention framework, not a final operational Mars Time Ephemeris. A realized sub-ps system still requires a selected planetary ephemeris, Mars orientation and seasonal-gravity model, spacecraft orbit determination, calibrated link delays, and covariance analysis. Time-variable low-degree gravity from seasonal CO2 exchange is a leading surface-realization term and must be modeled, monitored, or empirically bounded before sub-ps Mars surface-scale claims are made.

</details>


### [82] [\textsc{SPLIT}: a robust semi-coherent inference pipeline for long-inspiral gravitational-wave sources](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13728)
*Shubham Kejriwal*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文针对LISA引力波探测中EMRI/IMRI信号的长时段相位相干分析难题，提出了一个半相干贝叶斯推理框架（SPLIT），通过将数据分段独立处理再非相干重组，显著降低了因相位误差累积导致的系统偏差，并在注入测试中展示出相比全相干分析更优的参数精度（偏差从≈4.8σ降至≲0.5σ）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LISA将探测持续数月到数年的极端/中等质量比旋近（EMRI/IMRI）引力波（gravitational waves）信号。现有全相干分析流水线对波形精度要求极为严格，长时间信号建模不完善会导致显著系统性偏差（systematic biases），亟需一种能容忍模型不完美、同时保持参数推断可靠性的方法。

Method: 提出一个半相干贝叶斯推理框架（semi-coherent Bayesian inference framework）：将数据分割为若干独立块，对各块进行相干分析（coherent analysis），再以非相干方式（incoherently）重组各块的后验结果。该方法将相位追踪限制在较短的块时长内，从而阻止相位误差的长期累积。实现为GPU加速的Python软件包SPLIT（Semi-coherent Posteriors for Long-Inspiral Templates）。

Result: 在含有环境效应的注入测试中，全相干真空广义相对论（vacuum-GR）分析的最大一维系统偏差约为4.8σ；而半相干方法的相应偏差被限制在≲0.5σ以内。半相干方法虽然损失了部分最优信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio, SNR），但参数精度获得大幅提升，整体上呈现高度有利的权衡。

Conclusion: 半相干方法以少量信噪比损失为代价，显著提高了对长时间引力波信号的参数推断精度，对于LISA及未来引力波探测器具有重要的实用价值。

Abstract: The Laser Interferometer Space Antenna (LISA) will detect gravitational waves (GWs) from dozens of extreme- and intermediate-mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs/IMRIs). These sources will stay in-band for months to years, offering extraordinary scientific potential. However, their fully phase-coherent analysis standard in current pipelines imposes stringent waveform accuracy requirements; failing to model the signal over such long durations can result in significant systematic biases. To address this, we formulate a robust semi-coherent Bayesian inference framework that segments the data into independent blocks, analyzes each block coherently, and recombines the results incoherently. By restricting phase-tracking to much shorter block durations, this approach prevents significant accumulation of phase errors. We implement this methodology in \textsc{SPLIT} (Semi-coherent Posteriors for Long-Inspiral Templates), a GPU-accelerated Python package. Applying \textsc{SPLIT} to an environment-rich injection, we demonstrate that while a fully-coherent vacuum-GR analysis incurs a maximum 1D systematic bias of $\approx 4.8σ$ from the truth, the shorter integration window of our semi-coherent approach restricts such biases to $\lesssim 0.5σ$. Overall, despite a fractional loss of optimal signal-to-noise ratio, the substantial improvement in parameter accuracy offered by the semi-coherent approach presents a highly advantageous trade-off for LISA and other future GW detectors.

</details>


### [83] [Constraints on regular black holes with nonminimally coupled electromagnetic fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13773)
*Ana Bokulić,Tajron Jurić,Luka Kanai Pejić,Filip Požar,Ivica Smolić*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 论文系统研究了包含三种典型的非最小耦合相互作用项（$R F_{ab}F^{ab}$、$R_{ab} F^a_{\ \, c} \, F^{bc}$ 和 $R_{abcd} F^{ab} F^{cd}$）的理论，这些项通常出现在低能有效拉格朗日量（low-energy effective Lagrangian）中。此外，还拓展考察了 $f(R,F_{ab}{\star F}^{ab})$ 形式的拉格朗日项。

Result: 证明了磁荷正则黑洞（magnetically charged regular black hole）在非最小耦合理论中被排除，除非耦合常数经过精细调谐（finely tuned）；并论证了类似结论对电荷正则黑洞（electrically charged regular black hole）同样成立。进一步表明，上述结论也适用于 $f(R,F_{ab}{\star F}^{ab})$ 形式的拉格朗日项。

Conclusion: 非最小耦合引力理论在避免奇点（singularity）方面面临严格限制，正则黑洞解的构建条件极为苛刻。

Abstract: Construction of physically realistic theories admitting regular black hole solutions remains an important open problem in gravitational physics. While theories with electromagnetic fields minimally coupled to gravity have been extensively studied over the past two decades, theories with nonminimal couplings remain comparatively unexplored. We investigate theories containing the interaction terms $R F_{ab}F^{ab}$, $R_{ab} F^a_{\ \, c} \, F^{bc}$ and $R_{abcd} F^{ab} F^{cd}$, which generically arise in low-energy effective Lagrangians. We prove that magnetically charged regular black holes are excluded, except possibly for finely tuned choices of coupling constants, and argue that a similar conclusion applies to electrically charged regular black holes. We further show that similar conclusions hold for Lagrangian terms of the form $f(R,F_{ab}{\star F}^{ab})$.

### [84] [Relativistic and Newtonian Proca Stars: A Tale of Two Limits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13785)
*Alberto Diez-Tejedor,Carlos Herdeiro,Claudio Lazarte,Eugen Radu,Armando A. Roque,Nicolas Sanchis-Gual,Etevaldo dos Santos Costa Filho*

TL;DR: 本文研究了爱因斯坦-普罗卡理论（Einstein-Proca theory）在牛顿极限下的静态孤立子解，建立了与自旋-1薛定谔-泊松系统（spin-1 Schrödinger-Poisson system）之间的映射，发现非相对论区域支持比相对论理论更丰富的稳定平衡构型谱，包括稳定的激发态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究表明爱因斯坦-克莱因-戈登系统（Einstein-Klein-Gordon system）在牛顿极限下可映射到薛定谔-泊松系统，但对于矢量场（vector field）情形，由于普罗卡场（Proca field）的矢量性质与非相对论自旋-1区域的增强U(3)对称性，这种对应关系更加复杂，需要系统澄清。

Method: 在牛顿极限（场频率趋近于粒子质量，ω→μ）下，分析爱因斯坦-普罗卡理论的一组代表性静态孤立子解，并与自旋-1薛定谔-泊松系统的对应解进行对比，通过识别ℓ=0电普罗卡星（electric Proca stars）为径向极化（hedgehog）构型、ℓ=1电普罗卡星为线性极化构型，建立两种描述之间的映射。

Result: 建立了相对论与非相对论描述之间的系统映射关系，澄清了基态的若干特征，并解决了相对论与牛顿解在形态学和稳定性方面的若干明显不一致之处。发现非相对论区域支持比相对论理论更丰富的稳定平衡构型谱，包括稳定的激发态。

Conclusion: 非相对论自旋-1区域拥有更丰富的稳定平衡构型谱，这源于增强的U(3)对称性，表明牛顿极限下的有效描述能够揭示相对论理论中不存在的稳定激发态结构。

Abstract: We investigate a representative set of static solitonic solutions of the Einstein-Proca theory in the Newtonian regime, where the field frequency approaches the particle mass, $ω\to μ$, and compare them with the corresponding solutions of the spin-1 Schrödinger-Poisson system, which provides the effective description in this limit. While this correspondence is relatively straightforward in the Einstein-Klein-Gordon case, the vector nature of the Proca field, combined with the enhanced $U(3)$ symmetry of the nonrelativistic spin-1 regime, gives rise to several nontrivial features that require careful analysis. We establish a mapping between the two descriptions by identifying $\ell=0$ electric Proca stars with radially polarized (hedgehog) configurations and $\ell=1$ electric Proca stars with linearly polarized configurations. We further clarify some aspects of the ground state and resolve several apparent discrepancies between relativistic and Newtonian solutions, particularly concerning their morphology and stability properties. An important conclusion of this work is that the nonrelativistic regime supports a richer spectrum of stable equilibrium configurations than the relativistic theory, including stable excited states.

### [85] [Universality in the Transition from Inspiral to Plunge: High-Accuracy Analytic Solutions and Catastrophe Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13786)
*Ariadna Ribes Metidieri,Béatrice Bonga,Badri Krishnan,José Luis Jaramillo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文从突变论（catastrophe theory）视角重新审视极端质量比旋近（extreme mass-ratio inspiral）中从旋近到坠入的过渡过程，揭示了倾斜轨道下过渡动力学仍然受Painlevé I方程支配的内在数学结构，并将Kerr时空径向有效势的平衡结构与突变论中的折叠突变及尖点突变联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先分析由准圆形旋近缓慢演化的物理边界条件所选择的Painlevé I方程解，论证该解唯一对应tritronquée解；随后将tritronquée解的高精度解析近似与直接数值积分结果进行比较。第二部分展示了Kerr径向有效势的平衡结构可借助突变论自然解释，赤道轨道对应折叠突变（fold catastrophe），倾斜轨道对应尖点突变（cusp catastrophe）。

Result: 物理边界条件唯一地选择了Painlevé I方程的tritronquée解；解析近似与数值积分精度相当，且在微分和积分下稳定性更优。突变论分析表明，赤道轨道和倾斜轨道分别对应折叠突变与尖点突变，坠入过渡对应于在突变流形（catastrophe manifold）上沿折叠线的缓慢演化。

Conclusion: 突变论为过渡动力学的Painlevé I方程的普适出现提供了几何解释，揭示了Kerr时空中不同倾角轨道在旋近-坠入过渡阶段共享的统一数学结构。

Abstract: We revisit the transition from inspiral to plunge for extreme mass-ratio inspirals on quasi-circular, inclined orbits in Kerr spacetime from the perspective of catastrophe theory. Our goal is to uncover the mathematical structures underlying the universality of the transition dynamics, which remains governed by the same Painlevé I differential equation as for equatorial inspirals despite the additional complexity. We first analyze the solution of the Painlevé I equation selected by the physical boundary conditions of slowly evolving quasi-circular inspiral at early times. We argue that these conditions uniquely select the tritronquée solution of Painlevé I. We then compare existing high-accuracy analytic approximations of the tritronquée solution with direct numerical integrations of the Painlevé I equation, finding comparable accuracy and improved stability under differentiation and integration for the analytic solution. In the second part of this work, we show that the equilibrium structure of the Kerr radial effective potential admits a natural interpretation in terms of catastrophe theory. Equatorial orbits are associated with the fold catastrophe, while inclined orbits are described by the cusp catastrophe. In both cases, the transition to plunge corresponds to slow evolution across fold lines of the catastrophe manifold, providing a geometric explanation for the universal appearance of the Painlevé I equation in the transition dynamics.

### [86] [Mode decomposition methods for the analysis of black hole ringdown signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13851)
*Andrzej Krolak,Massimo Tinto*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了经验模态分解（EMD）和变分模态分解（VMD）在双黑洞并合后引力波信号环振阶段分析中的适用性，通过蒙特卡洛模拟评估了两种方法分离双拟正则模（QNM）及估计其频率的能力，结果表明VMD能提供显著更准确的频率估计，并引入了一种改进的瞬时频率估计器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用经验模态分解（Empirical Mode Decomposition, EMD）和变分模态分解（Variational Mode Decomposition, VMD）分析并合后引力波信号；通过包含成对QNM的含噪环振信号的蒙特卡洛模拟，评估两种方法分离双模并估计频率的能力；瞬时频率通过希尔伯特变换（Hilbert transform, HT）及新提出的瞬时频率与振幅确定法（instantaneous frequency and amplitude determination, IFAD）获取。

Result: EMD和VMD均能解析多个模态，VMD在频率估计精度上显著优于EMD；提出的改进瞬时频率估计器相比希尔伯特变换提高了精度；研究量化了双模可分辨的条件，揭示了模态频率间隔过近和信号持续时间短所造成的限制。

Conclusion: 这些结果对当前观测以及未来天基和下一代地基探测器预期的高信噪比探测具有参考价值，明确了多模分辨的可行条件与局限性。

Abstract: The ringdown phase of a binary black hole merger encodes fundamental information about the remnant through its quasinormal mode (QNM) spectrum. Extracting multiple modes from gravitational-wave data is essential for black-hole spectroscopy but remains challenging due to the short duration of the signal, limited signal-to-noise ratio (SNR), and interference between modes. In this work, we investigate the applicability of Empirical Mode Decomposition (EMD) and Variational Mode Decomposition (VMD) to the analysis of post-merger gravitational-wave signals. Using Monte Carlo simulations of noisy ringdown signals composed of pairs of QNMs, we assessed the ability of these methods to separate the two modes and estimate their frequencies. The instantaneous frequency is obtained via the Hilbert transform (HT) and our new proposed method, named instantaneous frequency and amplitude determination (IFAD). We analyze performance over a wide range of SNR values relevant to current and future gravitational-wave detectors. Our results show that both EMD and VMD can resolve multiple modes, and VMD provides significantly more accurate frequency estimates. We also introduce a modified instantaneous frequency estimator that improves accuracy over the Hilbert transform. The study quantifies the conditions under which two-mode resolution is feasible and highlights the limitations imposed by closely spaced mode frequencies and short signal duration. These results are relevant for current observations and for future high-SNR detections expected from space-based and next-generation ground detectors.

### [87] [Black hole physics within $f(R)$ gravity: Quasi-normal spectra and greybody factors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13926)
*Ángel Rincón,Grigoris Panotopoulos*

TL;DR: 本文在 $f(R)$ 引力框架下，研究了一个四维黑洞解的天体物理相关性质。该解通过单一额外参数 $\alpha$ 偏离广义相对论。作者利用三种独立方法（六阶WKB半解析法、解析表达式、eikonal极限解析式）分析了无质量标量扰动的拟正规模（quasinormal modes），并在WKB近似下计算了灰体因子（greybody factors），研究了参数 $\alpha$、泛音数 $n$ 和多重极数 $\ell$ 对拟正规频率实部与虚部的影响，以及这些参数对灰体因子、吸收截面、反射系数和透射系数的影响。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用三种独立方法研究无质量标量扰动的拟正规模：第六阶WKB（Wentzel-Kramers-Brillouin）半解析方法（sixth-order WKB semi-analytic method）、解析表达式（analytic expressions）以及eikonal极限（eikonal limit）下的解析表达式。灰体因子在WKB近似下计算。

Abstract: We investigate several astrophysical motivated properties of a four-dimensional black hole solution in the framework of $f(R)$ gravity. The model is characterized by a single additional parameter, $α$, which encodes nontrivial deviations from General Relativity. Using this black hole spacetime as the background geometry, we analyze: (i) the quasinormal modes of massless scalar perturbations (employing several complementary methods), and (ii) the greybody factors associated to the propagation of massless test scalar fields. Regarding quasinormal modes, we study the response of black holes to massless scalar perturbations using three independent approaches: the well-established sixth-order WKB semi-analytic method, analytic expressions, and the analytical expression in the eikonal limit. We examine the behavior of both the real and imaginary parts of the quasinormal frequencies as functions of the parameter $α$, the overtone number $n$, and the multipole number $\ell$. In addition to that, we compute the greybody factors within the WKB approximation for various combinations of the relevant parameters. In particular, we focus on the propagation of test massless scalar fields and investigate how the greybody factors depend on the multipole number $\ell$, and the free parameter $α$. The impact of the aforementioned parameters on the absorption cross-section and the reflection and transmission coefficients is studied in detail.

### [88] [Binary Black Hole Parameter Estimation with Hybrid CNN-Transformer Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13941)
*Panagiotis N. Sakellariou,Spiros V. Georgakopoulos,Sotiris Tasoulis,Vassilis P. Plagianakos*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统引力波信号检测依赖基于模板的匹配滤波（matched filtering）与多探测器符合分析（coincidence analysis），而近年来机器学习（Machine Learning）与深度学习（Deep Learning）的进展为信号检测和参数估计（parameter estimation）提供了新的可能性，促使研究者探索更高效的深度学习方法。

Method: 采用混合深度学习策略，将Transformer编码器与成熟的卷积神经网络架构相结合，以估计非进动双黑洞系统的内在参数（intrinsic parameters）与外在参数（extrinsic parameters）。研究对象为点估计，即为每个参数输出单一最佳拟合值（single best-fit values），而非完整的后验分布（posterior distributions）。

Result: 该方法在嵌入高斯噪声（Gaussian noise）的模拟信号以及真实引力波事件上进行了评估，在关键天体物理参数（astrophysical parameters）上展现出强大的预测性能和鲁棒性（robustness）。

Conclusion: 混合深度学习策略能够在引力波参数估计任务中实现有效的点估计，表明Transformer与卷积神经网络的组合架构在引力波数据分析中具有应用潜力。

Abstract: The detection of gravitational waves has revolutionized our ability to explore fundamental aspects of the Universe. Traditionally, modeled gravitational-wave signals have been identified using template-based matched filtering, followed by coincidence analysis across multiple detectors in the signal-to-noise ratio time series. Recent advances in Machine Learning and Deep Learning have sparked growing interest in their application to both signal detection and parameter estimation. In this study, a hybrid Deep Learning strategy is proposed that leverages the effectiveness of Transformer encoders alongside well-established Convolutional Neural Network architectures in an attempt to estimate the intrinsic and extrinsic parameters of non-precessing binary black hole systems. The primary focus of this work is point estimation, producing single best-fit values for each parameter rather than full posterior distributions. This method is evaluated on both simulated signals embedded in Gaussian noise and real gravitational-wave events, and it demonstrates strong predictive performance and robustness across key astrophysical parameters.

</details>


### [89] [A theory agnostic uniqueness theorem for the Kerr solution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14076)
*Joshua Baines*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在仅依赖对称性论证与渐近条件下，无需预设爱因斯坦方程（Einstein equations）的有效性，证明了克尔解（Kerr solution）的唯一性。该结果对量子引力和修改引力理论具有重要启示，并与彭罗斯奇点定理（Penrose's singularity theorem）互补。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 成功建立了理论无关的克尔时空唯一性定理。研究还表明，即使在不需要预设爱因斯坦方程有效性的情况下，奇点（singularities）仍可能是不可避免的。

Conclusion: 该定理对旨在消除时空奇点行为的量子引力理论或修改引力理论具有重要参考价值。同时，本工作与彭罗斯奇点定理形成互补关系，拓展了奇点不可避免性结论的适用范围。

Abstract: In this paper, we show that under a suitable set of symmetry arguments and asymptotic conditions, the uniqueness of the Kerr solution can be proven. None of the conditions considered herein explicitly assume the validity of the Einstein equations. Hence, we are able to construct a theory agnostic uniqueness theorem for the Kerr spacetime. This result has implications for theories of quantum gravity or modified theories of gravity which wish to excise singular behaviour from their corresponding spacetimes. Furthermore, this work is complimentary to Penrose's singularity theorem. While the spacetime considered herein is not as general as that assumed by Penrose, we show that singularities can be unavoidable even when the validity of the Einstein equations is not presupposed.

### [90] [Refocusing of Wheeler--DeWitt wave functions at inner horizons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14126)
*Takeshi Chiba,Keiju Murata,Daiki Saito*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨量子引力效应对黑洞内视界（inner horizon）结构的影响，特别是内视界在量子理论中是否仍能形成。

Method: 在微超空间（minisuperspace）近似下求解Wheeler-DeWitt (WDW)方程；针对方程中有效势为负的“快子区域”（tachyonic region）发展了一套数值演化方法，确保波函数在该区域稳定传播。

Result: 当量子引力参数κ较小时，波包沿经典轨迹传播且展宽微弱；κ增大时展宽显著增强。然而，初始态若局域在外视界附近，波包在内视界附近会重新局域化，即发生“再聚焦”现象。

Conclusion: 内视界附近的几何若在外视界附近是经典的，则在内视界附近也会恢复经典性；微超空间近似下，量子引力效应并不阻碍内视界的形成。

Abstract: We study quantum gravitational effects inside hyperbolic black holes with both outer and inner horizons by solving the Wheeler--DeWitt (WDW) equation in the minisuperspace approximation. The WDW equation contains a tachyonic region where the effective potential becomes negative. We develop a numerical method that consistently evolves the wave function across this region and obtain stable solutions throughout the entire minisuperspace. For small values of the parameter $κ$, which controls the strength of quantum gravitational effects, the wave packet propagates along the classical trajectory with only mild quantum spreading. As $κ$ increases, enhanced quantum effects lead to significant spreading of the wave packet during its propagation. Nevertheless, when the initial state is localized near the outer horizon, the wave packet becomes localized again in the vicinity of the inner horizon. We refer to this recovery of localization as a refocusing phenomenon. This result suggests that, if the geometry is classical near the outer horizon, it becomes classical again near the inner horizon. Within the minisuperspace approximation, inner-horizon formation is not obstructed by quantum gravitational effects.

### [91] [Note on the local calculation of decoherence of quantum superposition in the static black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14178)
*Ran Li,Zhong-Xiao Man,Jin Wang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文研究Schwarzschild和Reissner-Nordström黑洞中静态粒子量子空间叠加的退相干（decoherence）机制，通过Danielson-Satishchandran-Wald (DSW)思想实验的相干态（coherent state）重新表述，发现退相干行为依赖于环境场的量子态：Boulware真空下静态叠加退相干为零，而Unruh和Hartle-Hawking真空中 Hawking辐射的热效应可诱发非零退相干。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将粒子视为局域经典源（localized classical source）耦合到量子标量场，通过相干态生成（coherent state generation）重新表述DSW思想实验中的退相干过程；利用Wightman函数（Wightman function）导出退相干泛函的局域表达式；采用渐近匹配方法（asymptotic matching method）计算Boulware、Unruh和Hartle-Hawking三种真空态下Wightman函数的解析表达式。

Result: 在长时间极限下，退相干率由Wightman函数的低频行为决定。Boulware真空下静态叠加的退相干为零；Unruh和Hartle-Hawking真空中，与Hawking辐射相关的热效应可诱导出非零的退相干。

Conclusion: 退相干行为强烈依赖于环境量子场的态：Boulware真空（无热效应）不产生退相干，而Unruh和Hartle-Hawking真空（包含Hawking辐射的热效应）可导致非零退相干，表明黑洞背景下的热效应是诱导量子叠加退相干的物理起源。

Abstract: We investigate the decoherence of a quantum spatial superposition of a static particle in Schwarzschild and Reissner-Nordström black holes. By treating the particle as a localized classical source coupled to a quantum scalar field, we reformulate the decoherence process in the Danielson-Satishchandran-Wald (DSW) gedankenexperiment through coherent state generation and derive the local expression for the decoherence functional in terms of the Wightman function. In the long-time limit, the decoherence rate is shown to be characterized by the low-frequency behavior of the Wightman function. We then employ the asymptotic matching method to calculate the analytical expressions of the Wightman functions in the Boulware, Unruh, and Hartle-Hawking vacua. We show that the decoherence behavior depends on the quantum state of the environmental field. While the Boulware vacuum gives vanishing decoherence for a static superposition, the thermal effects associated with Hawking radiation in the Unruh and Hartle-Hawking vacua can induce nonvanishing decoherence.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Takagi分解（Takagi factorization）来解耦矩阵场方程，分析中微子在精确引力夹层波背景中的传播动力学。

Result: 局域脉冲（localized pulse）打破了质量本征态（mass eigenstates）在波区传播时的运动学对齐（kinematic alignment），在波前横向轮廓（transverse profile of the wavefront）上留下永久的残余相位偏移（residual phase shift）。波不对称性（wave asymmetry）直接耦合到马约拉纳自旋张量（Majorana spin tensor），迫使中微子从左旋（left-handed）过渡到右旋（right-handed）构型。波尾（wave tail）后，残余漂移参数（residual drift parameters）会极化中微子的手性（chirality），在横向动量平面（transverse momentum plane）引入强烈的各向异性（anisotropy）。

Conclusion: 经过的引力波会同时修改中微子束的味和手性，这是引力记忆效应的一个可观测信号。

Abstract: We present the propagation of massive Majorana neutrinos crossing an exact gravitational sandwich wave background. By employing a Takagi factorization to decouple the matrix field equations, We show that the localized pulse breaks the kinematic alignment of the mass eigenstates as they propagate through the wave zone, leaving a permanent residual phase shift across the transverse profile of the wavefront. The wave asymmetry couples directly to the Majorana spin tensor, forcing a transition from left-handed to right-handed configurations. Behind the wave tail, the residual drift parameters act to polarize the state's chirality, introducing a strong anisotropy across the transverse momentum plane. These results show that a passing gravitational wave leaves a modification on both the flavor and helicity of a neutrino beam, as a sign of the gravitational memory effect.

Result: 当引力波背景的能量密度参数Ω_GW ≥ 10^{-10}时，萨克斯-沃尔夫效应会在引力波背景中产生可探测的各向异性（anisotropies）和谱畸变（spectral distortions），且该效应在高频段尤为显著。

Abstract: The Sachs-Wolfe (SW) effect, arising from large-scale structures in the universe, modifies the frequencies of gravitational waves (GWs) sourced by a cosmological background. We show that for backgrounds with $Ω_{\rm GW}\gtrsim 10^{-10}$, this effect imprints anisotropies and spectral distortions that can be detectable with a network of space-based interferometers (such as LISA + Taiji) and, if not taken into account, may bias the estimate of the theoretical model of the GW background. The effect is particularly enhanced in the high-frequency end of the spectrum. The SW-induced anisotropies and spectral distortions present in a GW background sourced at primordial times will correlate with the SW signature present in the CMB. Any detection of a cross-correlation between the GW anisotropies and the CMB at large scales is therefore a smoking gun for confirming the primordial nature of the background.

### [94] [Dynamical tidal response of neutron stars via scattering amplitudes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14405)
*M. V. S. Saketh,Suprovo Ghosh,Nils Andersson*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在世界线有效场论（worldline EFT）框架下系统定义了中子星的动力学潮汐响应（dynamical tidal response），通过将散射振幅计算与恒星微扰论（stellar perturbation theory）匹配，得到了与静态极限、共振模式行为以及引力波耗散效应一致的结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波物理学的一个关键挑战是区分双星并合中致密天体的性质（特别是中子星与黑洞）。中子星的潮汐响应（tidal response）与其内部高密度物质物理及物态方程（equation of state）密切相关，但广义相对论中定义潮汐响应存在坐标模糊性以及连接双星动力学和引力波波形的复杂性。

Method: 在世界线有效场论框架下，将动力学潮汐响应问题转化为孤立中子星的引力波散射（gravitational-wave scattering）问题；分别在该EFT中使用量子场论技术以及在恒星微扰论（紫外理论）中求解广义相对论下的度规和物质扰动方程，并与外部区域的解析Mano-Suzuki-Takasugi（MST）解进行匹配，从而得到动力学潮汐响应。

Result: 匹配得到的动力学潮汐响应与已知预期一致，包括静态极限（static limit）行为、中子星共振模式（resonant modes）附近的行为，以及由引力波耗散（gravitational-wave dissipation）诱导的主导振荡模式的虚部。

Abstract: A key challenge of gravitational-wave physics is distinguishing the nature of compact objects involved in binary coalescences, particularly whether they are black holes or neutron stars. Neutron stars are distinguished from black holes by a stronger tidal response, with both static and dynamical aspects directly linked to their rich internal physics. Measurements of the tidal response through gravitational observations constrains the neutron-star equation of state and provides insight into the physics of high-density matter. However, defining the tidal response of neutron stars in general relativity is challenging due to coordinate ambiguities and the complexity of connecting the star's response to binary dynamics and the associated gravitational waveforms. In this paper, we show how the dynamical tidal response of a neutron star can be systematically defined within the worldline effective field theory (EFT) framework, connecting the problem to gravitational-wave scattering off an isolated neutron star. These scattering amplitudes are computed both within the EFT, using standard quantum field-theory techniques, and within stellar perturbation theory (the corresponding ultraviolet theory), where the coupled metric and matter perturbation equations are solved in the stellar interior within general relativity and matched to the analytical Mano-Suzuki-Takasugi (MST) solutions in the exterior. We match the scattering amplitude between effective theory and the ultraviolet theory to obtain the dynamical tidal response. We show the result to be consistent with known expectations, such as the static limit and the behaviour near the neutron star's resonant modes, while also recovering the imaginary part of the dominant oscillation mode induced by gravitational-wave dissipation. We conclude with a discussion of potential future improvements within both the EFT and the perturbation theory.

Method: 采用Mathisson-Papapetrou-Dixon方程（MPD方程）描述自旋测试粒子的运动；利用时空对称性（symmetries of the spacetime）简化并求解运动方程，得到一般精确解；进一步分析了径向运动和平面运动等特例。

Result: 粒子的轨迹、动量和自旋可以用关于极角和方位角的三个特定函数完全表达；证明了该动力学系统是完全可积的（completely integrable）；获得了粒子的一般非测地线轨迹（non-geodesic trajectory），并与无自旋粒子的测地线运动进行了比较。

Conclusion: 自旋导致粒子偏离测地线（geodesic）运动，且全局单极子时空中的自旋粒子动力学可以通过解析方法被完整描述；径向和平面运动的特例进一步揭示了自旋效应与时空拓扑缺陷的耦合机制。

Abstract: We investigate the motion of spinning test particles in the spacetime of a global monopole in the framework of the Mathisson-Papapetrou-Dixon equations. By making use of the symmetries of the spacetime, we obtain a general exact solution to the equations of motion. We show that the particle's trajectories, momenta, and spin can be expressed in terms of three specific functions of the polar and azimuthal angles. We also show that the system is completely integrable. We obtain the general non-geodesic trajectory of the particle, and also examine the particular cases of radial and planar motion. We compare the non-geodesic trajectories of a spinning particle with a non-spinning particle.

To this end, we derive an extended equation of state by using the nonrelativistic self-consistent Hartree-Fock-Bogoliubov theory and the hydrodynamic approach. The solutions of the obtained equations of state show that the key parameters of the dark matter halos such as the density, mass, and radius are sensitive to the interspecies interaction and to the quantum fluctuation strength. The stability and the dynamical evolution of the droplet Galactic halos are analyzed by considering small perturbations of the quantum hydrodynamical equations. ### [97] [Searching for Extra Dimensions with Gravitational Waves: Dark-Siren Constraints from GWTC-4](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14549)
*Anson Chen,Jun Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用GWTC-4目录中的暗汽笛（dark-siren）方法和GLADE+星系目录，对高维引力波传播（higher-dimensional GW propagation）进行了层次贝叶斯分析（hierarchical Bayesian analysis），得到额外维度数D=4.38^{+1.91}_{-1.01}（68%置信区间），结果表明当前观测数据与四维广义相对论（General Relativity）一致，且交叉尺度（crossover scale）R_c的约束较差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高维引力理论预言引力波（gravitational waves, GWs）可传播至额外空间维度（extra spatial dimensions），导致振幅在宇宙学尺度上出现修正性衰减。因此，通过测量引力波光度距离（luminosity distance）可以检验时空维数，为探测额外维度提供了独特的探针。

Method: 采用源自膜世界（braneworld）场景的现象学参数化方案，由时空维数D和交叉尺度R_c表征对广义相对论（General Relativity）的偏离。利用GWTC-4目录中141个致密双星并合事件（compact binary coalescences）与GLADE+星系目录的视线方向星系信息，进行层次贝叶斯分析（hierarchical Bayesian analysis）。

Result: 在H_0∈[65,77] km s⁻¹Mpc⁻¹和log(R_c/Mpc)∈[2.7,4.0]的先验下，得到D=4.38^{+1.91}_{-1.01}（68%置信区间）。R_c的后验分布累积在先验上限附近，表明交叉尺度受到当前观测数据的弱约束。D的推断结果对R_c的先验范围敏感。

Conclusion: 本研究提供了GWTC-4暗汽笛方法对高维引力波传播的首个约束，结果表明当前观测与四维广义相对论（General Relativity）一致，额外维度尚未得到显著证据支持。

Abstract: Higher-dimensional theories of gravity predict that gravitational waves (GWs) can propagate into extra spatial dimensions, leading to modified amplitude damping over cosmological distances. Measurements of GW luminosity distances therefore provide a unique probe of the dimensionality of spacetime. In this work, we constrain higher-dimensional GW propagation using the dark-siren method with the Gravitational-Wave Transient Catalog 4.0 (GWTC-4). We adopt a phenomenological parameterization motivated by braneworld scenarios, in which deviations from General Relativity are characterized by the spacetime dimension number $D$ and a crossover scale $R_c$ governing the transition between four- and higher-dimensional gravity. We perform a hierarchical Bayesian analysis combining 141 compact binary coalescences from GWTC-4 with line-of-sight galaxy information from the GLADE+ catalog. For a prior $H_0 \in [65,77]\ {\rm km~s^{-1}Mpc^{-1}}$ and $\log(R_c/{\rm Mpc}) \in [2.7,4.0]$, we obtain $D = 4.38^{+1.91}_{-1.01}$ (68\% credible interval). We also find that the inferred posterior distribution of $R_c$ accumulates near the upper prior boundary, indicating that the crossover scale remains poorly constrained by current observations. We further show that the inferred constraint on $D$ depends sensitively on the assumed prior range of $R_c$, which determines the characteristic distance scale at which deviations from General Relativity become significant. Our results provide the first GWTC-4 dark-siren constraints on higher-dimensional GW propagation and demonstrate that current observations remain consistent with four-dimensional General Relativity.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.dis-nn'></div>

# cond-mat.dis-nn [[Back]](#toc)

### [98] [Direct/adaptive-mixture phase-gradient learning for neural-network quantum states with complex phase structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13912)
*Yi-Ran Xue,Rui Wang,Baigeng Wang,Chenan Wei*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文指出神经量子态（NQS）在优化含非平凡符号或复相结构的基态时存在脆弱性问题，其根源在于相位梯度的随机估计器而非网络表达能力。提出一种基于局域能量直接微分的直接估计器（direct estimator），具有更低的方差且无偏，结合振幅-相位分离的变分ansatz，在100位点通量梯子模型中达到0.89%的中位误差，显著优于标准估计器。进一步推广到手性XXX链，并引入自适应混合估计器，证明其方差不会劣于最优混合系数下的较好端，种子诊断显示大部分增益源于消除了失败运行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经量子态（neural-network quantum states, NQS）在量子多体变分计算中效果显著，但当基态带有非平凡符号或复相位结构时（常见于规范场、时间反演对称性破缺和费米统计），其优化过程非常脆弱。现有研究多将问题归因于网络表达能力，本文则试图揭示其真正根源在于相位梯度的随机估计器，并设计更优的估计方案。

Method: 本文指出标准相位梯度估计是蒙特卡罗能量梯度中的有噪得分函数估计器（score-function estimator）；作为替代，通过直接对局域能量（local energy）求微分得到直接估计器（direct estimator），该估计量对同一相位力无偏且方差显著更低，但要求采用振幅-相位分离（amplitude–phase separated）的变分ansatz。进一步提出两种估计器的自适应混合（adaptive-mixture）方案。

Result: 在100位点通量梯子（flux ladder）模型中，采用直接估计器的小型网络达到0.89%中位误差，而调优后的标准基线停留在1.8%，更宽或更深的标准梯度网络误差从8.4%恶化至24.6%。在手性XXX链（chiral XXX chain）中，直接估计器同样收敛到显著更低的误差，且优势随通量增大、在零通量对照中消失。自适应混合估计器的方差在最优混合系数下不劣于较好的单一端，种子诊断表明大部分增益来自消除失败运行。

Conclusion: 估计器设计（estimator design）成为处理复值神经量子态（complex-valued NQS）的一项首要杠杆，表明通过改进梯度估计而非单纯增加网络容量即可大幅提升变分优化性能。

Abstract: Neural-network quantum states (NQS) are a leading variational tool for quantum many-body physics, yet their optimization is fragile whenever the ground state carries a non-trivial sign or complex phase structure, a situation generic to gauge fields, broken time-reversal symmetry, and fermionic statistics. We trace this fragility to the stochastic estimator of the phase gradient rather than to network expressiveness. The phase sector of the Monte Carlo energy gradient is a noisy score-function estimator; differentiating the local energy instead yields a direct estimator that is unbiased for the same phase force, has far lower variance, and requires only a separated amplitude--phase ansatz. Demonstrated on a 100-site flux ladder, a small network trained this way reaches $0.89\%$ median error, where tuned standard baselines plateau at $1.8\%$ and wider or deeper standard-gradient networks degrade from $8.4\%$ to $24.6\%$. The advantage carries over to chiral XXX chains: the direct estimator again converges to a markedly lower error than the standard one, across $α$ and size; it grows with flux and vanishes in zero-flux controls. An adaptive-mixture of the two estimators is provably never worse in variance than the better endpoint at the optimal mixing coefficient, with seed-resolved diagnostics tracing much of the gain to eliminating failed runs. Estimator design thus emerges as a first-class lever for complex-valued neural quantum states.

</details>


### [99] [Local Coverage Governs Memorization in Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14390)
*Claudia Merger,Sebastian Goldt*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文通过建立扩散模型（diffusion model）与核密度估计（kernel density estimation, KDE）之间的联系，推导出一个理论判据，证明记忆化（memorization）由局部数据覆盖率（local data coverage）决定：低覆盖区域中的孤立训练样本容易被记忆，而高密度区域则支持插值与泛化。实验验证了局部稀疏性（local sparsity）增加记忆化，并在多类设置中发现类内稀疏性更高的类别记忆更强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散模型中的记忆化通常被视为模型或数据集的全局属性，但实践中同一模型可同时生成记忆化样本和新颖样本，因此需要回答哪些训练样本最可能被记忆，即从局部视角理解记忆化发生的条件。

Method: 利用扩散模型与核密度估计之间的理论联系，推导出一个基于训练数据在邻域中的密度和数据集大小的理论判据，用于预测一个点是否被记忆化；在高维极限下该判据呈现尖锐的局部相变。

Result: 低覆盖率区域中的孤立训练样本被记忆化，而高密度区域则支持插值与泛化；记忆化程度随局部稀疏性增加而上升；同一扩散模型内同时存在记忆化和新颖样本；多类设置中类内稀疏性较高的类别记忆化更强。

Conclusion: 记忆化由局部数据覆盖率主导，提供了一个基于数据几何（data geometry）的局部视角，解释了扩散模型中记忆化何时、何处发生。

Abstract: Memorization in diffusion models is often treated as a global property of the model or dataset. In practice, however, a single diffusion model can simultaneously generate both memorized and novel samples. Which training samples are most likely to be memorized? In this work, we show that memorization is governed by \emph{local data coverage}. Leveraging the connection between diffusion models and kernel density estimation (KDE), we derive a theoretical criterion that predicts whether a point is memorized based on the density of training data in its neighborhood and the size of the training dataset. In the high-dimensional limit, this leads to a sharp, local transition: regions of low coverage are dominated by isolated training samples, which are memorized, while dense regions support interpolation and generalization. We validate these predictions empirically, showing that memorization increases with local sparsity and that diffusion models exhibit a coexistence of memorized and novel samples within the same model. Extending this framework to multi-class settings, we further show that classes with higher intra-class sparsity (and thus lower local coverage) are more strongly memorized. Our results provide a local view of memorization in diffusion models, explaining when and where memorization occurs in terms of data geometry.

</details>

### [100] [Digital programming of spin correlations in a fermionic lattice quantum simulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13772)
*Yann Kiefer,Lars Fischer,Zijie Zhu,Konrad Viebahn,Tilman Esslinger*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出一种混合方法，将模拟量子制备与数字量子门协议相结合，从同一初始资源态工程化具有特定长程自旋关联的目标态，并通过碰撞门对绝热制备并过滤的四费米子单重态链进行编程，实现了包括海森堡链在内的多种自旋关联模式，为强关联物质态的目标制备铺平了道路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的模拟量子仿真（analog quantum simulation）在初始态制备上局限于热系综（thermal ensembles）或无关联乘积态（uncorrelated product states），限制了可研究的量子多体现象范围。因此需要一种更灵活的目标态制备方法。

Method: 提出一种混合（hybrid）方法，将模拟量子系统（analog quantum system）的绝热制备与过滤过程，与基于数字量子门（digital quantum-gate）协议相结合。通过施加碰撞门（collisional gates）对预先制备并过滤的四费米子单重态链（four-fermion singlet chains）进行编程，从而构建具有不同自旋关联模式的目标态。

Result: 成功编程出多种自旋关联模式，包括海森堡链（Heisenberg chain）的自旋关联。通过一系列量子门操作结合单重态对测量（singlet-pair measurements），实现了对自旋关联（spin correlations）的测量。

Conclusion: 该方法为制备具有特定长程自旋关联的强关联物质态（strongly correlated states of matter）提供了可行途径，拓展了模拟量子仿真的初始态制备能力。

Abstract: Analog quantum simulation provides a highly controlled platform to study diverse quantum many-body phenomena. However, current methods for state initialisation are limited to thermal ensembles or uncorrelated product states. Here we present a hybrid approach that complements analog preparation with a digital quantum-gate protocol. This approach enables the engineering of target states with specific, long-range spin-correlations from the same initial resource state. By applying collisional gates to adiabatically prepared and filtered four-fermion singlet chains, we program diverse spin-correlation patterns, including that of a Heisenberg chain. We measure the spin correlations using a sequence of quantum gates followed by singlet-pair measurements. Our method paves the way to the targeted preparation of strongly correlated states of matter.

### [101] [Fermi gas of polar molecules in the Pauli-blocked regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14135)
*Junyu Lin,Annette N. Carroll,Phillip Martin,Calder Miller,Reuben R. W. Wang,Kevin Xu,John L. Bohn,Tim de Jongh,Jun Ye*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本论文通过偶极碰撞（dipolar collisions）在三维（3D）和准二维（quasi-2D）约束几何中成功将费米子KRb分子蒸发冷却至远低于费米温度（Fermi temperature），首次独立测量了泡利抑制（Pauli suppression）对弹性碰撞的效应，并发现泡利阻塞（Pauli blockade）限制了蒸发效率，最终温度约为费米温度（Fermi temperature）的25%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极性分子（polar molecules）量子气体为探索奇异多体动力学（many-body dynamics）和关联量子行为（correlated quantum behavior）提供了强大平台，但实现该平台的潜力需要能够在任意约束几何中制备高度简并（deeply degenerate）的分子量子气体。

Method: 利用偶极碰撞（dipolar collisions）在三维简谐势阱以及单层和双层二维（2D）构型中对费米子KRb分子进行蒸发冷却（evaporative cooling），并通过测量泡利抑制（Pauli suppression）对弹性碰撞的影响独立验证了泡利阻塞（Pauli-blocked）区域的存在。

Result: 在三维和准二维几何中，分子均被蒸发冷却至远低于费米温度，最终温度约为费米温度的25%。首次独立测量到极性分子在简并区域中的泡利抑制弹性碰撞效应。在准二维蒸发中，泡利阻塞大幅降低了原本很大的弹性与非弹性散射比（elastic to inelastic scattering ratio），从而限制了冷却效率。

Conclusion: 该工作实现了极性分子在三维和二维构型中的简并费米气体（degenerate Fermi gas）制备，揭示了泡利不相容原理（Pauli-exclusion principle）对分子费米气体蒸发冷却的基本限制，并指出未来可通过引入可区分散射伙伴（distinguishable scattering partners）来克服这一限制。

Abstract: Quantum gases of polar molecules have recently emerged as a powerful platform for exploring exotic many-body dynamics and correlated quantum behavior. To achieve the full potential of this platform, the production of deeply degenerate quantum gases of molecules in arbitrary confinement geometries is necessary. Here, we successfully evaporate fermionic KRb molecules in both 3D and quasi-2D geometries to well below their Fermi temperatures utilizing dipolar collisions. As we evaporate deeper into degeneracy in both geometries, we enter the Pauli-blocked regime with polar molecules, which we independently confirm for the first time by measuring the Pauli suppression of elastic collisions. Moreover, the Pauli suppression of collisions contributes to the limitation of our final molecular temperature to about 25% of the Fermi temperature in both geometries, particularly limiting quasi-2D evaporation where the Pauli blockade drastically reduces an otherwise large elastic to inelastic scattering ratio. This work demonstrates the production of degenerate Fermi gases of polar molecules both in a 3D harmonic trap and in mono- and bi-layer 2D configurations. Further, our work explores the fundamental limits on evaporation of molecular Fermi gases set by the Pauli-exclusion principle, which could be overcome in the future by introducing distinguishable scattering partners.

</details>


### [102] [Spin mixing induced dynamics of spinor solitons in $F=1$ Bose Einstein condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14231)
*T. Panagos,A. Romero-Ros,G. C. Katsimiga,P. Schmelcher,P. G. Kevrekidis*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟与有效经典模型研究了自旋F=1玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（BEC）中暗-亮-暗与亮-暗-亮孤子构型的相互作用，发现自旋相互作用导致的粒子交换动力学（particle exchange dynamics）会破坏原本可能的束缚态（bound state），并建立了一个拉格朗日（Lagrangian）有效模型以准确描述孤子运动轨迹与组分间粒子交换。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索均匀自旋F=1 BEC外加磁场背景下，暗-亮-暗与亮-暗-亮孤子构型之间的相互作用，特别是亮孤子相位差对其行为的影响，以及自旋相互作用（spinor interaction）如何改变经典的孤子束缚态行为。

Method: 采用数值模拟与拉格朗日方法（Lagrangian approach）构建有效经典模型（effective classical model），以此描述复杂自旋孤子系统的动力学行为，并通过与数值结果对比验证模型准确性。

Result: 发现自旋相互作用引发的超精细态（hyperfine state）之间的粒子交换动力学，会导致原本可能形成的孤子束缚态（bound state）被破坏；所提出的有效经典模型在大多数情况下能够提供一致的孤子运动轨迹与跨组分粒子交换动力学描述。

Conclusion: 该有效模型能够捕捉自旋相互作用下孤子行为的主要特征，为理解自旋F=1 BEC中多分量孤子相互作用提供可行的简化描述工具。

Abstract: We explore soliton interactions in a homogeneous spinor $F=1$ Bose Einstein Condensate (BEC) in the presence of a magnetic field, focusing on dark bright dark and bright dark bright configurations. We investigate how these interactions depend on the phase differences among bright solitons and their influence during the dynamics. Our findings align with prior non spinor results, i.e., repulsion among in phase bright solitons and attraction among out of phase pairs in self repulsive atomic BECs. The potential bright soliton attraction, added to the short range repulsion of dark dark soliton interactions, can lead to bound states. However, we find that these bound states break in the presence of spinor interactions due to the particle exchange dynamics between the hyperfine states of the components. Additonally, we develop an effective classical model to describe the soliton dynamics, using a Lagrangian approach. The accuracy of the model is tested by comparing it against numerical simulations. Our results suggest that the proposed model captures the essential features of soliton behavior in the presence of spin interactions, and provides congruent soliton trajectories and interspecies particle exchange dynamics in most of the cases.

</details>


### [103] [Mass-imbalanced two-dimensional Bose-Fermi mixtures with boson-fermion pairing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14338)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用图解T-矩阵方法（diagrammatic T-matrix approach）在零温下对二维玻色-费米混合体系进行理论分析；解析证明该形式在弱耦合极限下可正确恢复化学势的二阶微扰展开（second-order perturbative expansion），并通过数值计算加以验证。

Result: 数值结果确认了质量平衡情况下已有的近普适行为在不同质量比下依然成立，且当玻色子质量较大时精度更高；质量不平衡会定性改变玻色子动量分布，并可用于实验观测有限动量处的特征峰。

Conclusion: 质量不平衡可作为二维玻色-费米混合体系中除密度和耦合强度之外的新调控参数，为在实验中观测玻色子动量分布的非平凡结构提供了可行途径。

Abstract: We analyze a two-dimensional Bose-Fermi mixture at zero temperature in the presence of a tunable Bose-Fermi attraction. We adopt a diagrammatic T-matrix approach and study the behavior of several thermodynamic quantities for the two species as functions of density, mass ratio, and coupling strength. These include the chemical potentials, the boson momentum distribution function, the condensate density, and Tan's contact parameter. We analytically demonstrate that the present T-matrix formalism recovers the correct second-order perturbative expansion of the chemical potentials in the weak-coupling regime, and test it numerically. The near-universal behavior already found in prior work for the mass-balanced case is confirmed for different masses and becomes even more accurate when the boson mass is large. The mass imbalance emerges as an additional control parameter that qualitatively affects the bosonic momentum distribution. In particular, we found that it can be used to allow for the experimental observation of a peculiar peak in the boson momentum distribution at finite momentum.

### [104] [Modeling light-matter coupled systems with neural quantum states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14352)
*Noe Salmeron,Marin Bukov,Markus Schmitt*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文发展了一种基于神经量子态（neural quantum state）的方法，用于数值研究冷原子系统中短程相互作用与光子介导长程相互作用共存的混合希尔伯特空间（hybrid Hilbert space）多体系统。在一维里德伯原子（Rydberg atoms）与光子模耦合的模型上，该方法在强耦合区域高效捕捉了超辐射基态（superradiant ground state）及其关联，并观察到与平均场理论（mean-field theory）定量偏离的基态相边界。该方法可推广至自旋-声子（spin-phonon）等类似系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 冷原子操控的进展使得研究短程与长程相互作用共存的多体系统成为可能，但超越平均场方法的理论处理极具挑战性，亟需一种能够处理此类混合希尔伯特空间的数值方法。

Method: 提出一种基于神经量子态的神经网络架构，专门设计用于处理强相互作用自旋-光子系统中具有大局部玻色子维度（large local bosonic dimensions）的混合希尔伯特空间。

Result: 在二维里德伯原子与光子模耦合模型上的基准测试表明，该方法在强自旋-光子耦合区域有效找到了超辐射基态，验证了在高光子占据（high photon occupation）条件下的效率。同时，该方法成功捕捉了自旋-自旋和自旋-光子关联，从而在基态相边界（phase boundaries）上观察到与平均场理论的定量偏差。

Conclusion: 该方法可扩展至自旋-声子等其他具有混合希尔伯特空间结构的系统，为研究其基态性质提供了一个可扩展的框架。

Abstract: Recent advances in cold atom manipulation enable the study of many-body systems where short-range interactions between neighboring atoms coexist with long-range interactions mediated by photons. Such a combination of interactions makes a theoretical approach challenging beyond mean-field methods. In this work, we develop a neural quantum state based approach to study these systems numerically. We introduce a neural-network architecture capable of handling hybrid Hilbert spaces with large local bosonic dimensions in strongly interacting spin-photon systems. We benchmark this approach on a model of a two-dimensional lattice of Rydberg atoms coupled to a photon mode. The superradiant ground states found in the large spin-photon coupling regime allow us to demonstrate the efficiency of the method in the presence of high photon occupation. Furthermore, the ability to capture spin-spin and spin-photon correlations leads us to observe quantitative deviations in the ground state phase boundaries with respect to mean-field theory. The method extends to other systems with a similar hybrid Hilbert space structure, such as spin-phonon systems, and provides a scalable framework for investigating their ground state properties.

</details>

### [105] [Nodal degeneration of chiral algebras II: Local structure and chiral Zhu algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13986)
*Elchanan Nafcha*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 该论文为顶点代数（vertex algebra）的Zhu结合代数（Zhu's associative algebra）及其相关模结构提供了一种几何构造。通过将泛因子化代数（universal factorization algebra）在两点半稳定亏格零曲线上积分，构造了一个导出结合代数，其零阶同调恢复了Zhu代数。进一步构造了手征双模（chiral bimodule）及其形变，其零阶同调分别对应节点顶点代数的模转移代数（mode-transition algebra）及其形变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法核心是将泛因子化代数在两点半稳定亏格零曲线的稳定配置（stable configurations）上进行积分，由此构造一个导出结合代数。通过改变构造方式，进一步得到手征双模；再通过对节点形式光滑化（formal smoothing）进行积分，得到该双模的形变。

Result: 构造了一个导出结合代数，其零阶同调在顶点代数情形下恢复为Zhu结合代数。构造了一个手征双模，其零阶同调恢复为Damiolini、Gibney和Krashen定义的模转移代数。通过对形式光滑化积分得到形变，其零阶同调描述了模转移代数的形变。

Conclusion: 本文为Zhu结合代数及其相关模结构提供了统一的几何框架，展示了因子化代数的积分构造能够自然地恢复顶点代数表示论中的关键代数对象，并推广到节点和非平凡形变情形。

Abstract: Given a vertex algebra $V$, Zhu constructed an associative algebra $A(V)$, whose representation theory provides an approximation to the category of $V$-modules. We describe a geometric construction of a certain derived associative algebra $\mathfrak{Z}_{\mathcal{A}}^0$ associated to any universal factorization algebra $\mathcal{A}$, whose zeroth homology recovers Zhu's associative algebra in the case where $\mathcal{A}$ is obtained from a vertex algebra. The construction is given by integrating $\mathcal{A}$ over stable configurations parametrized by two-pointed semistable genus zero curves. By a variant of this construction, we obtained a chiral $\mathcal{A}$-bimodule $\mathfrak{Z}_{\mathcal{A}}$ describing the value of a factorization algebra at a nodal point. We show that its zeroth homology recovers the bimodule underlying the mode-transition algebra $\mathfrak{A}(V)$ defined by Damiolini, Gibney, and Krashen, which they use to describes a vertex algebra at a node. Finally, the value over a formal smoothing of a node provides a deformation $\tilde{\mathfrak{Z}}_{\mathcal{A}}$ of $\mathfrak{Z}_{\mathcal{A}}$, whose zeroth homology describes a deformation of the mode-transition algebra in the case of a vertex algebra.

Systematic approaches to PDE model exploration are a holy grail of computational science. ### [107] [Spin disorder competing with positional symmetry breaking governs the metal-insulator behavior in oxide paramagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14624)
*Jia-Xin Xiong,Xiuwen Zhang,Alex Zunger*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用对称性破缺的密度泛函理论（density-functional theory, DFT）研究顺磁（paramagnetic, PM）绝缘体 NaFeO3 与新发现的金属性 NaOsO3，提出磁性与位置对称性破缺之间的竞争是决定过渡金属氧化物顺磁相绝缘或金属行为的一般框架，无需引入强关联效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大量过渡金属氧化物在低温下表现为反铁磁（antiferromagnetic, AFM）绝缘态，高温下则为顺磁（PM）相，但PM相既可绝缘也可导电。文章旨在不借助强关联机制的情况下，解释这一差异的物理根源。

Method: 采用对称性破缺的密度泛函理论（DFT）分别计算绝缘性NaFeO3与金属性NaOsO3的顺磁相。通过分析磁有序与位置对称性破缺之间的相互作用，比较两种材料中自旋无序诱导的局域磁矩分布与偏离中心的原子位移分布的相对强弱。

Result: NaFeO3具有较大的位置位移但较小的自旋无序诱导磁矩分布，从而形成绝缘的顺磁相；NaOsO3则呈现显著的自旋无序诱导磁矩分布，迫使顺磁相转变为金属态。

Conclusion: 磁性与位置对称性破缺之间的竞争为理解过渡金属氧化物顺磁体中看似迥异的金属-绝缘体行为提供了一般性框架，且无需引入强关联效应。

Abstract: Numerous transition-metal oxides have low-temperature antiferromagnetic (AFM) states and high-temperature paramagnetic (PM) phases, where the AFM state is usually insulating while the PM phase can be either insulating or metallic. Without involving strong correlation, we use symmetry-broken density-functional theory (DFT) to obtain the PM phases of insulating NaFeO3 vs the recently discovered metallic NaOsO3. We develop the understanding of insulating and metallic behaviors in paramagnetic oxides by analyzing the interactions between magnetic and positional symmetry breaking: The insulating gap is governed by the competition between the spin disorder that induces a distribution of different magnitudes of local magnetic moments and the polymorphous distribution of off-center atomic displacements. NaFeO3, on the other hand, has large positional displacement with small spin-disorder-induced moments distribution, leading to insulating PM phase, whereas NaOsO3 has a pronounced spin-disorder-induced moments distribution that forces the PM phase to become metallic. Our work identifies this symmetry-breaking competition as a general framework to bridge seemingly disparate metal-insulator behaviors in transition-metal oxides paramagnets without invoking strong correlation.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用de Sitter时空中标量场的不变两点函数通过Lorentzian调和分析（Lorentzian harmonic analysis）表达为Legendre函数（Legendre functions）的结构，结合Mehler–Fock变换（Mehler–Fock transform）得到完整Riemann ξ函数的积分表示；在此基础上定义谱权重由ξ函数给出的推迟传播子，并在允许符号不定谱测度的Krein空间量子化（Krein space quantization）框架下进行分析。

Result: 建立了Riemann ξ函数在临界线（critical line）上的几何与谱解释；揭示了ξ函数零点的渐近间距与de Sitter几何中质量-时间尺度（mass–time scaling）之间的关联。

Conclusion: 该工作为de Sitter量子场论、调和分析与解析数论之间提供了一个新颖的解释框架，展示了跨领域数学与物理结构之间的深层对应。

Abstract: The invariant two-point function of a scalar field in de Sitter spacetime can be expressed in terms of Legendre functions via Lorentzian harmonic analysis. Using this structure together with the Mehler--Fock transform, we obtain an integral representation of the completed Riemann $ξ$-function in which the Legendre kernel appears naturally. Motivated by this correspondence, we introduce a retarded propagator whose spectral weight is given by the $ξ$-function and analyze it within the framework of Krein space quantization, where sign-indefinite spectral measures are admissible. This construction yields a geometric and spectral interpretation of the $ξ$-function restricted to the critical line and relates the asymptotic spacing of its zeros to a mass--time scaling in de Sitter geometry. The results provide a novel interpretive framework linking de Sitter quantum field theory, harmonic analysis, and analytic number theory.

### [110] [Coherent structures and bifurcation analysis in a toxin-driven plant-herbivore model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14559)
*Grifo Gabriele,Valenti Giovanna*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究毒素介导的相互作用与定向运动如何塑造植物-食草动物系统中的相干结构（coherent structures），通过一个包含毒素依赖功能响应（toxin-dependent functional response）和交叉扩散项（cross-diffusion term）的两室模型，揭示了弱毒性与强毒性下的不同动力学机制，以及图灵失稳（Turing instability）和混合时空模式的条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解植物化学防御（化学毒素）与食草动物定向运动如何共同驱动系统从均匀态向振荡、空间斑图及混合行为的涌现，填补现有理论中对毒素介导的非线性反馈与运动策略耦合机制的空白。

Method: 采用两室模型（two-compartment model），包含毒素依赖的功能响应函数和表征食草动物趋向或远离植被的交叉扩散项；通过弱非线性分析（weakly nonlinear analysis）推导Stuart-Landau振幅方程以描述分岔附近的模式调制；辅以数值模拟进行验证。

Result: 弱毒性下系统至多存在一个生物学可行的共存平衡态，可通过Hopf分岔（Hopf bifurcation）失稳产生小幅时间振荡；强毒性下功能响应变为非单调，允许多个共存平衡态与突变性转变（abrupt regime shifts）。交叉扩散可诱导图灵失稳及混合时空模式，数值模拟证实了从均匀态到振荡、空间斑图及混合行为的转变。

Conclusion: 化学防御、非线性反馈与运动策略共同决定了植物-食草动物系统中相干结构的涌现、选择与鲁棒性。

Abstract: This work investigates how toxin-mediated interactions and directed movements shape the emergence of coherent structures in plant-herbivore systems. The analysis focuses on a two-compartment model enclosing a toxin-dependent functional response and a cross-diffusion term that represents ecologically plausible herbivores' movement towards, or away from, vegetation. Two distinct dynamical regimes arise depending on toxicity strength. Under weak toxicity, the system admits at most one biologically feasible coexistence equilibrium, which may lose stability through a Hopf bifurcation generating small-amplitude temporal oscillations. Under strong toxicity, the nonlinear functional response becomes non-monotonic, allowing for multiple coexistence equilibria and abrupt regime shifts. The influence of cross-diffusion on stability is also examined, identifying the conditions under which Turing instabilities and mixed spatiotemporal patterns occur. Near the corresponding bifurcation thresholds, Stuart-Landau amplitude equations are derived via weakly nonlinear analysis, providing a unified framework for the modulation of oscillatory, stationary, and combined Turing-Hopf modes. Numerical simulations corroborate the theoretical predictions, illustrating transitions from spatially uniform states to oscillations, spatial patterns, and mixed behaviour. Overall, this manuscript highlights how chemical defences, nonlinear feedbacks, and movement strategies jointly determine the emergence, selection, and robustness of coherent structures in plant-herbivore systems.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

### [112] [Universal Construction of Generalized Lyapunov Functions for Nonlinear Dynamical Systems Using Physics-Informed Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14174)
*Z. C. Tu*

Main category: nlin.CD

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于广义Lyapunov函数（generalized Lyapunov function）的非平衡势（nonequilibrium potential）构建框架，通过数据无关的物理信息神经网络（physics-informed neural network）直接嵌入Lyapunov不等式与弱散度-尺度相容性条件，实现对非线性非梯度系统（non-gradient system）标量势能景观（scalar potential landscape）的学习与构造。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对于非梯度动力学（non-gradient dynamics），如何为含有回归结构（recurrent structure）的非线性流构造全局Lyapunov型标量函数仍是一大障碍，而标量势能景观是理解动力系统稳定性与跃迁的最有效工具之一。

Method: 引入广义Lyapunov函数作为非平衡势的统一概念，将普通Lyapunov函数、Freidlin–Wentzell拟势（quasi-potential）以及Ao型势（Ao-type potential）作为特例纳入该框架；提出一种数据无关的物理信息神经网络框架，将Lyapunov不等式和弱散度-尺度相容性条件直接编码到损失函数中。

Result: 在线性系统、Hopf标准型（Hopf normal form）、van der Pol振荡器（van der Pol oscillator）以及具有两个链接极限环的三维Hopf-link流（three-dimensional Hopf-link flow）上进行了测试，学习得到的势能景观与可用的解析基准一致，并将不变集（invariant set）揭示为低势或常势结构。

Conclusion: 该方法为非线性非梯度系统的势能景观构建提供了一条实用路径。

Abstract: A scalar potential landscape is one of the most useful ways to understand the stability and transition of a dynamical system. For non-gradient dynamics, however, the construction of a global Lyapunov-type scalar for nonlinear flows with recurrent structures remains a major obstacle. We introduce the generalized Lyapunov function, a scalar function that is non-increasing along deterministic trajectories, as a unifying notion of nonequilibrium potential. Ordinary Lyapunov functions, Freidlin--Wentzell quasi-potentials, and Ao-type potentials are recovered as special representatives. We then propose a data-free physics-informed neural-network framework in which the Lyapunov inequality and a weak divergence-scale compatibility condition are directly embedded into the loss function. The method is tested on linear systems, the Hopf normal form, the van der Pol oscillator, and a three-dimensional Hopf-link flow with two linked limit cycles. The learned landscapes agree with available analytical benchmarks and reveal the invariant sets as low-potential or constant-potential structures, providing a practical route to potential-landscape construction for nonlinear non-gradient systems.

### [113] [4d CFT Correlators from Ambitwistors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13770)
*Mariana Carrillo González,Théo Keseman*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文发展了一套四维共形场论中自旋关联函数的ambitwistor空间表述，证明了共形对称性和守恒性可通过ambitwistor Penrose变换平凡化，并显式构造了两点和三点ambitwistor关联函数。文中还提出了投影到奇偶宇称扇形的普适公式，并在多个非平凡例子中验证，同时讨论了边界双拷贝、twistor表示以及边界传播子的整合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在四维共形场论（CFT）中，具有自旋的守恒关联函数（spinning correlators）的构造与对称性分析通常复杂。本文旨在利用ambitwistor空间形式，简化共形对称性与守恒条件的处理，并系统化自旋关联函数的构造。

Method: 采用ambitwistor空间的Penrose变换（ambitwistor Penrose transform），将共形对称性与守恒律“平凡化”；显式构造两点和三点ambitwistor关联函数；提出区分宇称（parity-even/parity-odd）的投影公式，并在非平凡例子中验证；利用twistor表示中的三次曲线（degree-three curves）定位三点关联函数；扩展形式以纳入整数共形维数幺正算符的边界传播子（boundary propagators）及共形耦合标量场（conformally coupled scalars）。

Result: 成功构造了ambitwistor空间下的自旋关联函数，证明了该形式能够自然生成与边界双拷贝（boundary double copy）兼容的基；三点关联函数在双twistor表示中局域化于三次曲线；该形式可推广至整数维数算子及共形耦合标量。

Conclusion: ambitwistor空间形式为四维CFT中的守恒自旋关联函数提供了一种系统、简洁的构造方法，并能自然兼容边界双拷贝结构，有望在共形场论与散射振幅的交叉研究中发挥作用。

Abstract: We develop an ambitwistor-space formulation of conserved spinning correlators in four-dimensional CFTs. We show that conformal symmetry and conservation are trivialised by the ambitwistor Penrose transform, and construct the two- and three-point ambitwistor correlators explicitly. We further propose a simple formula for projecting onto parity-even and parity-odd sectors, and verify it in several non-trivial examples. The resulting correlators furnish a natural basis compatible with a boundary double copy for arbitrary spin. At three points, we show that they localise on degree-three curves in a two-twistor representation. We also explain how the formalism incorporates boundary propagators for unitary operators of integer conformal dimension, and extend it to conformally coupled scalars.

</details>


### [114] [Bootstrapping Euclidean Lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13771)
*Francesco Bertucci,James Bonifacio*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用半正定规划（semidefinite programming）和共形自举（conformal bootstrap）方法，从平坦环面（flat tori）与轨形（orbifolds）上的拉普拉斯谱（Laplace spectrum）与本征函数乘积积分导出的谱恒等式出发，推导出三重积平方和的上界。这些上界在物理上约束了高维场论环面紧化（toroidal compactification）中的三次耦合常数平方和，并在数学上给出了格子最小向量均方数的上界。通过构造精确泛函，证明该上界在 2、4、8、24 维分别由六边形格、D₄ 格、E₈ 格和 Leech 格饱和。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将共形自举方法推广到平坦环面和轨形的拉普拉斯谱分析中，建立谱恒等式与半正定规划之间的桥梁，从而获得关于本征函数三重积平方和的系统性上界。

Method: 从拉普拉斯谱与本征函数乘积积分的谱恒等式出发，采用半正定规划方法推导三重积平方和的上界，这一思路借用了共形自举（conformal bootstrap）的框架。针对格子问题，进一步构造精确泛函（exact functionals）以证明上界的饱和性。

Result: 推导出三重积平方和的上界；对于欧几里得格子（Euclidean lattices），得到关于最小向量均方数的上界，该上界除以接触数（kissing number）后，在 2、4、8、24 维分别由六边形格、D₄ 格、E₈ 格和 Leech 格实现饱和。

Conclusion: 半正定规划与谱恒等式的结合为场论紧化中的耦合常数约束和格点几何中的极值问题提供了统一的理论框架，并揭示了若干经典极值格在相应维度上的最优性。

Abstract: We derive spectral identities involving the Laplace spectrum and the integrals of products of eigenfunctions on flat tori and orbifolds. Using semidefinite programming, we derive upper bounds on sums of squares of triple products from these spectral identities, following the approach of the conformal bootstrap. Physically, these upper bounds give constraints on sums of squares of cubic coupling constants in toroidal compactifications of higher-dimensional field theories. For Euclidean lattices, one of the bootstrap bounds leads to an upper bound on the mean square number of minimal vectors that are minimal distance from each minimal vector, divided by the kissing number of the lattice. By finding exact functionals for the semidefinite programming problems, we prove that this bound is saturated in 2, 4, 8, and 24 dimensions by the hexagonal lattice, the $D_4$ lattice, the $E_8$ lattice, and the Leech lattice, respectively.

### [115] [A note on the quantization of angular momentum for black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13774)
*Jon Goker,Luca V. Iliesiu,Elisa Tabor*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文论证了旋转黑洞的引力路径积分（gravitational path integral）在角速度（angular velocity）上具有周期性，这一周期性意味着在任意维度的渐近平直（asymptotically flat）或反德西特（AdS）边界条件下，角动量均被量子化（quantization of angular momentum）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究旋转黑洞引力路径积分的结构，特别是角速度周期性的起源及其对角动量量子化的影响。

Method: 通过分析路径积分中由角速度整数位移标记的无限族鞍点（saddles），论证其周期性与角动量量子化；在AdS$_3$中归因于边界映射类群（boundary mapping class group），在高维情形则与边界大微分同胚（large boundary diffeomorphism）无关；并针对Kerr-Newman黑洞和4D Schwarzschild黑洞构造了这些鞍点的显式形式。

Result: 发现角速度的周期性在任意维度下均成立；高维情形的周期性源于与边界映射类群无关的无限族鞍点；即使是最简单的4D Schwarzschild黑洞，其路径积分也包含来自无限旋转鞍点的贡献。

Conclusion: 旋转黑洞的引力路径积分具有内在的角速度周期性，这一性质强制了角动量的量子化，并且该结论适用于渐近平直和AdS两种边界条件，且不依赖于边界大微分同胚。

Abstract: We argue that the gravitational path integral for rotating black holes is periodic in the angular velocity, implying the quantization of angular momentum in arbitrary dimensions for either asymptotically flat or AdS boundary conditions. In AdS$_3$, this periodicity is a consequence of the boundary mapping class group. In higher dimensions, the periodicity arises from an infinite family of saddles labeled by integer shifts of the angular velocity unrelated to the boundary mapping class group; summing over these saddles enforces quantization independently of any large boundary diffeomorphism. We construct these saddles explicitly for Kerr-Newman black holes in both asymptotically flat space and AdS$_4$, and observe that even the path integral for the 4D Schwarzschild black hole, typically the simplest case, receives contributions from an infinite set of rotating saddles.

### [116] [Mirror symmetry on a circle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13775)
*Siqi Chen,Shehab Hossam Fadda,Matteo Sacchi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了三维阿贝尔镜像对称（abelian mirror symmetry）中超对称指标恒等式（supersymmetric index identities）的小圆（高温）极限，发现该极限总能将一侧约化为二维 $\mathcal{N}=(2,2)$ 规范线性西格玛模型（GLSM）的球面配分函数，另一侧可解释为 Hori–Vafa 对偶的 Landau–Ginzburg (LG) 模型配分函数或 Liouville/Toda CFT 的库仑气体积分（Coulomb gas integral），从而系统性地建立了 GLSM、LG 模型与 CFT 之间的积分恒等式，并应用于 2d/2d 对应（2d/2d correspondence）。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过分析 SQED 超对称指标恒等式在小圆极限下的两种缩放方案，分别考察两侧的约化行为；一侧恒化为二维 $\mathcal{N}=(2,2)$ GLSM 的球面配分函数，另一侧则具有双重解释——作为 Hori–Vafa 对偶的 LG 模型配分函数，或作为 Liouville/Toda CFT 相关函数的库仑气体积分。此外，还给出了纯二维视角的推导，受 Kapustin–Strassler 对三维阿贝尔镜像对称的分段推导方法启发。

Result: 系统性地生成了 GLSM 配分函数与 LG 模型配分函数或 CFT 库仑气体积分之间的积分恒等式；以 $(A_{k-1},A_{N-1})$ Argyres–Douglas 理论为例，展示了 CFT 为非幺正极小模型（non-unitary minimal model）的具体实现。

Conclusion: 小圆极限方法为生成不同二维理论（GLSM、LG 模型）与 CFT 之间的恒等式提供了系统途径，在 2d/2d 对应中有实用价值，且可通过纯二维方式重新推导，进一步统一了三维镜像对称与二维对偶的图景。

Abstract: We investigate the small circle, or high temperature, limit of the supersymmetric index identities for the three-dimensional abelian mirror symmetry of SQED. There exist two possible limits, depending on how the parameters of the theory are scaled with the radius of the circle. In both cases the result is qualitatively similar. One side always reduces to the sphere partition function of a two-dimensional $\mathcal{N}=(2,2)$ gauged linear sigma model (GLSM). The opposite side has a two-fold interpretation, either as the sphere partition function of the Landau--Ginzburg (LG) model that is Hori--Vafa dual to the GLSM, or as a Coulomb gas integral for a correlation function of Liouville or Toda CFT. This approach thus provides a systematic way to generate integral identities between partition functions of GLSMs on the one hand, and partition functions of LG models or CFT Coulomb gas integrals on the other. The latter perspective finds useful applications in the recently proposed 2d/2d correspondence, which relates sphere partition functions of unitary 2d $\mathcal{N}=(2,2)$ theories and correlation functions of non-unitary 2d CFTs that both descend from compactifications of a unitary 4d $\mathcal{N}=2$ SCFT. We present an example based on the $(A_{k-1},A_{N-1})$ Argyres--Douglas theories, where the CFT is a non-unitary minimal model. We also give a purely two-dimensional derivation of the identities obtained in the small circle limit which is inspired by the Kapustin--Strassler piecewise derivation of 3d abelian mirror symmetry.

### [117] [Resurgence of the Thermal Transition between Bounce and Sphaleron](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13778)
*Shaun D. Hampton,Kyungsun Lee,Sungjay Lee*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文从Borel重求和（Borel resurgence）视角研究了量子力学中具有亚稳态真空（metastable vacuum）的热跃迁（ bounce 与 sphaleron 之间的转变），通过计算热自由能的高阶微扰展开并提取主导Borel奇点数据，证明了微扰展开能够确定跃迁温度、跃迁阶数以及包含单圈预因子的衰变率，无需依赖半经典（semiclassical）输入。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，亚稳态真空的热衰变（thermal decay）依赖于半经典方法（如 bounce 和 sphaleron 解），但其适用范围和精确度存在局限。本文旨在探索能否仅从微扰理论（perturbation theory）出发，通过 Borel 重求和框架自洽地提取跃迁信息，从而摆脱对半经典输入的依赖。

Method: 选取分别代表二级相变（second-order transition）和一级相变（first-order transition）的两个模型，计算热自由能（thermal free energy）的高阶微扰展开，并从中提取主导Borel奇点数据 \((A, b, S)\) 作为温度的函数。其中 \(A\) 为奇点位置，\(b\) 为特征指数（characteristic exponent），\(S\) 为Stokes常数。

Result: Borel奇点位置 \(A\) 重现了跃迁两侧主导鞍点（saddle）的在壳作用量（on-shell action），在二级相变中光滑连接，在一级相变中形成扭结（kink）。特征指数 \(b\) 在跃迁前后从 \(0\) 跳变到 \(1/2\)，计数相应鞍点的零模（zero modes）数目。Stokes常数 \(S\) 与鞍点周围的单圈行列式（one-loop determinant）一致。

Conclusion: 围绕假真空（false vacuum）的微扰展开足以确定跃迁温度、跃迁阶数以及包含单圈预因子的衰变率，从而建立了一种无需半经典输入的热衰变分析方法，验证了 Borel 重求和框架在量子力学热跃迁问题中的有效性。

Abstract: We study the thermal transition between the bounce and the sphaleron in quantum mechanics with a metastable vacuum from the viewpoint of Borel resurgence. For two models representing a second-order and a first-order transition, we compute the perturbative expansion of the thermal free energy to high orders and extract the leading Borel singularity data $(A,b,S)$ as functions of temperature. The Borel singularity location $A$ reproduces the on-shell action of the dominant saddle on both sides of the transition, joining smoothly in the second-order case and developing a kink in the first-order case. The characteristic exponent $b$ jumps between $0$ and $1/2$ across the transition, counting the zero modes of the corresponding saddle. The Stokes constant $S$ matches the one-loop determinant around the saddle. The perturbative expansion around the false vacuum thus determines the transition temperature, the order of the transition, and the decay rate including the one-loop prefactor without relying on semiclassical inputs.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用重整化群（renormalization group）方法分析费米子相互作用算符$(ψ^\dagger ψ)^{2n}$的beta函数，推导拖拽机制（drag mechanism）的数学形式，并在2+1维非费米液体（non-Fermi liquid）与临界玻色子耦合的模型中验证该机制。

Result: BCS四费米耦合的增长会诱导拖拽机制，使所有高阶费米子耦合在红外方向被驱动至强耦合，但重整化群流保留了一个层次结构（hierarchy），高阶算符相对于BCS相互作用保持参数化压低。在2+1维非费米液体中，高阶相互作用虽被增强，但不会破坏足够大$N$下的红外稳定非费米液体不动点。

Conclusion: 拖拽机制普遍适用于费米子算符的整个层级，高阶费米子相互作用不一定会破坏非费米液体固定点的稳定性，该结果对多组分超导体（multicomponent superconductors）及其他强关联金属体系具有潜在意义。

Abstract: We study the renormalization-group flow of higher-dimensional fermionic interactions $(ψ^\dagger ψ)^{2n}$ in the presence of a Fermi surface. We show that the growth of the BCS four-fermion coupling induces a drag mechanism whereby higher-order fermionic couplings are driven to strong coupling in the infrared. We derive the corresponding beta functions and show that the drag effect applies generically to the whole tower of fermionic operators. Remarkably, although all couplings are driven toward the same strong-coupling scale, the renormalization-group flow preserves a hierarchy in which higher-dimensional operators remain parametrically suppressed relative to the BCS interaction. We then investigate this mechanism in a $2+1$-dimensional non-Fermi liquid coupled to a critical boson. While higher-order fermionic interactions are similarly enhanced along the flow, we show that they do not destabilize the IR stable non-Fermi-liquid fixed point, present for sufficiently large $N$. We briefly discuss possible implications for multicomponent superconductors and other strongly correlated metallic systems.
