### [121] [Black hole thermodynamics and KK photon quantum corrections in 2D effective dilaton gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14016)
*Yoshihiko Abe,Tetsutaro Higaki,Yu Miyauchi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过四维爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦理论（Einstein–Maxwell theory）的降维得到一个二维有效理论（effective theory），研究球形带电黑洞的热力学。该二维理论再现了半经典相结构（包括Hawking–Page相变和小/大Reissner–Nordström–AdS黑洞相变），并表明在未取近视界和近极端极限时，该理论可捕捉非极端热力学。此外，通过积分掉内球面上的电磁卡鲁扎-克莱因模式（Kaluza–Klein modes），得到单圈有效标量引力（one-loop effective dilaton gravity），其导数展开的首阶修正表现为黑洞熵和有效电荷参数的常数平移，因此半经典相结构在局域近似下不发生定性改变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索二维有效理论是否能在不取近视界和近极端极限（near-horizon and near-extremal limits）的情况下，准确捕捉四维带电黑洞的非极端（non-extremal）热力学以及半经典相结构（semiclassical phase structure）。

Method: 将四维Einstein–Maxwell理论通过球对称降维（dimensional reduction）得到二维标量引力（dilaton gravity），并进一步积分掉内球面上的电磁Kaluza–Klein模式，在导数展开（derivative expansion）的首阶导出单圈有效dilaton引力。

Result: 二维有效理论再现了半经典相结构，包括Hawking–Page相变和小/大Reissner–Nordström–AdS黑洞相变。单圈修正表现为黑洞熵（black hole entropy）和有效电荷参数的常数平移，在半经典相结构上未引入定性改变。

Conclusion: 二维降维方法在非极端区域也能准确描述四维黑洞热力学，且量子修正（单圈效应）在局域导数展开近似下仅产生常数偏移，不会改变半经典相结构的定性行为。

Abstract: We study black hole thermodynamics using a two-dimensional effective theory obtained by dimensional reduction of four-dimensional Einstein--Maxwell theory. For spherically symmetric charged black holes, the resulting dilaton gravity has a nonlinear potential that reproduces the semiclassical phase structure of four-dimensional AdS black holes, including the Hawking--Page transition and the small/large Reissner--Nordström--AdS black hole transition. This shows that the two-dimensional theory before taking the near-horizon and near-extremal limits captures non-extremal thermodynamics beyond the Jackiw--Teitelboim gravity regime. We also include electromagnetic Kaluza--Klein modes on the internal sphere and integrate them out to derive the one-loop effective dilaton gravity. At leading order in the derivative expansion, these corrections appear as constant shifts in the black hole entropy and in the effective charge parameter of the dilaton potential. Therefore, the semiclassical phase structure is not qualitatively modified within this leading local approximation.

</details>


### [122] [Hydrodynamics of Nonminimal $F^{(a)αβ} F^{(a)γλ} R_{αγ} R_{βλ}$ AdS Black Brane](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14115)
*Mehdi Sadeghi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过AdS黑洞解中引入非最小耦合项 $q_2 F^{(a)αβ}F^{(a)γλ}R_{αγ}R_{βλ}$，采用微扰展开和流体-引力对应（fluid-gravity correspondence），计算了强耦合非阿贝尔等离子体的DC色电导率（DC color conductivity）$σ$ 和剪切粘滞熵比（shear viscosity to entropy density ratio）$η/s$。结果表明，该耦合项会违反 $σ\ge 1$ 的导电率下界（当 $q_2>0$），并修正KSS下界 $η/s = 1/(4π)$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究强耦合非阿贝尔等离子体在引力对偶框架下，非最小耦合的高阶导数修正对流体动力学输运系数的影响，特别是检验导电率下界和KSS下界（KSS bound）在弯曲耦合规范相互作用下的鲁棒性（robustness）。

Method: 在四维AdS黑膜（AdS black brane）体时空作用量中引入非最小耦合项 $q_2 F^{(a)αβ}F^{(a)γλ}R_{αγ}R_{βλ}$，该高阶导数项实现了杨-米尔斯场强（Yang-Mills field strength）与里奇张量（Ricci tensor）的直接耦合。采用关于小耦合参数 $q_2$ 的微扰展开，构造至一阶的黑膜解，并利用流体-引力对应计算输运系数。

Result: DC导电率结果为 $σ= 1 - q_2 \bigl(9κQ^2/(L^2 r_h^4) + 7κ^2 Q^4/(4 r_h^8)\bigr)$：$q_2>0$ 时 $σ<1$，违反导电率通用下界 $σ\ge 1$；$q_2<0$ 时下界仍保持。剪切粘滞熵比为 $η/s = (1/(4π))\bigl(1 + q_2\, 7κ^2 Q^4/(2 r_h^8)\bigr)$，KSS下界被 $q_2$ 线性项修正，$q_2$ 的符号决定比值高于或低于 $1/(4π)$。

Conclusion: 非最小曲率-规范耦合对全息输运（holographic transport）具有显著影响，提供了一个高阶导数修正如何影响强耦合等离子体流体动力学区域的可控范例，表明KSS下界和导电率下界在更一般的引力对偶中并非普适守恒量。

Abstract: We investigate the hydrodynamic properties of a strongly coupled non-Abelian plasma dual to a four-dimensional AdS black brane with a nonminimal coupling of the form $q_2 F^{(a)αβ}F^{(a)γλ}R_{αγ}R_{βλ}$ in the bulk action. This higher-derivative term introduces a direct interaction between the Yang-Mills field strength and the Ricci tensor, leading to corrections beyond the minimal Einstein-Yang-Mills theory. Using a perturbative expansion in the small coupling $q_2$, we construct the black brane solution up to first order and employ the fluid-gravity correspondence to compute two key transport coefficients: the DC color conductivity $σ$ and the shear viscosity to entropy density ratio $η/s$. In holography, $η/s$ is inversely proportional to the square of the coupling constant of the boundary theory, while $σ$ in Einstein-Maxwell theory satisfies a universal lower bound $σ\ge 1$ (in units where $\hbar=1$), saturated for uncharged black holes and characterizing a perfect quantum critical fluid. Our results reveal that the nonminimal coupling significantly alters these transport quantities. For the DC conductivity, we find $σ= 1 - q_2 \bigl(9κQ^2/(L^2 r_h^4) + 7κ^2 Q^4/(4 r_h^8)\bigr)$, indicating a violation of the conductivity bound for $q_2>0$ while the bound is preserved for $q_2<0$. For the shear viscosity, we obtain $η/s = (1/(4π))\bigl(1 + q_2\, 7κ^2 Q^4/(2 r_h^8)\bigr)$, showing that the KSS bound is modified by a term linear in $q_2$. The sign of $q_2$ determines whether the ratio increases above or decreases below the universal value $1/(4π)$. These findings highlight the sensitivity of holographic transport to curvature-coupled gauge interactions and provide a controlled example of how higher-derivative corrections influence the hydrodynamic regime of strongly coupled plasmas.

</details>


### [123] [Quantum Entanglement of Bethe States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14140)
*Yu Hao,Yunfeng Jiang,Bi-Quan Yang,De-liang Zhong*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文系统地研究了包括XXX₁/₂模型、高自旋XXXₛ模型以及非紧致SL(2,ℝ)链在内的可积自旋链家族中Bethe态的量子纠缠。通过全面扫描有限周期链的二分纠缠熵，识别出了使纠缠最小化和最大化的Bethe解，揭示了自旋依赖的极值模式；同时发现最小纠缠态在不同模型中并不总是基态，并开发了用于离壳Bethe态纠缠极值优化的算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可积系统中的量子纠缠结构是理解强关联量子多体系统的重要视角，但Bethe态（Bethe states）在整个能谱上的纠缠极值行为尚缺乏系统性研究，尤其是高自旋和非紧致情形下的规律尚未被揭示。

Method: 对有限周期边界条件下的XXX₁/₂、XXXₛ及SL(2,ℝ)自旋链，计算并扫描所有壳上Bethe本征态（on-shell eigenstates）的二分纠缠熵（bipartite entanglement entropy），识别极值解并分析其Bethe量子数（Bethe quantum numbers）的模式；对离壳Bethe态（off-shell Bethe states）则开发了一种在快度分布（rapidity distribution）上优化纠缠熵的算法。

Result: 在XXX₁/₂反铁磁链中，给定固定磁子数（fixed-magnon sector）下最小纠缠态始终对应基态（ground state）；但在高自旋XXXₛ模型中，最小纠缠态并不总是基态，甚至可以是最高能态。最大纠缠态的Bethe根（Bethe roots）结构更为复杂。奇异解（singular and strange solutions）等特殊Bethe根配置会影响纠缠，且非紧致SL(2,ℝ)链表现出紧致自旋链所不具备的纠缠特征。

Conclusion: Bethe态纠缠极值的系统模式揭示了可积系统中纠缠结构与能级、自旋及模型紧致性之间的深层关联；所开发的离壳优化算法为在更一般条件下探索Bethe态的最大纠缠提供了新工具。

Abstract: We investigate the quantum entanglement of Bethe states across a family of integrable spin chains, including the XXX$_{\frac{1}{2}}$ model, its higher-spin generalizations (XXX$_s$), and the non-compact $SL(2,\mathbb{R})$ chain. For on-shell eigenstates, we perform a comprehensive scan of the bipartite entanglement entropy across the entire spectrum of finite chains with periodic boundary conditions, and identify the Bethe solutions that minimize and maximize the entanglement. These extremal solutions follow systematic, spin-dependent patterns in the Bethe quantum numbers. In the XXX$_{\frac{1}{2}}$ spin chain, for the antiferromagnetic chain, the state with minimal entropy always coincides with the lowest-energy state (the ground state) within a given fixed-magnon sector. For the higher-spin XXX$_s$ model, however, the lowest-entropy state is not always identical to the ground state, and can even be the state of highest energy. By contrast, the Bethe roots that maximize entropy exhibit considerably more intricate structure. Our analysis further reveals how special Bethe root configurations, such as singular and strange solutions, affect entanglement, and it uncovers characteristic entanglement features in the non-compact $SL(2,\mathbb{R})$ chain that are absent from compact spin chains. For off-shell Bethe states, we develop an optimization algorithm that extremizes the entanglement entropy over rapidity distributions, enabling us to explore the maximum entanglement achievable by a Bethe state without imposing the Bethe ansatz equations.

</details>


### [124] [Real-time pseudo entropy and modular-Hamiltonian correlations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14208)
*Tatsuhiro Misumi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究量子态在实时幺正演化下伪熵（pseudo entropy）的短时行为，揭示其实部与虚部分别由哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）与模哈密顿量（modular Hamiltonian）的对易子与协方差控制，并将这一“面向时间的模响应”与熵产生及非厄米推广联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 伪熵是纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）向复数域的推广，其物理含义在实时演化场景下尚未被充分理解。本文旨在建立实时伪熵短时展开的严格形式，阐明其虚部并非单纯的支点假象，而是反映微观时间演化与子系统粗粒化之间关联的物理量。

Method: 作者从约化转移矩阵（reduced transition matrix）出发，对初始纯态经幺正时间演化后的实时伪熵进行短时间展开，推导出其一阶项由物理哈密顿量 $H$ 与模哈密顿量 $K_A=-\log\rho_A$ 的关联决定。通过分析厄米动力学下展开系数的对称化协方差与对易子结构，作者进一步在Schmidt对角模型、两比特模型及横场伊辛链淬火（transverse-field Ising-chain quench）中进行了验证，并给出$\mathcal{PT}$对称非厄米推广的玩具模型。

Result: 严格推导了实时伪熵的短时展开公式 $S_A(t,0)=S_A(0)-it \langle K_A(H-\langle H\rangle)\rangle + \mathcal{O}(t^2)$，其中虚部响应由对称化协方差（symmetrized covariance）控制，实部响应由对易子（commutator）控制。在横场伊辛链临界区域附近完成了模磁化率（modular susceptibility）的有限尺寸标度分析。

Conclusion: 实时伪熵的虚部承载了面向时间的模响应（time-oriented modular response）信息，体现了微观动力学与子系统纠缠结构之间的关联。该响应可通过模磁化率与普通熵产生相联系，并可向非厄米$\mathcal{PT}$对称系统自然推广。

Abstract: Pseudo entropy is a complex-valued generalization of entanglement entropy defined from a reduced transition matrix. We study the pseudo entropy associated with a real-time transition matrix between an initial pure state and its unitary time evolution. For a subsystem $A$, we show that the short-time behavior of real-time pseudo entropy is governed by the correlation between the physical Hamiltonian $H$ and the modular Hamiltonian $K_A=-\logρ_A$ of the initial reduced state, $ S_A(t,0)=S_A(0)-it \langle K_A(H-\langle H\rangle)\rangle + \mathcal{O}(t^2)$. For Hermitian dynamics, the initial imaginary response is controlled by the symmetrized covariance of $H$ and $K_A$ with an overall minus sign, while the initial real response is governed by their commutator. Thus the imaginary part of real-time pseudo entropy is not merely a branch artifact: it is a time-oriented modular response generated by the correlation between microscopic time evolution and subsystem coarse graining. We clarify the relation of this result to the known first law of pseudo entropy, derive an all-order expression in a Schmidt-diagonal model, recover thermal pseudo entropy as a special case, illustrate the covariance/commutator decomposition in a two-qubit model, and confirm the covariance response in transverse-field Ising-chain quenches, including a finite-size study of a modular susceptibility near the Ising critical region. We discuss how this amplitude-level oriented response can be related to ordinary entropy production, and also give a concrete $\mathcal{PT}$-symmetric toy-model illustration of the non-Hermitian extension.

</details>

### [128] [A Supernova Constraint on F-theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14575)
*Sebastian Vander Ploeg Fallon,James Halverson,Liam McAllister,David J. E. Marsh*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究F-理论（F-theory）中量子色动力学轴子（QCD axion）的约束条件，发现当紧致化基底三维流形（toric threefold $B_3$）的Hodge数 $N=h^{1,1}(B_3)$ 足够大时，QCD轴子质量增大，与超新星1987A中微子暴观测数据冲突。至少95%的 $N \ge 8,791$ 模型被排除，这一限制独立于宇宙学假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在弦理论（string theory）的强耦合极限——F-理论框架下，研究QCD轴子的参数空间约束，旨在从高能理论角度检验轴子暗物质候选者的可行性。

Method: 通过将F-理论紧致化至四维，构造基于环面三维流形 $B_3$ 上椭圆纤维化（elliptic fibration）的QCD模型，并以Hodge数 $N=h^{1,1}(B_3)$ 表征模型族。仅考虑弱弯曲三维流形以忽略 $α'$ 修正。

Result: QCD轴子质量随 $N$ 增大而上升；当 $N \ge 8,791$ 时，至少95%的模型预测轴子质量 $m_{QCD}>15~meV$，与超新星1987A中微子暴观测相冲突，从而排除该参数区域中绝大多数已知F-理论拓扑。

Conclusion: F-理论中模空间（moduli space）的大片区域因QCD轴子质量过大而被观测排除，该约束不依赖于宇宙学模型，对弦论景观（string landscape）中轴子模型的构建具有筛选意义。

Abstract: We study constraints on the quantum chromodynamics (QCD) axion in F-theory, a strongly coupled limit of string theory. We build models of QCD from compactifications to four dimensions on elliptic fibrations over toric threefolds $B_3$, characterized by an integer $N=h^{1,1}(B_3)$. The QCD axion mass increases with $N$, and we find that models with sufficiently high $N$ are inconsistent with observations of the neutrino burst from supernova 1987A, disfavoring large regions of the moduli space. Specifically, at least $95\%$ of models with $N \ge 8,791$ -- a regime that arguably contains the vast majority of known F-theory topologies -- have a QCD axion mass $m_{QCD}>15~meV$ and are thus constrained. This limit is independent of cosmology. We only consider weakly-curved threefolds, where $α'$ corrections are plausibly negligible.

</details>


### [129] [On the gauge-invariant dynamical charges and densities of the 1-instanton solution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14641)
*C. A. da Silva,L. A. Ferreira*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用积分非阿贝尔高斯定律，计算了四维欧几里得空间中SU(2)杨-米尔斯瞬子解（instanton）的规范不变磁通与电通，进而定义了规范不变的荷密度，并讨论了重参数化不变性，揭示了瞬子内部结构的物理图像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在杨-米尔斯理论中，瞬子解的规范不变守恒荷及其密度尚未被充分分析。本文旨在通过积分非阿贝尔高斯定律（integral non-Abelian Gauss law），从广义环路空间（generalized loop spaces）的积分方程出发，系统构建并理解这些荷的物理意义。

Method: 采用广义环路空间技术，基于杨-米尔斯理论的积分方程构造规范不变的动力学守恒荷；利用积分非阿贝尔高斯定律，在以瞬子解原点为中心的球面上评估非阿贝尔磁通与电通的规范不变通量；通过无穷小球壳内的荷定义规范不变的荷密度（charge densities）。

Result: 在欧几里得时间 x^4=0 且半径 r=1（对应瞬子尺寸 λ）处，瞬子与反瞬子（anti-instanton）的磁通与电通非零且可观测；该结果刻画了瞬子的内部结构，并可能与杨-米尔斯 θ-真空（θ-vacuum）的性质相关。

Conclusion: 本文为瞬子解的规范不变荷与密度提供了明确的构造和物理解释，展示了规范不变的磁通与电通是可观测的，这一图像对理解杨-米尔斯 θ-真空的结构具有重要意义。

Abstract: We study the gauge invariant dynamically conserved charges, and their corresponding densities, for instanton solutions of Yang-Mills theories in four dimensional Euclidean space, for the gauge group SU(2). Those charges were constructed in [1,2] through the integral equations of Yang-Mills theory, using techniques on generalized loop spaces. We use the integral non-Abelian Gauss law to evaluate the gauge-invariant flux of the magnetic and electric non-abelian fields through spherical surfaces centered at origin of the instanton solution. From such a flux, we define gauge-invariant charge densities by considering the charge within an infinitesimal spherical shell of radius $r$. We discuss the issue of the reparameterization invariance of the charges and densities, and show that the magnetic and electric fluxes for the instanton and anti-instanton, at the Euclidean time $x^4 = 0$ and radius $r=1$, which here corresponds to the size $λ$ of those solutions, are non-zero and observable. Our results give an interesting picture of the internal structure of the instanton, and may be important for the properties of the Yang-Mills $θ$-vacuum.

</details>


### [130] [Primal Bootstrap for Pion Scattering at Large-N](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14676)
*Sebastiano Bocchia,Alessandro Vichi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在树级（tree-level）亚纯散射振幅（meromorphic scattering amplitudes）中引入一种适用于大N极限（large-N limit）下π介子散射描述的新基，该基由洛甫雷斯-夏皮罗型振幅（Lovelace-Shapiro-like amplitudes）的线性组合构成，通过构造满足解析性、交叉对称性和雷吉行为，并借助后验的幺正性约束（unitarity）通过优化问题求解，构建出满足全部约束的亚纯振幅族。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大N极限下π介子散射振幅描述缺乏一个同时满足解析性、交叉对称性、雷吉行为（Regge behavior）等基本要求且可系统化构建的基。论文旨在构造一个可线性组合的振幅基，使得这些基本要求由构造保证，同时允许后验施加幺正性（unitarity）约束，从而系统性地探索允许的参数空间。

Method: 方法包括：1）构造作为洛甫雷斯-夏皮罗型振幅（Lovelace-Shapiro-like amplitudes）线性组合的亚纯振幅基，各基元具有不同的雷吉斜率（Regge slope）和截距（intercept）；2）通过构造确保解析性（analyticity）、交叉对称性（crossing symmetry）和雷吉行为；3）后验施加幺正性，要求分波分解（partial-wave decomposition）的正定性，这被转化为一个优化问题（optimization problem）并数值求解，形成一种原始自举问题（primal bootstrap problem）。

Result: 求解该原始自举问题后，获得了满足所有前述约束的亚纯振幅。将若干可观测量与由对偶正定性条件（dual positivity conditions）得到的边界进行比较，发现该振幅族覆盖了全部允许的参数空间（full allowed parameter space）。

Conclusion: 所构造的亚纯振幅基能够在大N极限下完整描述π介子散射的允许参数空间。该方法经过适当修改可推广至更广泛的振幅族构造，具有潜在的应用前景。

Abstract: We introduce a basis for tree-level meromorphic scattering amplitudes suitable for describing pion scattering in the large-N limit. The basis is constructed as linear combinations of Lovelace-Shapiro-like amplitudes with varying Regge slopes and intercepts. The resulting amplitudes satisfy by construction the fundamental requirements of analyticity, crossing symmetry, and Regge behavior. We analyze their behavior in specific kinematical regimes, including the high-energy fixed-angle limit. We also show that finite linear combinations of our basis elements need not violate unitarity. Nonetheless, because unitarity is not imposed by construction, we enforce it a posteriori by requiring positivity of the partial-wave decomposition. This condition can be formulated as an optimization problem and solved numerically. The solutions to this primal bootstrap problem yield meromorphic amplitudes that satisfy all the aforementioned constraints. We compare several observables with the bounds obtained from the dual positivity conditions and show that our family of amplitudes spans the full allowed parameter space. With appropriate modifications, this method can be extended to construct amplitude families for broader applications.

</details>

### [131] [Stochastic Thermodynamics on Time-Evolving Curved Spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14186)
*Rihito Nagase,Shoki Sugimoto,Asuka Takatsu,Takahiro Sagawa*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文为具有时变度规的非相对论弯曲空间上的过阻尼朗之万系统（overdamped Langevin systems）构建了随机热力学（stochastic thermodynamics）框架。时变度规通过对动能做功（work）贡献于能量平衡，该能量在过阻尼区域瞬时以热（heat）的形式耗散。该框架满足热力学第二定律（second law of thermodynamics），并且在度规按后向里奇流（backward Ricci flow）演化的特殊情形下，熵平衡（entropy balance）结构类似于佩雷尔曼熵泛函（Perelman's entropy functional）。该工作为量化时变空间（如膜上扩散）中动力学的热力学成本提供了途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在具有时间演化几何的弯曲空间（如生物膜扩散）上建立一致的热力学描述是一项尚未解决的问题。已有框架未能正确处理时变度规（time-dependent metric）带来的能量-功-热关系，导致热力学不一致。

Method: 从非相对论性弯曲空间上的过阻尼朗之万方程出发，显式引入时变度规对动能的做功项，并将其在过阻尼极限下处理为瞬时热耗散（instantaneous dissipation as heat），从而重新定义能量平衡方程。

Result: 该框架确保了熵产生（entropy production）满足热力学第二定律；在度规按后向里奇流演化的特例中，熵平衡方程与佩雷尔曼熵泛函具有结构上的类比性。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个定量框架，用于评估随时间演化的弯曲空间上随机动力学过程（如膜表面扩散）所伴随的热力学成本（thermodynamic costs）。

Abstract: We construct stochastic thermodynamics of overdamped Langevin systems on nonrelaticvistic curved spaces with time-dependent metrics. The time dependence of the metric contributes to the energy balance by performing work on the kinetic energy, which is instantaneously dissipated as heat in the overdamped regime. This contribution makes our framework thermodynamically consistent so that entropy production satisfies the second law of thermodynamics. As a special case, when the metric evolves according to backward Ricci flow, the entropy balance exhibits a structure similar to Perelman's entropy functional. Our framework provides a way to quantify thermodynamic costs in dynamics on time-evolving spaces such as diffusion on membranes.

</details>


### [132] [Boltzmann-Like Occupation of Nonequilibrium Steady States on Dense Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14542)
*Jacob Calvert*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文证明，在大型稠密网络上，非平衡稳态（nonequilibrium steady states, NESS）尽管存在大量熵产生，却仍具有类似玻尔兹曼分布（Boltzmann-like）的占据行为；同时表明“低抖动”（low rattling）的活性物质启发式方法在渐近意义上是精确的。该解释可推广至更广泛的“等可达”（equiaccessible）稳态类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 统计物理中的一个核心问题是如何将玻尔兹曼分布（Boltzmann distribution）推广到非平衡稳态（nonequilibrium steady states, NESS）。现有理论在处理非平衡系统的稳态占据分布时面临挑战，尤其是当系统存在大量熵产生时。

Method: 采用大型稠密网络（large dense networks）上的理论分析方法，引入“等可达”（equiaccessible）稳态概念作为核心分析工具，类比平衡态在线性响应（linear response）中的作用。

Result: 在大型稠密网络上，NESS 尽管具有大量熵产生，仍表现出类似玻尔兹曼的占据行为；活性物质领域中的“低抖动”（low rattling）启发式方法被证明在渐近意义上是精确的。直观上，这些 NESS 会在系统离开较慢的状态上花费更多时间。

Conclusion: 非平衡稳态的占据分布具有类似平衡态的玻尔兹曼形式，其背后机制可归结为“状态停留时间更长则占据分数更高”的直观原理。这一发现通过“等可达”稳态类获得了统一的理论框架，有助于将平衡态统计力学方法扩展到非平衡领域。

Abstract: A central problem in statistical physics is to extend the Boltzmann distribution to nonequilibrium steady states (NESS). We prove that NESS on large dense networks have Boltzmann-like occupation despite extensive entropy production. We further show that the active-matter heuristic of "low rattling" is asymptotically exact. Intuitively, these NESS spend a greater fraction of their time in states they leave more slowly. This explanation extends to the broader class of "equiaccessible" steady states, which play a role in our analysis akin to that of equilibrium in linear response.

</details>


### [133] [Mean-field theory of myopic self-avoiding fractional Brownian motion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13972)
*Rashad Bakhshizada,Skirmantas Janušonis,Ralf Metzler,Thomas Vojta*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文发展了一种近视自回避分数布朗运动（myopic self-avoiding fractional Brownian motion）的平均场理论，基于Fokker-Planck方法推导了相互作用主导区域概率密度的闭式多项式解，并通过高效径向分箱算法与一至三维大规模模拟验证了解析结果，同时讨论了该过程在脊椎动物大脑中血清素能轴突自组织中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解近视自回避分数布朗运动（myopic self-avoiding FBM）在相互作用主导区间的动力学行为，建立解析理论框架，并提高计算效率以支持大规模模拟，最终应用于生物系统中轴突纤维的自组织问题。

Method: 采用Fokker-Planck方法（Fokker-Planck approach）发展相互作用主导区间的平均场理论（mean-field theory），推导概率密度的闭式多项式解（closed-form polynomial solutions）；同时开发基于径向分箱（radial binning）的高效算法以降低计算复杂度，并在1至3维空间中进行大规模计算机模拟（computer simulations）验证。

Result: 发现系统存在两个动力学区域：相互作用主导区域（$α<α_c=4/(d+2)$），其均方位移（mean-squared displacement）按$\langle r^2(t) \rangle \sim t^{4/(d+2)}$标度且与$α$无关；噪声主导区域（$α>α_c$），则恢复标准FBM标度$\langle r^2(t) \rangle \sim t^α$。解析理论预测与一至三维的模拟结果吻合。

Conclusion: 成功建立了相互作用主导区间的解析平均场理论，并验证了其在不同维度下的有效性。该过程为理解脊椎动物大脑中血清素能轴突纤维（serotonergic axons）密度的空间异质性提供了自然框架。

Abstract: Myopic self-avoiding fractional Brownian motion (FBM) is a stochastic process in which an ensemble of particles is driven by fractional Gaussian noise while being repelled by the gradient of the time-integrated ensemble density [J. House, R. Bakhshizada, S. Janušonis, R. Metzler, and T. Vojta, Phys. Rev. E 112, 034119 (2025)]. Depending on the anomalous diffusion exponent $α$ characterizing the noise, the process features two dynamical regimes: an interaction-dominated regime ($α< α_c=4/(d+2)$) where the mean-density interaction governs long-time dynamics, and a noise-dominated regime ($α> α_c$) where FBM correlations prevail. In the interaction-dominated regime, the mean-squared displacement grows as $\langle r^2(t) \rangle \sim t^{4/(d+2)}$ regardless of $α$, while for $α> α_c$ the standard FBM scaling $\langle r^2(t) \rangle \sim t^α$ is recovered. Here, we develop an analytical mean-field theory of myopic self-avoiding FBM, based on a Fokker-Planck approach to the interaction-dominated regime. This allows us to derive closed-form polynomial solutions for the probability density. To compare with computer simulations, we develop an efficient radial binning algorithm that significantly reduces the computational complexity, making large-scale three-dimensional simulations feasible. Extensive simulations in one, two, and three dimensions confirm the analytical predictions. We also discuss the application of the process to the self-organization of serotonergic axons (fibers) in vertebrate brains, where FBM paths with self-avoidance provide a natural framework for understanding spatial heterogeneities of fiber densities.

</details>


### [134] [Diffusion-driven autocatalytic dynamics on a sphere](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14133)
*Denis S. Grebenkov*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究独立粒子在球面外扩散并受催化复制的集体动力学，在三维及以上空间中揭示了次临界（灭绝）、临界（稳态）和超临界（增长）三种长时行为，并利用扩散传播子显式形式推导了种群规模（粒子数）的均值、方差、高阶矩及完整分布，给出了长时分布的显式形式及其幂律趋近行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解扩散过程中自发催化复制与逃逸事件之间的竞争机制，揭示此类非平衡系统中种群演化的相变行为及其长时统计特性。

Method: 利用球形域的旋转对称性和单粒子扩散传播子（diffusion propagator）的显式形式，解析推导种群规模的统计量（均值、方差、高阶矩、完整分布），并分析其长时渐近行为。

Result: 在三维及以上空间，系统存在次临界（灭绝）、临界（稳态）和超临界（增长）三种长时相；获得了种群规模均值、方差、高阶矩及完整分布的显式解析结果；长时分布呈幂律（power-law）趋近稳态极限。

Conclusion: 独立粒子在球面外的扩散-复制动力学呈现丰富的相图，且由扩散的瞬态性质主导；解析方法可完全刻画种群规模的长时统计行为，包括其非平凡幂律收敛特性。

Abstract: We study the collective dynamics of independent particles that diffuse outside a spherical surface, on which they are replicated with a prescribed catalytic rate. In spatial dimensions three and higher, the transient nature of diffusion creates the competition between autocatalytic and escape events, thus leading to a rich phase diagram between subcritical (extinction), critical (steady-state), and supercritical (growth) regimes at long times. The rotational symmetry of the domain and an explicit form of the single-particle diffusion propagator allow us to obtain the statistics of the population size (i.e., the number of particles). In this way, we analyze the mean population size, its variance and higher-order moments, as well as the full distribution. In particular, we obtain a fully explicit form of the distribution at long times and describe a slow, power-law approach to this steady-state limit.

</details>


### [135] [Thermodynamic Framework for $q$-Affinity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14285)
*Dani Rodríguez-Castellanos,Petr Jizba*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文基于广义熵（Rényi熵与Tsallis熵）发展了非平衡亲和势（affinities）的热力学框架，将De Donder的经典概念推广到具有长程相互作用或强关联的系统，并建立了与Jarzynski型涨落关系及广义第二定律的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典非平衡热力学中De Donder的亲和势（affinity）概念主要适用于短程相互作用和弱关联系统。本文旨在将其推广至长程相互作用（long-range interactions）和强关联（strong correlations）体系，为此引入基于广义熵（generalized entropies）的q-亲和势（$q$-affinity）。

Method: 针对Rényi熵，利用Baez的热力学诠释，通过两个温度下亥姆霍兹自由能（Helmholtz free energy）的有限差分表达熵，导出广义热力学势，其关于反应坐标的导数定义Rényi q-亲和势，并得到指数功平均表示，联系到Jarzynski型涨落关系。针对Tsallis熵，采用主方程（master-equation）方法处理马尔可夫跳变过程（Markov jump processes），导出q-变形熵平衡方程并得到Tsallis熵产生率的显式表达式。

Result: 导出了Rényi q-亲和势的显式表达式及其与指数功平均的联系；建立了Tsallis熵产生率的显式形式，证明其非负性，从而恢复了广义第二定律（generalized second-law structure）结构；识别出局域随机q-亲和势作为进入熵产生率的广义热力学力（generalized thermodynamic force）。

Conclusion: 本文构建的非平衡q-亲和势框架为处理长程相互作用和强关联系统的不可逆过程提供了统一的热力学形式，既推广了De Donder经典理论，又通过涨落关系与广义第二定律验证了其自洽性。

Abstract: We develop a thermodynamic framework for non-equilibrium affinities based on generalized entropies. In particular, we extend the classical concept of De Donder by introducing $q$-affinities associated with Rényi and Tsallis entropies. This in turn allows us to generalize thermodynamic driving forces to systems with long-range interactions and/or strong correlations. For Rényi entropy, we build on a thermodynamic interpretation due to Baez, where the entropy is expressed through finite differences of the Helmholtz free energy at two temperatures. This leads to a generalized thermodynamic potential whose derivative with respect to a reaction coordinate defines the Rényi $q$-affinity. The resulting expression admits a representation in terms of exponential work averages, establishing a connection to Jarzynski-type fluctuation relations. For Tsallis entropy, we consider Markov jump processes using a master-equation-based approach. We derive a $q$-deformed entropy balance law and obtain an explicit expression for the Tsallis entropy production rate, proving its non-negativity and thus recovering a generalized second-law structure. This allows to identify a local stochastic $q$-affinity with the generalized thermodynamic force entering the entropy production rate.

</details>


### [136] [Thermodynamic Bounds from Otto--Villani Functional Inequalities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14329)
*Andrea Auconi*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过自由能差量化保守随机系统（conservative stochastic systems）向稳态松弛过程中的耗散，重访Otto-Villani框架中的函数不等式，建立自由能动力学与最优传输（optimal transport）的联系，并利用Landau-Ginzburg势的数值松弛实验加以验证。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 重访Otto-Villani框架（[F. Otto and C. Villani, J. Funct. Anal. 173, 361 (2000)]）中的函数不等式（functional inequalities），建立自由能动力学（free energy dynamics）与最优传输（optimal transport）之间的连接关系；并通过Landau-Ginzburg势（Landau-Ginzburg potentials）的数值松弛实验进行示例验证。

Result: 松弛过程中的耗散可由自由能差（free energy difference）量化；自由能动力学与最优传输之间的函数不等式提供了一个几何视角，用以刻画势垒存在下的瞬时松弛速度。

Conclusion: 该几何视角为理解保守随机系统向稳态松弛的耗散行为提供了理论框架，数值实验支持其有效性。

Abstract: The dissipation in the relaxation of an ensemble of conservative stochastic systems towards the steady state is quantified by the free energy difference. Functional inequalities within the framework of [F. Otto and C. Villani, J. Funct. Anal. 173, 361 (2000)] are here revisited which connect the free energy dynamics and optimal transport, offering a geometric perspective on the instantaneous speed of relaxation in the presence of potential barriers. These are illustrated with numerical relaxation experiments on Landau-Ginzburg potentials.

### [137] [Generic nonlocal statistics of the stationary measure in conserved active systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14483)
*Filippo De Luca,Michael E. Cates,Cesare Nardini*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过在高斯模型极限附近对非线性进行微扰展开，在无序相深处构建了一类活性系统（active systems）的定态测度（stationary measure）。研究发现，非局域性（nonlocality）与动力学守恒律（dynamical conservation law）相关联，并且对于守恒型活性场论（conserved active field theories），普适性地排除了对定态测度进行朗道-金兹堡展开（Landau–Ginzburg expansion）的可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平衡系统（equilibrium systems）满足细致平衡（detailed balance），其定态测度服从玻尔兹曼分布（Boltzmann distribution），对于短程相互作用而言具有局域性。但活性系统（active systems）破坏细致平衡，即使动力学完全是局域的，其定态测度也可能呈现非局域性（nonlocality）。本文旨在探索此类非局域性的来源及其普遍结构。

Method: 在高斯模型（Gaussian-model）极限附近对非线性项进行微扰展开，在无序相（disordered phase）深处构建定态测度的微扰表达式。研究对象涵盖Active Model A、Active Model B+、Model AB、Nonreciprocal Cahn–Hilliard模型以及Toner–Tu模型等一类活性系统模型。

Result: 在该微扰区域内，非局域性与动力学守恒律（dynamical conservation law）之间存在关联。对于守恒型活性场论，无法对定态测度（而非动力学方程）进行朗道-金兹堡展开（Landau–Ginzburg expansion）。

Conclusion: 守恒型活性场论的定态测度不具备局域朗道-金兹堡形式的展开，这一结果具有普遍性，意味着构建其定态测度需要采用不同于动力学方程的处理方式。

Abstract: The stationary measure of equilibrium systems with detailed balance follows a Boltzmann distribution, so that for short-ranged interactions the measure is local, meaning that distant spatial domains are statistically independent. In contrast, active systems break detailed balance, and can have nonlocal stationary measure even for fully local dynamics. Here, by expanding in nonlinearity about a Gaussian-model limit, we construct the measure perturbatively deep in the disordered phase for a class of models that includes Active Model A, Active Model B+, Model AB, the Nonreciprocal Cahn--Hilliard model, and the Toner--Tu model. In this regime, nonlocality is linked to a dynamical conservation law. Our results generically preclude construction of a Landau--Ginzburg expansion of the stationary measure (as opposed to the dynamical equations) for conserved active field theories.

</details>


### [138] [Extending Covariant Fluctuation Theorems into Quantum Regime through Quasiprobability Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14519)
*Ji-Hui Pei,Tingzhang Shi,Jin-Fu Chen,H. T. Quan*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的准概率分布（quasiprobability distribution），用以定义相对论性量子热力学中的功四矢量（work 4-vector），从而将协变涨落定理（covariant fluctuation theorems）从经典领域扩展到量子领域。该分布结合了Wigner与Margenau-Hill两种准概率，并借助经典粒子驱动的标量场（scalar field）及广义迹公式（trace formula）验证了结果。该工作建立了协变方式下研究相对论量子热力学的准概率框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机热力学（stochastic thermodynamics）的协变表述要求将随机功（stochastic work）处理为四矢量（4-vector），但由于量子力学中的非对易性（non-commutativity），这一处理在量子系统中面临重大困难。为此，需要发展一种能够适用于相对论性量子系统的功四矢量准概率分布方法。

Method: 提出一种结合Wigner准概率（Wigner quasiprobability）与Margenau-Hill准概率（Margenau-Hill quasiprobability）的新型准概率分布，用于定义量子系统中的功四矢量。通过一个由经典粒子驱动的标量场（scalar field）结合广义版本的迹公式（trace formula）来展示和分析所得结果。

Result: 成功将协变涨落定理（covariant fluctuation theorems）从经典随机热力学扩展到了量子领域。基于准概率分布的功四矢量定义在相对论性量子系统中保持了协变性（covariance）。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一种以准概率（quasiprobability）为核心工具的协变框架，可用于研究相对论量子热力学（relativistic quantum thermodynamics），为未来探索相对论与量子效应共同作用下的热力学过程提供了方法论基础。

Abstract: The covariant formulation of stochastic thermodynamics requires treating the stochastic work as a 4-vector, posing significant challenges for quantum systems due to the non-commutativity. We introduce a new quasiprobability distribution for the work 4-vector, which combines the Wigner and Margenau-Hill quasiprobabilities. This extends the covariant fluctuation theorems from classical to quantum regime. We illustrate our findings with a scalar field driven by classical particles with a generalized version of trace formula. Our work establishes a quasiprobability approach to studying relativistic quantum thermodynamics in a covariant way.

</details>

Method: 采用唯象理论（phenomenological theory）进行解析分析，并通过不同温度热浴中布朗胶体的数值模拟进行验证。

Result: 线性理论是短程的，非线性项在重整化群意义上不相关，但这些非线性项在各向同性无序相中产生了长程的三点关联。

Conclusion: 非平衡混合物中“危险的不相关非线性项”为长程关联提供了新机制，支持长程关联在非平衡体系中是规则而非例外。

Abstract: We study correlation functions in generic non-equilibrium mixtures, including multi-temperature systems and non-reciprocal field theories. The corresponding linear theory is short-ranged, and nonlinearities are irrelevant in the renormalization-group sense. Nonetheless, we find that these nonlinearities generate long-ranged three-point correlations in the isotropic disordered phase. Our analytical predictions, which are based on a phenomenological theory, are confirmed by numerical simulations of Brownian colloids in contact with thermal baths at different temperatures. Dangerously irrelevant nonlinearities in non-equilibrium mixtures thus offer a new route to long-range correlations, supporting the hypothesis that such correlations are not the exception but the rule out of equilibrium.

### [140] [Observation of intertwined charge density wave order and superconductivity in Janus monolayer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13828)
*Subhajit Pramanick,Shubham Patel,Sudip Chakraborty,A. Taraphder*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）研究了1T ZrSeTe Janus单层的电荷密度波（CDW）与超导不稳定性，发现Te层被Se替代会削弱CDW不稳定性，同时高温无畸变相中存在声子介导的双能隙超导电性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 1T ZrTe2单层中发现了涌现的电荷密度波（CDW）序，一个重要问题是：当一个Te硫族层被Se取代后，这种不稳定性是否仍然存在？本研究旨在回答这一问题。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），分析1T ZrSeTe Janus单层的声子谱、电子结构及电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon interaction），并考察电子关联（electronic correlation）和双轴应变（biaxial strain）的调控效应，同时考虑自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling, SOC）对超导转变温度的影响。

Result: 声子谱在不可约布里渊区M点出现显著反常，源于增强的电子-声子相互作用及带间和带内散射引起的电子不稳定性。晶格畸变打开了一个小的间接带隙，驱动体系从半金属转变为半导体。畸变对应的能量增益远小于ZrTe2单层，表明Se替代Te削弱了CDW不稳定性。高温无畸变相中，ZrSeTe表现出声子介导的双能隙超导电性，主要源于M点软声子模式与Zr d轨道和Te p轨道电子带的强耦合。SOC进一步修饰电子态并降低超导转变温度。

Conclusion: Te层被Se部分替代会显著削弱1T ZrSeTe Janus单层中的CDW不稳定性；电子关联和双轴应变可作为有效调控参数；该材料在高温相中仍可维持双能隙超导电性，但自旋-轨道耦合会抑制超导转变温度。

Abstract: Low-dimensional transition-metal dichalcogenides (TMDCs) provide an ideal platform for studying the emergence of charge density wave (CDW) and superconductivity. The discovery of emergent CDW order in 1T $\mathrm{ZrTe_2}$ monolayer raises an important question: does this instability persist when one $\mathrm{Te}$ chalcogen layer is substituted by $\mathrm{Se}$? In the present work, we investigate the CDW (2$\times$2$\times$1) and superconducting instability in 1T $\mathrm{ZrSeTe}$ Janus monolayer using first-principles calculations. The phonon spectrum exhibits a pronounced anomaly at the $\mathrm{M}$ point of the irreducible Brillouin zone, arising from enhanced electron-phonon interaction together with electronic instabilities originating from both interband and intraband scattering. The resulting lattice distortion reconstructs the electronic structure, opening a small indirect band gap, driving the system from a semi-metallic to a semiconducting state. The energy gain associated with the distortion is significantly smaller than that of $\mathrm{ZrTe_2}$ monolayer, indicating that the replacement of one $\mathrm{Te}$ chalcogen layer with $\mathrm{Se}$ weakens the CDW instability. We have further investigated the effects of electronic correlation and biaxial strain, both acts as effective tuning parameters for the instabilities concerened. In the high temperature undistorted phase, $\mathrm{ZrSeTe}$ exhibits phonon mediated two-gap superconductivity. It originates primarily from the robust coupling between the soft phonon mode at $\mathrm{M}$ point and the electronic bands predominantly derived from $\mathrm{Zr}$ $\mathit{d}$ and $\mathrm{Te}$ $\mathit{p}$ orbitals crossing the Fermi level. Spin-orbit coupling (SOC) further modifies the electronic states and reduces the superconducting transition temperature.

Abstract: We study a variety of nano-scale superconducting devices containing more than one weak link. Abstract: Wafer-level 3D integration of superconducting interconnects requires low-thermal budget bonding processes compatible with superconducting materials. In this study, we develop an oxidation-resistant bonding process using an ultrathin Au passivation layer to suppress oxide formation during bonding. ### [143] [Tailoring the properties of YBa$_{2}$Cu$_{3}$O$_{7-δ}$ thin films by 30 keV He$^+$ irradiation: An enabling route to superconducting device nanopatterning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14588)
*Bernd Aichner,Simon Koch,Philipp A. Korner,Max Karrer,Katja Wurster,Christoph Schmid,Ulrich Kentsch,Reinhold Kleiner,Edward Goldobin,Dieter Koelle,Wolfgang Lang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究系统表征了30 keV聚焦氦离子束（He-FIB）辐照对YBa₂Cu₃O₇（YBCO）薄膜电输运和超导特性的影响，确定了重离子辐照导致的晶体无序化、超导电性抑制与载流子散射增强的物理机制，并建立了适用于YBCO量子电路纳米图案化的可用注量窗口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 30 keV氦离子束是高温超导（high-Tc）铜氧化物器件纳米图案化和缺陷工程的关键工具，但其可用剂量窗口受到可靠超导抑制与最小结构损伤之间的竞争性约束，现有研究缺乏对该窗口边界条件的定量描述。

Method: 作者对高质量外延YBCO薄膜进行大面积30 keV He⁺离子辐照，利用X射线衍射（XRD）表征晶体结构变化，拉曼光谱（Raman spectra）分析氧缺陷状态，并结合电阻率-温度测量、上临界场各向异性分析以及霍尔角（Hall-angle）分析等手段系统评估辐照对电输运和超导性质的影响。

Result: XRD显示辐照导致晶格有序度下降、面外晶格膨胀以及正交-四方相变，在最高注量1×10¹⁶ cm⁻²时出现显著非晶化。拉曼光谱表明辐照主要产生氧相关的弗仑克尔缺陷（Frenkel defects）而非改变载流子浓度。超导临界温度Tc的抑制符合Abrikosov-Gor'kov对破缺模型，在4.5×10¹⁵ cm⁻²时达到完全淬灭。上临界场各向异性随注量增加而减小，与氧缺失YBCO行为相反。霍尔角分析证实载流子密度基本不变，但缺陷散射系统增强、迁移率降低，体系在高注量区间趋于脏极限（dirty limit）。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了He-FIB辐照YBCO薄膜的定量注量阈值和实际工艺操作窗口，为YBCO量子电路的纳米图案化提供了关键的物理参数依据。

Abstract: Focused helium ion beam (He-FIB) irradiation with 30 keV ions is a key tool for nanoscale patterning and defect engineering in high transition temperature (Tc) cuprate superconducting devices, yet its usable fluence window is constrained by the competing requirements of reliable superconductivity suppression and minimal structural degradation. In this work, we provide a comprehensive dataset on the effects of large-area 30 keV He+ ion exposure on the electric transport and superconducting properties of epitaxial YBa2Cu3O7 (YBCO) thin films. X-ray diffraction shows a fluence-driven loss of crystalline order accompanied by an out-of-plane lattice expansion and an orthorhombic-to-tetragonal transition, culminating at predominant amorphization at the highest fluence of 1 x 10^16 cm^-2. Raman spectra exhibit increasing disorder while lacking signatures of oxygen depletion, indicating that irradiation mainly generates oxygen-related Frenkel defects rather than changing the carrier concentration. Consistently, with increasing fluence, the normal-state resistivity ρ_N(T) at temperature T above Tc increases strongly, while d ρ_N/d T remains nearly unchanged at moderate fluence. The suppression of Tc is accurately described by Abrikosov-Gor'kov pair breaking and reaches complete quenching of superconductivity at 4.5 x 10^15 cm^-2. The anisotropic upper critical fields decrease approximately exponentially with increasing fluence, the vortex activation energy is reduced, and the anisotropy drops, in contrast to oxygen-depleted YBCO. Hall-angle analysis confirms a nearly constant carrier density but a systematic increase in defect scattering and reduced mobility, consistent with a crossover toward the dirty limit at high fluence. These results establish quantitative fluence thresholds and a practical operational window for He-FIB nanopatterning of YBCO quantum circuits.

### [144] [Wave turbulence theory of odd fluids and solids: kinetic equations and solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14583)
*Xander M. de Wit,Léo Touzo,Sébastien Galtier,Michel Fruchart,Federico Toschi,Vincenzo Vitelli*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文发展了奇数波动湍流（odd wave turbulence）理论，针对具有奇数黏滞性（odd viscosity）和奇数弹性（odd elasticity）的手性介质（chiral media），解析推导了动理学方程（kinetic equations），得到了各向异性的Kolmogorov-Zakharov（KZ）谱，并通过直接数值模拟验证了理论结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 波动湍流（wave turbulence）理论描述弱振幅随机波非线性相互作用的系统，但以往理论主要针对传统耗散系统。本文旨在拓展该理论至手性介质中由非互易应力（non-reciprocal stresses）产生的奇数波动湍流。

Method: 针对奇数黏滞性，构建了三维模型，涉及三波相互作用（three-wave interactions）；针对奇数弹性，构建了准一维过阻尼模型（quasi-one-dimensional overdamped model），涉及六波相互作用（six-wave interactions）。对两类模型均解析推导了描述能谱或波作用量（wave action）长期统计行为的动理学方程。

Result: 奇数黏滞性情况下，直接能量级联（direct energy cascade）产生各向异性的KZ谱。奇数弹性情况下，正向级联（forward cascade）对应的KZ谱非局域（nonlocal），非物理解；而波作用量逆级联（inverse cascade）对应的KZ谱仅边缘非局域（marginally non-local），在考虑对数修正后有效。直接数值模拟（direct numerical simulations）在两种情形下均观测到了相应的KZ谱。

Conclusion: 两种解析理论为数值模拟中观测到的KZ谱提供了严格的物理解释，建立了奇数波动湍流中前向级联与逆级联的理论基础。

Abstract: The theory of wave turbulence describes the properties of physical systems composed of a set of weak-amplitude random waves interacting nonlinearly. Here, we study odd wave turbulence, which arises in chiral media subjected to non-reciprocal stresses, notably odd viscosity and odd elasticity. In both cases, we consider simple models for which we can derive and solve analytically the kinetic equations describing the long-term statistical behavior of spectral quantities such as energy or wave action. For odd viscosity, we consider a three-dimensional model that exhibits wave turbulence involving three-wave interactions, which gives rise to a direct energy cascade characterized by an anisotropic Kolmogorov-Zakharov (KZ) spectrum. For odd elasticity, we consider a quasi-one-dimensional overdamped model that exhibits much slower dynamics involving six-wave interactions. In that case, the KZ spectrum corresponding to a forward cascade of a conserved quantity we call odd energy, is nonlocal and therefore does not constitute a physical solution. However, the other KZ solution, which describes an inverse cascade of wave action, is only marginally non-local and is therefore valid up to a logarithmic correction. These two analytical theories provide a rigorous interpretation of direct numerical simulations, where the KZ spectrum is observed both in the case of odd viscosity (forward cascade) and of odd elasticity (inverse cascade).

</details>


### [145] [Scalar dissipation anomaly and scalar-gradient scaling in turbulence: A joint velocity-scalar multifractal view](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14696)
*Dhawal Buaria*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文通过理论分析与高达8192³网格的DNS数据，研究了被动标量湍流中标量耗散异常（scalar dissipation anomaly）与标量梯度标度律的问题，揭示标量梯度对Schmidt数（Sc）和Reynolds数（Reλ）的不同依赖机制，并验证了多重分形（multifractal）框架的预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 被动标量湍流中标量耗散异常与标量梯度标度行为是湍流研究中的重要问题。以往的DNS分辨率有限或Sc与Reλ的取值范围较窄，难以系统检验理论预测；且标量梯度对Reλ和Sc的依赖机制尚不清晰。

Method: 基于纵向速度增量与标量增量的联合多重分形（joint multifractal）描述，并引入Yaglom定律和波动Batchelor截止尺度（fluctuating Batchelor cutoff scale）约束，建立理论框架；DNS数据在8192³网格、Reλ=140–1000、Sc=1–512范围内验证理论。

Result: 归一化平均标量耗散随Reλ和Sc增大趋于单一渐近值；在多重分形框架中，有效标量Hölder指数趋于零，对应锋面状标量前沿；联合速度-标量耗散结构的分形维数趋于7/3，支持非空间填充结构；标量梯度的高阶中心矩对Sc独立，该预测被DNS数据与标量梯度概率分布坍塌验证。

Conclusion: 标量梯度的Sc标度仅由标量耗散异常决定，而其对Reλ的依赖反映强间歇性，可与混合速度-标量结构函数指数直接关联。

Abstract: We revisit the problem of scalar dissipation anomaly and scaling of scalar gradients in passive scalar turbulence using theory and data from well-resolved direct numerical simulations (DNS) on grid sizes of up to $8192^3$, spanning Taylor-scale Reynolds numbers $Re_λ=140-1000$ and Schmidt numbers $Sc = 1-512$. The theory is based on a joint multifractal description of longitudinal velocity increments and scalar increments, constrained by Yaglom's law and extended to gradients via a fluctuating Batchelor cutoff scale. The DNS data show that the normalized mean scalar dissipation approaches a single asymptotic value as both $Re_λ$ and $Sc$ increase, although larger $Sc$ requires larger $\re$ to reach this state. In the multifractal framework, this corresponds to an effective scalar Hölder exponent tending to zero, associated with sharp cliff-like scalar fronts, and saturation of inertial-range scaling scalar structure-function exponents. The joint velocity-scalar fractal dimension of the dissipative structures is inferred to approach $7/3$, indicating a non-space-filling support. The framework further predicts that for fixed $Re_λ$, higher-order central moments of scalar gradients are independent of $Sc$. This prediction is confirmed by DNS data and by the collapse of standardized probability distributions of scalar-gradient across Schmidt numbers. These results suggest that the $Sc$-scaling of scalar gradients is dictated solely by scalar dissipation anomaly. In contrast, their $Re_λ$-dependence reflects strong intermittency, which can be directly related to mixed velocity-scalar structure function exponents.

</details>

### [146] [Altermagnetism and bond-nematicity in the spin-$1/2$ square lattice $J_1-J_2-δ$ model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14101)
*Tanja Đurić,Shenlong Yu,Pinaki Sengupta*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过结合对称性增强神经网络（symmetry enhanced neural network）和变分蒙特卡洛（variational Monte Carlo）方法，研究自旋-1/2方格子$J_1-J_2-\delta$模型中发现，在交换调制参数$\delta$较大且阻挫增强导致交错磁序（altermagnetic order）熔化时，会出现一种共存对称保护拓扑价键固体（symmetry protected topological valence bond solid）和键向列序（bond-nematic order）的新奇相，该相由磁振子对（magnon pairs）凝聚驱动，并伴随U(1)自旋旋转对称性与$\mathbb{Z}_2$自旋反演对称性的破缺。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前对交错磁体（altermagnets）的研究主要集中于交错磁矩对电子能带结构（electronic band structure）和超导等性质的非平凡影响，而强量子涨落以及交错磁序熔化可能导致的物相则远未被充分探索。因此，识别交错磁序邻近区域中涌现的奇异物相是重要的研究步骤。

Method: 采用新颖的机器学习方法，将对称性增强的神经网络架构与变分蒙特卡洛（variational Monte Carlo）相结合，研究自旋-1/2方格子$J_1-J_2-\delta$模型。该模型在小几何阻挫区域具有交错磁序（altermagnetic ordering），在强阻挫和小交换调制参数$\delta$区域存在无能隙自旋液体（gapless spin liquid）相。

Result: 在交换调制较大导致交错磁序区不同手性磁振子模式显著劈裂的参量下，增加阻挫使交错磁序熔化，从而产生共存对称保护拓扑价键固体和键向列序的相。该相的特征包括：磁振子对凝聚导致的键向列性（bond-nematicity）、U(1)自旋旋转对称性（U(1) spin rotation symmetry）和$\mathbb{Z}_2$自旋反演对称性（$\mathbb{Z}_2$ spin inversion symmetry）的破缺，以及激发谱中类似三子（triplon）能级的宇称劈裂。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了受强量子涨落驱动、从交错磁序熔化过程中涌现的奇异物相，为理解交错磁体邻近区域中可能出现的新型量子态迈出了重要一步。

Abstract: We study appearance of bond-nematicity in insulating altermagnetic materials induced by increased frustration and quantum-fluctuations driven melting of the altermagnetic order. Using novel machine learning approach that combines symmetry enhanced neural network architectures and variational Monte Carlo we consider the spin-$1/2$ square lattice $J_1-J_2-δ$ model known to have altermagnetic ordering in the regime of small geometric frustration and a gapless spin liquid phase in the regime of strong frustration and small exchange interaction modulation parameter $δ$. In the regime where exchange modulation is relatively large, resulting in the significant splitting of the magnon modes with different chiralities in the altermagnetic regime, we find that melting of the altermagnetic order by increased frustration leads to an intriguing phase that hosts coexisting symmetry protected topological valence bond solid and bond-nematic orders. The phase is characterized by condensation of magnon pairs that results in bond-nematicity, breaking of U(1) spin rotation and $\mathbb{Z}_2$ spin inversion symmetries and chiral splitting of the triplon-like energy levels in the excitation spectrum. Whilst numerous recent studies address non-trivial impact of altermagnetic moments on various properties in altermagnetic materials, like electronic band structure and superconductivity, influence of strong quantum fluctuations and phases that can result from melting of the altermagnetic order are much less explored. Our study therefore presents an important step in identifying exotic phases of matter that can emerge in vicinity of the altermagnetic order.

### [147] [Ferromagnetic Order of Reduced Magnetic Moments in a Frustrated Sawtooth Chain of the Magnetic Semiconductor ZnYb$_2$S$_4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14196)
*Shinji Okada,Hiroto Suzuki,Nonoka Higa,Yasuyuki Shimura,Takanori Taniguchi,Takahiro Onimaru*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究通过比热、磁化强度和粉末中子衍射测量，系统研究了正交半导体ZnYb₂S₄中Yb³⁺有效自旋-1/2锯齿轮链（sawtooth chain）的磁性质。实验发现其基态为铁磁序，但磁矩幅度因磁挫败（magnetic frustration）显著减小至0.1 μ_B/Yb，且比热尖峰处的磁熵仅释放27%的Rln2，表明基态双重态（ground state doublet）的部分熵在较高温度下已提前释放。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在锯齿轮链（sawtooth spin chain）中，竞争性的最近邻与次近邻相互作用会抑制长程有序，产生如自旋二聚体单重态（spin-dimer singlet）、1/2磁化平台（magnetization plateau）和自旋收缩（spin contraction）等新奇量子态。本研究旨在探究正交半导体ZnYb₂S₄的磁性质，其中Yb³⁺离子具有有效自旋-1/2（effective spin-1/2）并沿b轴形成锯齿轮链。

Method: 通过比热（specific heat）测量观测到1.4 K处的尖峰并分析磁熵释放；在0.28 K下进行等温磁化（isothermal magnetization）测量，观察磁滞回线和自发磁化强度；采用粉末中子衍射（powder neutron diffraction）检测反铁磁有序引起的超晶格反射（superlattice reflections）。

Result: 比热在T_m = 1.4 K处出现尖峰，此时磁熵S_m仅达Rln2的27%；0.28 K下的等温磁化曲线在|B| ≤ 0.2 T范围内表现出磁滞，在B > 0.2 T时单调增大；自发磁化强度仅为0.1 μ_B/Yb，比Yb³⁺基态双重态预期值小一个数量级；粉末中子衍射在T < T_m下未观测到反铁磁有序的超晶格反射。

Conclusion: 在基态下，Yb磁矩呈现铁磁排列（ferromagnetically aligned），但其磁矩幅度因锯齿轮链中的磁挫败（magnetic frustration）而显著降低。T_m处减小的磁熵表明Yb³⁺基态双重态的熵在T > T_m时已部分释放，与挫败磁系统的典型行为一致。

Abstract: In a sawtooth spin chain, competing nearest- and next-nearest-neighbor interactions suppress long-range order, yielding novel quantum states such as a spin-dimer singlet, 1/2 magnetization plateau, and spin contraction. Here, we investigate the magnetic properties of the orthorhombic semiconductor ZnYb$_2$S$_4$, in which Yb$^{3+}$ ions with an effective spin-1/2 form a sawtooth chain along the $b$-axis. The specific heat exhibits a sharp peak at ${T}_{\rm m}$ $=$ 1.4 K, at which the magnetic entropy $S_{\rm m}$ reaches only 27% of $R$ln2. This reduced $S_{\rm m}$ at $T_{\rm m}$ indicates the entropy release of the ground state doublet of Yb$^{3+}$ even for $T$ $>$ $T_{\rm m}$. The isothermal magnetization $M(B)$ at 0.28 K exhibits hysteresis for $\left|B\right| \leq 0.2$ T and increases monotonically for $B > 0.2$ T. The spontaneous magnetization is only 0.1 ${\it μ}_{\rm B}$$/$Yb, an order of magnitude smaller than that expected for the ground state doublet of Yb$^{3+}$. Moreover, in powder neutron diffraction measurements, no superlattice reflections due to antiferromagnetic order are observed for $T$ $<$ $T_{\rm m}$. Therefore, in the ground state, the Yb moments are ferromagnetically aligned, but their amplitude is reduced by magnetic frustration in the sawtooth Yb chain.

</details>


### [148] [Bond-operator analytical approach for the $t$-$J$ model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14374)
*A. V. Syromyatnikov*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种键算符理论（bond-operator theory, BOT），用于解析处理t-J模型及其含长程跳跃项的扩展。该理论基于预先提出的电子算符表示，通过局域自旋1/2和无自旋费米子算符（移动空穴子）来描述，二者之间无需约束条件。BOT在（扩展）原胞中引入自旋、空穴子和电子算符的表示，利用玻色子和费米子算符作用在整个原胞所有量子态的希尔伯特空间上。BOT通过常规图技术提供物理量在1/n幂次下的正则展开，其中n≥1是原胞可占据的最大准粒子（玻色子和费米子）数量。该表示在任意n>0下复现所有算符的对易代数，并能处理磁有序相和磁无序相。BOT中用单独玻色子或费米子描述的一些元激发，在常规方法中表现为传统准粒子的束缚态。特别地，双空穴束缚态（两个空穴的库珀对）在BOT中用独立的玻色子描述。论文详细讨论了方晶格上最多两个空穴（极化子）的t-J模型性质。尽管在物理上有意义的n=1情形下展开参数1/n并不小，但在计入少量简单图后，即使是在1/n的一阶，结果也与之前n=1的数值研究达到良好的定量一致。在1/n一阶的自洽计算使基态能量、交叠磁化强度以及磁振子、极化子和最低能量双空穴束缚态谱的数值结果与之前的数值研究达到非常好的定量一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: t-J模型及其扩展在强关联电子系统（strongly correlated electron systems）中具有核心地位，但现有的解析方法难以同时处理磁有序与磁无序相，且难以描述双空穴束缚态等复合激发。因此，需要发展一种系统的解析框架，能够正则展开并统一描述这些现象。

Method: 论文提出键算符理论（BOT），其核心是将电子算符表示为局域自旋1/2算符和无自旋费米子算符（移动空穴子）的组合，且二者之间不施加约束条件。在（扩展）原胞中，通过引入多种玻色子和费米子算符，构建作用于整个原胞所有量子态的希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）上的算符表示。BOT利用常规图技术（diagrammatic technique）提供物理量在1/n幂次下的正则展开，n为原胞可容纳的最大准粒子数。

Result: 在方晶格t-J模型中最多两个空穴（极化子）的情形下，尽管在n=1时展开参数1/n并不小，但计入少量简单图后，一阶1/n展开结果与之前的数值研究良好定量一致。进行一阶自洽计算后，基态能量（ground state energy）、交叠磁化强度（staggered magnetization）、磁振子（magnon）谱、极化子（polaron）谱以及最低能量双空穴束缚态（two-hole bound state）谱均与数值结果达到非常好的定量一致。

Conclusion: BOT提供了一种系统的解析框架，能够在1/n展开下正则处理t-J模型及其扩展，即使n=1时也能通过自洽计算获得与数值方法高度一致的定量结果。该理论同时覆盖磁有序与磁无序相，并能将常规方法中的束缚态（如库珀对）描述为独立的玻色子或费米子，展现了其在强关联电子系统研究中的广泛适用性。

Abstract: We present a bond-operator theory (BOT) for analytical consideration of the $t$-$J$ model and its extensions with longer-rage hopping terms. This technique is based on previously suggested representation of electron operators via localized spins 1/2 and spinless Fermi-operators of mobile holons which requires no constraint between them. We introduce a representation of operators of spins, holons, and electrons in (extended) unit cell containing several lattice sites via a zoo of Bose- and Fermi-operators acting in the Hilbert space of all quantum states of the whole unit cell. BOT provides a regular expansion of physical quantities in powers of $1/n$ using conventional diagrammatic technique, where $n\ge1$ is the maximum number of introduced quasiparticles (bosons and fermions) which can occupy a unit cell. The suggested representation reproduces commutation algebra of all operators at any $n>0$ and allows to consider both magnetically ordered and disordered phases. Some elementary excitations described in the BOT by separate bosons or fermions appear in common approaches as bound states of conventional quasiparticles. In particular, there are two-hole bound states (Cooper pairs of two holes) which are described within the BOT by separate bosons. We discuss in detail properties of the $t$-$J$ model on the square lattice with no more than two holes (polarons). Although the expansion parameter $1/n$ is not small in the physically meaningful case of $n=1$, we obtain a good quantitative agreement with previous numerical findings at $n=1$ even in the first order in $1/n$ after taking into account a few simple diagrams. Self-consistent calculations in the first order in $1/n$ bring our results to a very good quantitative agreement with previous numerical findings of the ground state energy, staggered magnetization, and spectra of magnons, polarons, and lowest-energy two-hole bound states.

</details>


### [149] [SmoQyElPhQMC.jl: An open-source Julia package for efficient and scalable quantum Monte Carlo simulations of electron-phonon coupled models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14425)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于SmoQyDQMC代码库构建，实现了文献[B. Cohen-Stead et al., Phys. Rev. E 105, 065302 (2022)]中算法的改进版本，在系统尺寸和逆温度（inverse temperature）两个维度上均实现了线性标度（linear-scaling）模拟，并扩展了灵活的脚本接口。

Result: 发布了SmoQyElPhQMC v1.0软件包，支持广泛类型的无关联电子-声子模型的线性标度模拟，可通过GitHub仓库或Julia包管理器获取，并配有在线文档和示例。

Abstract: We introduce version 1.0 of the SmoQyElPhQMC package, an open-source Julia code for performing scalable quantum Monte Carlo simulations of electron-phonon coupled model Hamiltonians. SmoQyElPhQMC is built upon the SmoQyDQMC codebase and implements improved versions of the algorithms presented in [B. Cohen-Stead \textit{et al}., Phys. Rev. E {\bf 105}, 065302 (2022)] to enable linear-scaling simulations of a broad class of uncorrelated $e$-ph models both in system size and inverse temperature. By extending the functionality of the flexible scripting interface introduced in SmoQyDQMC, the SmoQyElPhQMC package continues to allow users to adapt it to different workflows and interface with other software packages in the Julia ecosystem. The code for this package can be downloaded from our GitHub repository at https://github.com/SmoQySuite/SmoQyElPhQMC.jl or installed using the Julia package manager. The online documentation, including examples, can be obtained from our documentation page at https://smoqysuite.github.io/SmoQyElPhQMC.jl/stable/.

### [150] [Open Wilson chain numerical renormalization group approach to steady-state non-equilibrium quantum transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14635)
*Anand Manaparambil,Frithjof B. Anders*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将数值重整化群（NRG）扩展到非平衡态的方法，通过为每个Wilson位点添加一个储库（reservoir）并采用开链全密度矩阵（OC-FDM）方法，精确计算了量子点（QD）在有限偏压和温度梯度下的电荷与自旋输运性质，实现了低至 $T_K/D \approx 10^{-8}$ 的近藤能级（Kondo energy scale）探索，并与平衡态基准及实时量子蒙特卡洛（RT-QMC）结果高度吻合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数值重整化群（NRG）方法在平衡态下能够高精度地识别和量化量子杂质系统（QIS）的不同平衡态，但在非平衡态下稳态密度算符不再具有玻尔兹曼（Boltzmannian）形式，而是由边界条件决定，因此亟需将NRG扩展至非平衡体系。

Method: 通过在传统NRG的每个Wilson位点（Wilson site）上附加一个储库（reservoir），并利用连分式展开（continuous fraction expansion）精确恢复连续极限（continuum limit）以计算耦合函数；将非平衡参数（有限偏压和温度梯度）通过布洛赫-雷德菲尔德张量（Bloch-Redfield tensor, BRT）引入，其零本征向量即为稳态密度算符；最终采用开链全密度矩阵（OC-FDM）方法结合有效的单导引描述（effective single lead description）进行求解。

Result: 该方法成功研究了量子点（QD）在有限偏压和温度梯度下的电荷与自旋输运，分析了导引不对称性（lead asymmetry）和外磁场的影响；探索了低至 $T_K/D \approx 10^{-8}$ 的近藤能级（Kondo energy scale），且与全密度矩阵数值重整化群（FDM-NRG）及费米液体标度（Fermi-liquid scaling）在小平移和温度下定量一致；在局部性质（如电荷涨落）方面与实时量子蒙特卡洛（RT-QMC）数据高度吻合；且由于采用有效单导引描述，单次数值计算在普通笔记本上所需时间远低于其他先进数值方法。

Conclusion: 所提出的OC-FDM方法成功将NRG扩展至非平衡态，能够高效且精确地研究量子杂质系统的非平衡输运性质，在计算效率上相比现有方法具有显著优势，同时保持了与平衡态基准的一致性和对极低近藤能级的探测能力。

Abstract: The numerical renormalization group (NRG) approach was developed to identify and quantify different equilibrium regimes of quantum impurity systems (QISs) with unprecedented accuracy by a tailored finite size representation. Out of equilibrium, the steady-state density operator is not of the Boltzmannian form but one that is determined by the imposed boundary conditions. We extend the NRG to the nonequilibrium setting by augmenting each Wilson site with a reservoir, whose coupling functions are calculated via a continuous fraction expansion in order to recover the continuum limit exactly. The nonequilibrium parameters such as a finite bias as well as a finite temperature gradient enters through the Bloch-Redfield tensor (BRT), whose zero eigenvector gives the steady-state density operator. We used the resulting open chain full density matrix (OC-FDM) approach with an effective single lead description to investigate the charge and spin transport through a quantum dot (QD) under finite bias and temperature gradient. The influence of lead asymmetry and an external magnetic field on the transport properties are also studied. For completeness, we have also investigated local properties of the QD, such as charge fluctuations and find excellent agreement with real-time quantum Monte Carlo (RT-QMC) data. The OC-FDM approach was able to explore Kondo energy scales as low as $T_K/D \approx 10^{-8}$ in the non-equilibrium regime, as well as show convergence with the established equilibrium benchmarks, such as a quantitative agreement with full density matrix numerical renormalization group (FDM-NRG) and Fermi-liquid scaling at small bias and temperature. Owing to the effective single lead description, a single OC-FDM data point takes orders of magnitude less time on a standard laptop, compared to other state-of-the-art numerical methods.

</details>


<div id='q-bio.NC'></div>

# q-bio.NC [[Back]](#toc)

### [151] [Prospective Coding and Path Integration Emerge as Equilibrium Solutions of Self-Organizing Neural Networks with Firing-Rate Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14649)
*Facundo Emina,Emilio Kropff*

Main category: q-bio.NC

TL;DR: 本文提出一个理论框架，展示了连续吸引子神经网络（CANN）中的结构化连接及其计算特性（如预期编码和路径积分）如何通过赫布可塑性、发放率适应和全局抑制等生物机制自组织涌现，而无需人工预置连接。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的连续吸引子神经网络（CANN）依赖于预先布线（pre-wired）的递归连接来实现空间表征、路径积分和预期动力学，但其结构化连接通过学习涌现的生物机制尚未被充分探索。

Method: 通过理论分析与建模，研究平移不变输入如何驱动稳定的高斯型前馈权重涌现；引入赫布可塑性（Hebbian plasticity）、发放率适应（firing-rate adaptation）和全局抑制（global inhibition）等生物机制；在不同网络配置（前馈架构、引入递归交互、调制外部基线电流）下分析动力学行为。

Result: 平移不变输入自然驱动高斯型前馈权重涌现；预期动力学在前馈结构中自发产生，无需递归兴奋侧支；这种预测性偏移可在多层网络中线性放大；引入递归交互后网络可学习自维持移动活动簇的连接；通过调制编码速度的外部时变基线电流，系统可作为精确的单向路径积分器（path integrator）。

Conclusion: 预期编码（prospective coding）和路径积分并非人工设计的特征，而是单一自组织竞争网络中自然共涌现的特性。

Abstract: Continuous Attractor Neural Networks (CANNs) traditionally rely on pre-wired recurrent connectivity to model spatial representations, path integration, and anticipatory dynamics. However, the biological mechanisms through which this structured connectivity emerges via learning remain relatively unexplored. This work presents a theoretical framework revealing how continuous attractor connectivity and its computational properties self-organize through Hebbian plasticity, firing-rate adaptation, and global inhibition. We show that translationally invariant inputs naturally drive the emergence of stable, Gaussian-profiled feedforward weights. Crucially, anticipatory dynamics arise spontaneously within these feedforward architectures, shifting the activity bump forward without requiring recurrent excitatory collaterals. This predictive shift can be linearly amplified across multilayer networks, consistent with anticipatory activity observed in the superficial layers of the entorhinal cortex. Furthermore, introducing recurrent interactions allows the network to learn connections capable of self-sustaining a moving bump of activity. Finally, by modulating the network with an external, time-varying baseline current that encodes speed, the system adjusts its intrinsic velocity to function as a precise unidirectional path integrator. Ultimately, this study suggests that prospective coding and path integration are not manually engineered features, but rather naturally co-emergent properties of a single self-organizing competitive network.

</details>

### [152] [Quantum dynamical Weyl groups from quantum loop groups of arbitrary shuffle type](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14262)
*Tianqing Zhu*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 本文构造了任意混洗型量子环路群（quantum loop groups）的量子动力Weyl群元（quantum dynamical Weyl group elements），并据此定义了量子格点算子（quantum lattice operator）与代数量子差分方程（algebraic quantum difference equations），证明了这些差分算子构成交换族，且与qKZ算子对易，从而恢复了先前构造并被视为三角Casimir联络的差分类比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为任意混洗型（shuffle type）量子环路群构造量子动力Weyl群元，并建立相应的量子格点算子与代数量子差分方程，以推广和统一先前在特定构型下的构造。

Method: 通过构造任意混洗型量子环路群的量子动力Weyl群元，定义作用于范畴$\mathcal{O}$中半单模$V$的张量积上的量子格点算子与代数量子差分方程；随后证明这些差分算子的可交换性及其与qKZ算子的对易关系。

Result: 构造的代数量子差分算子构成一个交换算子族，并且与范畴$\mathcal{O}$中上述类型模的张量积上的qKZ算子对易；该构造恢复了文献[OS22]中的结果。

Conclusion: 该构造可视为当量子环路群对应于有限型可对称化Cartan矩阵时，三角Casimir联络（trigonometric Casimir connection）的差分类比（difference analog）。

Abstract: We construct quantum dynamical Weyl group elements associated with quantum loop groups of arbitrary shuffle type. Using the construction, we define the quantum lattice operator and the algebraic quantum difference equations for each tensor products of semisimple modules $V$ in category $\mathcal{O}$. We prove that algebraic quantum difference operators form a family of commuting operators, and they also commute with the qKZ operators for the tensor products of modules of the above type in $\mathcal{O}$. This recovers the construction in \cite{OS22} and can be viewed as the difference analog of the trigonmetric Casimir connection when the quantum loop group corresponds to the finite type symmetrisable Cartan matrix.

</details>

### [153] [Constraints on Stable Scalar-Tensor Dark Energy from DESI Data and Solar System Tests](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14014)
*Husam Adam,Mark P. Hertzberg,Daniel Jiménez-Aguilar*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了具有四次多项式非最小耦合（quartic polynomial nonminimal coupling）与线性标量势（linear scalar potential）的标量-张量（quintessence）暗能量模型，通过对比DESI暗能量状态方程约束、太阳系测试以及有效牛顿常数随时间变化的限制，发现满足所有约束的参数带非常狭窄。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有暗能量模型在早期宇宙中场稳定性方面存在不足，需要引入合适的非最小耦合（nonminimal coupling）结构来确保场在早期充分稳定，同时模型必须与最新的天文观测和局域引力实验约束兼容。

Method: 采用四次多项式非最小耦合与线性标量势的组合，对二次和四次非最小耦合系数以及势能斜率构成的参数空间进行系统性搜索，并将模型预测与DESI暗能量状态方程（dark energy equation of state）约束、太阳系测试及有效牛顿常数（effective Newton's constant）时间变化的上限进行对比。

Result: 在参数空间中识别出能够同时满足所有约束的参数带（parameter bands），并且这些参数带非常狭窄（very narrow）。

Conclusion: 具有四次多项式非最小耦合和线性势的标量-张量暗能量模型在理论上可行，但其参数空间受到DESI数据和局域引力实验的强烈限制，仅存在于极为狭窄的区域内。

Abstract: We investigate the viability of scalar-tensor (quintessence) models of dark energy with a quartic polynomial nonminimal coupling to gravity and a linear scalar potential. The polynomial nonminimal coupling is used to ensure that the field is well stabilized in the early universe. We perform a systematic exploration of the parameter space spanned by the quadratic and quartic nonminimal couplings, as well as the slope of the potential. We confront the predictions of the model with the latest Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument (DESI) constraints on the dark energy equation of state and also with complementary bounds from local tests of gravity, including solar system constraints and limits on the time variation of the effective Newton's constant. We identify bands in parameter space where all these constraints are satisfied, finding such bands to be very narrow.

</details>

# physics.soc-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [154] [Wealth Inequality and Planetary Boundaries in a Stylized Agent-Based Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14331)
*Thomas Valade,Michael Benzaquen,Matthieu Cristelli,Stanislao Gualdi,Pierre Lenders*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过构建基于主体（agent-based）的模型，研究财富不平等如何阻碍生态转型。研究发现，当不平等程度超过发达国家的常见阈值时，即使多数主体关注外部性，经济仍会锁定在“棕色”模式；不同财政政策的效果强烈依赖于不平等体制与财政机制的累退性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究较少关注财富不平等（wealth inequality）对生态转型（ecological transition）的反向因果作用，本文旨在揭示不平等本身可能成为阻碍绿色转型的结构性障碍。

Method: 构建了一个风格化的基于主体模型（agent-based model），其中初始财富服从帕累托分布（Pareto distribution）的异质性主体通过效用函数（utility function）在棕色部门（Brown sector）与绿色部门（Green sector）之间配置收入；效用函数捕捉短期回报与长期系统性风险之间的权衡，关键假设是富裕主体感知自身对环境冲击的脆弱性较低。

Result: 当不平等程度超过与多数发达国家相当的阈值时，即便相当比例的主体对外部性敏感，经济仍会锁定于棕色体制；基础收入、碳税、绿色激励及组合方案等财政政策的效果强烈依赖于不平等体制及政策嵌入的累退性（regressivity）。

Conclusion: 不平等是生态转型的内生障碍，财政政策的有效性取决于其所处的不平等背景，并在转型速度、累积环境破坏、增长与财政压力之间表现出多维权衡。

Abstract: At the intersection of rising wealth inequality and intensifying environmental pressures, we investigate a reverse causal relationship that has received comparatively little attention: wealth inequality may not only be a consequence of environmental crises, but also act as a structural obstacle to the ecological transition itself. We develop a stylized agent-based model in which heterogeneous agents, whose initial wealth follows a Pareto distribution, allocate their income between either a Brown or a Green sector through a utility function. The function is designed to capture the trade-off between short-term returns and exposure to long-term systemic risks. A central ingredient is that wealthier agents perceive themselves as less vulnerable to environmental shocks, thereby reducing the amount of resources available for the transition. We show that, beyond inequality thresholds compatible with those observed in most developed countries, the economy remains locked in a Brown regime, even when a substantial share of agents is sensitive to externalities. We then assess a set of stylized fiscal policies (basic income, carbon taxation, Green incentives, and a combined scheme) and find that their effectiveness depends strongly on the inequality regime and on the regressivity embedded in the fiscal mechanism, revealing multidimensional trade-offs between transition speed, cumulative environmental destruction, growth, and fiscal pressure.

</details>


### [155] [Detecting Historical Turning Points in Italian Media: A Complex Systems Approach to a Diachronic News Corpus](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14348)
*Dario Zarcone,Salvatore Miccichè,David Sanchez*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 本研究基于约60万篇意大利《共和国报》文章（1985–2000年），运用自然语言处理（NLP）与复杂系统、统计物理学方法，重建历时语料库并追踪媒体话语变迁，从而无需人工标注即可检测重大历史转型期。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模文本语料库的日益可得为数据驱动的定量历史分析开辟了新可能，但前数字时代具有历史相关性的历时语料库（diachronic corpora）仍然稀缺且不完整，因此需要一种能够从大规模文本数据中定量重建和探索历史变迁的方法。

Method: 构建了约60万篇意大利《共和国报》（La Repubblica）文章的历时语料库（1985年1月1日至2000年12月31日）；运用自然语言处理（NLP）技术在词汇（lexical）与语义（semantic）层面分析文本，再应用复杂系统（complex systems）与统计物理学（statistical physics）工具追踪媒体话语随时间的变迁。

Result: 该方法无需先验标签即可检测到关键转型期，包括意大利从第一共和国（First Republic）到第二共和国（Second Republic）的政治体制转型，以及海湾战争（Gulf War）、科索沃战争（Kosovo War）等重大国际冲突。

Conclusion: 计算语言学（computational linguistics）与复杂系统思想的结合能够为历史变迁提供新的定量洞见，为通过大规模文本数据研究媒体与社会的动态演变开辟了新路径。

Abstract: The increasing availability of large-scale textual corpora has opened new possibilities for data-driven, quantitative approaches to historical analysis using Natural Language Processing (NLP). However, diachronic corpora with historical relevance from the pre-digital era remain scarce and often incomplete. We present a quantitative approach to historical analysis based on the reconstruction and exploration of a diachronic corpus of around 600,000 articles from the Italian newspaper "La Repubblica", covering all the articles published from the 1st of January 1985 to the 31st of December 2000 - a period of major political, social, and geopolitical change in Italy and globally. Using NLP techniques, we analyze the text at both lexical and semantic levels; we then apply tools from complex systems and statistical physics to trace shifts in media discourse over time. This allows us to detect key transition periods, such as the transition from the First Republic to the Second Republic in Italy, or major international conflicts like the Gulf War or the Kosovo War, without relying on prior labeling. The results show how combining computational linguistics with ideas from complex systems can offer new quantitative insight into historical changes, opening up new paths for studying the dynamics of media and society through large-scale textual data.

</details>
